    <script>
        // Use the actual cloud URL, without hardcoding the port
        const API = window.location.origin;

        async function loadModule(moduleName) {
            const stage = document.getElementById('module-stage');
            stage.innerHTML = `<div class="p-20 text-center animate-pulse text-slate-400 font-bold">Loading ${moduleName}...</div>`;
            
            try {
                // Fetch the JS file from the /modules/ directory
                const script = document.createElement('script');
                script.src = `./modules/${moduleName}.js?v=${Date.now()}`;
                
                script.onload = () => {
                    if (window[`init_${moduleName}`]) {
                        window[`init_${moduleName}`](stage, API);
                    } else {
                        // If we hit this, it means FastAPI returned an error JSON instead of a real JS file
                        stage.innerHTML = `
                        <div class="p-10 text-red-500 font-bold border border-red-200 bg-red-50 rounded-2xl">
                            Module Error: Could not find <code>${moduleName}.js</code> in the /modules/ folder on the server.
                        </div>`;
                    }
                };

                script.onerror = () => {
                    stage.innerHTML = `<div class="p-10 text-red-500 font-bold border border-red-200 bg-red-50 rounded-2xl">Failed to load module file: /modules/${moduleName}.js</div>`;
                };

                document.body.appendChild(script);
            } catch (e) {
                stage.innerHTML = `<div class="p-10 text-red-500 font-bold">Fatal error loading module: ${e.message}</div>`;
            }
        }

        // Default view on load
        window.onload = () => { 
            // Boot into the Developer Console by default
            loadModule('admin_dev'); 
            lucide.createIcons(); 
        };
    </script>
</body>
</html>

<script>
let backendData = {};

function enforceSheetLimits(maxShort, maxLong) {
    let wEl = document.getElementById('w');
    let hEl = document.getElementById('h');
    let warnEl = document.getElementById('sheet-warn');
    if (!wEl || !hEl) return;
    
    let w = parseFloat(wEl.value) || 0;
    let h = parseFloat(hEl.value) || 0;
    let didClamp = false;

    if (w > maxLong) { w = maxLong; wEl.value = w; didClamp = true; }
    if (h > maxLong) { h = maxLong; hEl.value = h; didClamp = true; }
    if (w > maxShort && h > maxShort) {
        if (w > h) { h = maxShort; hEl.value = h; } else { w = maxShort; wEl.value = w; }
        didClamp = true;
    }

    if (warnEl) {
        if (didClamp) {
            warnEl.classList.remove('hidden');
            clearTimeout(warnEl.timeoutId);
            warnEl.timeoutId = setTimeout(() => warnEl.classList.add('hidden'), 3000);
        }
    }
}

function runCalc() {
    if(!backendData.Retail_Min_Order) return;
    enforceSheetLimits(48, 96); // PVC max sheet

    try {
        const inputs = {
            qty: parseFloat(document.getElementById('qty').value) || 1,
            w: parseFloat(document.getElementById('w').value) || 24,
            h: parseFloat(document.getElementById('h').value) || 18,
            thickness: document.getElementById('thickness').value, 
            sides: parseInt(document.getElementById('sides').value) || 1,
            laminate: document.getElementById('laminate').value,
            shape: document.getElementById('shape').value
        };

        const result = calculatePVC(inputs, backendData);
        if (!result || !result.retail) return;

        const ret = result.retail;
        const fmt = (n) => "$" + (n || 0).toFixed(2);
        const totalSqFt = ((inputs.w * inputs.h) / 144) * inputs.qty;

        document.getElementById('lbl-sqft').innerText = totalSqFt.toFixed(1);
        document.getElementById('ui-unit').innerText = fmt(ret.unitPrice);
        document.getElementById('ui-total').innerText = fmt(ret.grandTotal);
        document.getElementById('ui-print').innerText = fmt(ret.printTotal);

        if (ret.routerFee > 0) {
            document.getElementById('row-router').classList.remove('hidden');
            document.getElementById('ui-router').innerText = fmt(ret.routerFee);
        } else { 
            document.getElementById('row-router').classList.add('hidden'); 
        }

        const minOrder = parseFloat(backendData.Retail_Min_Order || 50);
        document.getElementById('ui-min-text').innerText = `Shop Minimum: $${minOrder}`;
        document.getElementById('min-badge').classList.toggle('hidden', !ret.isMinApplied);

        const sideTxt = inputs.sides === 2 ? "Double-Sided" : "Single-Sided";
        const cutTxt = inputs.shape === 'Rectangle' ? 'Square/Rectangle Cut' : 'Custom CNC Cut';
        const lamTxt = inputs.laminate === 'None' ? 'No Laminate' : `${inputs.laminate} Laminate`;
        
        document.getElementById('job-desc').value = `(x${inputs.qty}) ${inputs.w}" x ${inputs.h}" ${inputs.thickness} PVC Signs.\n${sideTxt}. ${lamTxt}. ${cutTxt}.`;

    } catch(e) {
        console.error(e);
    }
}

// API FETCH & NATIVE STATUS BAR UPDATER
window.addEventListener('load', async () => {
    if (typeof injectHeader === 'function') injectHeader("PVC Signs");
    
    const statusText = document.getElementById("status-text");
    const statusDot = document.getElementById("status-dot");

    try {
        const req = await fetch(`${SCRIPT_URL}?req=view_module&tab=PROD_PVC_Signs`);
        backendData = await req.json();
        
        if(backendData.error) throw new Error(backendData.error);
        
        if(statusText) {
            statusText.innerText = "ONLINE";
            statusText.className = "font-bold text-green-500";
            if(statusDot) {
                statusDot.className = "w-2 h-2 rounded-full bg-green-500";
                statusDot.classList.remove("animate-pulse");
            }
        }
        
        runCalc(); 
    } catch(e) {
        if(statusText) {
            statusText.innerText = "OFFLINE";
            statusText.className = "font-bold text-red-500";
        }
        console.error(e);
    }
});
</script>
</body>
</html>

        <span class="font-bold text-gray-200 uppercase" id="auth-user">---</span>

</div>

<div class="flex-1 flex flex-col md:flex-row overflow-hidden relative">
    <!-- CONTROLS -->
    <div class="w-full md:w-1/3 min-w-[320px] bg-white border-r border-gray-200 flex flex-col shadow-xl z-20 h-1/2 md:h-full order-2 md:order-1">
        <div class="p-4 border-b border-gray-100 flex justify-between items-center bg-gray-50">
            <div><h1 class="text-lg font-black text-gray-900 leading-none">Yard Signs</h1><p class="text-[10px] text-gray-500 font-bold mt-1">24" x 18" Coroplast</p></div>
            <div class="text-right"><div class="text-xs font-bold text-gray-400">TOTAL</div><div class="text-2xl font-black text-blue-600 leading-none" id="total-price">---</div></div>

                <div><label class="block text-[10px] font-bold text-gray-500 uppercase mb-1">Sides</label><select id="sides" class="w-full border border-gray-300 p-2 rounded font-bold text-gray-800 bg-white" onchange="calculate(); update3DState()"><option value="1">Single Sided</option><option value="2">Double Sided</option></select></div>
            </div>
            <div class="flex items-center p-3 border rounded bg-gray-50"><input type="checkbox" id="stakes" class="w-5 h-5 text-blue-600 rounded" checked onchange="calculate(); update3DState()"><label for="stakes" class="ml-2 text-xs font-bold text-gray-700">Include H-Stakes</label></div>

                    <button onclick="openEditor('A')" class="border border-blue-200 bg-blue-50 text-blue-700 font-bold py-3 rounded text-xs hover:bg-blue-100 transition flex items-center justify-center gap-1"><span>🎨 Edit Front</span></button>
                    <button onclick="openEditor('B')" id="btn-edit-b" class="border border-gray-200 bg-gray-50 text-gray-400 font-bold py-3 rounded text-xs hidden flex items-center justify-center gap-1"><span>🎨 Edit Back</span></button>
                </div>

            <div id="ar-status" class="hidden text-center p-2 bg-blue-50 text-blue-600 text-[10px] font-bold rounded animate-pulse">Preparing AR Experience...</div>

        <div class="absolute bottom-4 right-4 flex gap-2 z-20"><button onclick="fitCamera()" class="bg-white p-2 rounded shadow text-gray-600 hover:text-blue-600" title="Fit to View">⛶</button></div>
        <div class="absolute bottom-4 left-4 z-20"><button id="btn-ar" class="bg-gray-900 hover:bg-black text-white px-4 py-2 rounded-full shadow-lg text-xs font-bold flex items-center gap-2 transition transform hover:scale-105">View in AR</button></div>

        <div class="bg-gray-900 text-white px-4 py-3 flex justify-between items-center shrink-0"><h3 class="font-bold">Design Studio <span id="editor-side-label" class="text-blue-400 ml-2">SIDE A</span></h3><button onclick="closeEditor()" class="text-gray-400 hover:text-white">✕</button></div>
        <div class="flex-1 flex flex-col md:flex-row overflow-hidden">
            <div class="w-full md:w-64 bg-gray-50 border-r border-gray-200 p-4 overflow-y-auto flex md:flex-col gap-6 shrink-0">
                <div>
                    <h4 class="text-[10px] font-bold text-gray-400 uppercase tracking-wider mb-2">Source</h4>
                    <label class="block w-full bg-blue-600 hover:bg-blue-700 text-white font-bold py-2 px-3 rounded cursor-pointer text-center text-xs shadow"><input type="file" id="editor-upload" accept="image/*" class="hidden"> 📷 Upload Image</label>
                    <div class="mt-3 flex items-center gap-2"><label class="text-xs text-gray-600 font-bold">Background:</label><input type="color" id="editor-bg-color" value="#ffffff" class="w-8 h-8 rounded cursor-pointer border border-gray-300"></div>

                    <div class="space-y-2"><button class="w-full text-xs bg-white border border-gray-300 rounded py-2 hover:bg-blue-50 font-medium" onclick="setSizing('fit')">Fit (Contain)</button><button class="w-full text-xs bg-white border border-gray-300 rounded py-2 hover:bg-blue-50 font-medium" onclick="setSizing('fill')">Scale to Fill</button><button class="w-full text-xs bg-white border border-gray-300 rounded py-2 hover:bg-blue-50 font-medium" onclick="setSizing('stretch')">Stretch</button></div>
                </div>

                <canvas id="editor-canvas" class="shadow-2xl border-4 border-white max-w-[90%] max-h-[90%] cursor-move"></canvas>
            </div>
        </div>
        <div class="bg-white border-t border-gray-200 px-4 py-3 flex justify-end gap-3 shrink-0"><button onclick="closeEditor()" class="px-4 py-2 text-sm text-gray-600 hover:bg-gray-100 rounded font-bold">Cancel</button><button id="btn-editor-save" class="px-6 py-2 text-sm bg-blue-600 text-white font-bold rounded shadow hover:bg-blue-700">Save & Apply</button></div>
    </div>

<script type="module">
import * as THREE from 'three';
import { OrbitControls } from 'three/addons/controls/OrbitControls.js';
import { GLTFExporter } from 'three/addons/exporters/GLTFExporter.js';
import { USDZExporter } from 'three/addons/exporters/USDZExporter.js';

let backend = {};
const uName = sessionStorage.getItem('signos_user') || 'Guest';
document.getElementById('auth-user').innerText = uName;

// --- PRICING ---
window.calculate = function() {
    if(!backend.Item_Name) return;
    const qty = parseFloat(document.getElementById('qty').value)||1;
    const sides = parseInt(document.getElementById('sides').value);
    const hasStakes = document.getElementById('stakes').checked;
    
    let base = parseFloat(backend.Retail_Price_Sign_SS || 12);
    if(sides===2) base += parseFloat(backend.Retail_Price_Sign_DS || 3);
    
    // Tiers Logic
    let disc = 0;
    if(qty >= parseFloat(backend.Tier_4_Qty||250)) disc = parseFloat(backend.Tier_4_Disc||0.1);
    else if(qty >= parseFloat(backend.Tier_3_Qty||100)) disc = parseFloat(backend.Tier_3_Disc||0.08);
    else if(qty >= parseFloat(backend.Tier_2_Qty||50)) disc = parseFloat(backend.Tier_2_Disc||0.05);
    else if(qty >= parseFloat(backend.Tier_1_Qty||20)) disc = parseFloat(backend.Tier_1_Disc||0.02);

    let price = (base * (1-disc)) * qty;
    if(hasStakes) price += (qty * parseFloat(backend.Retail_Price_Stake || 2.50));
    price += parseFloat(backend.Retail_Fee_Setup || 15);
    
    const min = parseFloat(backend.Retail_Min_Order || 75);
    if(price < min) price = min;
    document.getElementById('total-price').innerText = "$" + price.toFixed(2);
};

// --- 3D ENGINE & EDITOR (Same logic as v3.4 but wrapped in module) ---
// Note: Keeping this section concise for the update, but it assumes the same Three.js logic as provided in source [3-33].
let scene, camera, renderer, controls, signGroup, matFront, matBack;
const defaultState = { img: null, imgLoaded: false, x:600, y:450, w:0, h:0, rot:0, flipX:1, flipY:1, bgColor: '#ffffff', canvasW:1200, canvasH:900 };
const savedStates = { A: { ...defaultState }, B: { ...defaultState } };
let activeSide = 'A';
let currentState = savedStates.A;

function initThree() {
    const container = document.getElementById('canvas-container');
    scene = new THREE.Scene(); scene.background = new THREE.Color(0xe5e7eb);
    camera = new THREE.PerspectiveCamera(45, container.clientWidth/container.clientHeight, 0.1, 100);
    camera.position.set(0, 15, 45);
    renderer = new THREE.WebGLRenderer({ antialias: true, alpha: true, preserveDrawingBuffer: true });
    renderer.setSize(container.clientWidth, container.clientHeight);
    renderer.shadowMap.enabled = true;
    renderer.outputColorSpace = THREE.SRGBColorSpace;
    container.appendChild(renderer.domElement);
    controls = new OrbitControls(camera, renderer.domElement);
    controls.enableDamping = true; controls.target.set(0, 17, 0);
    scene.add(new THREE.AmbientLight(0xffffff, 1.2));
    const dir = new THREE.DirectionalLight(0xffffff, 1.5); dir.position.set(10, 20, 20); dir.castShadow = true; scene.add(dir);
    buildSign(); animate(); fitCamera();
    window.addEventListener('resize', () => { camera.aspect = container.clientWidth/container.clientHeight; camera.updateProjectionMatrix(); renderer.setSize(container.clientWidth, container.clientHeight); });
}

function buildSign() {
    if(signGroup) scene.remove(signGroup);
    signGroup = new THREE.Group();
    const matWhite = new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({ color: 0xffffff, roughness: 0.3, metalness: 0 });
    matFront = new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({ color: 0xffffff, roughness: 0.3, metalness: 0 });
    matBack = new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({ color: 0xffffff, roughness: 0.3, metalness: 0 });
    const blankUrl = "data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVR42mP8/x8AAwMCAO+ip1sAAAAASUVORK5CYII=";
    new THREE.TextureLoader().load(blankUrl, (t) => { matFront.map=t; matBack.map=t; matFront.needsUpdate=true; matBack.needsUpdate=true; });
    const bBase = new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.BoxGeometry(24, 18, 0.14), matWhite); bBase.position.y=17; bBase.castShadow=true; signGroup.add(bBase);
    const fFace = new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.PlaneGeometry(24, 18), matFront); fFace.position.set(0, 17, 0.075); signGroup.add(fFace);
    const bFace = new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.PlaneGeometry(24, 18), matBack); bFace.rotation.y=Math.PI; bFace.position.set(0, 17, -0.075); signGroup.add(bFace);
    const wireMat = new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({ color: 0x888888, metalness: 0.6, roughness: 0.4 });
    const legL = new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.CylinderGeometry(0.08,0.08, 24), wireMat); legL.position.set(-5, 4, 0); legL.name="stake";
    const legR = new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.CylinderGeometry(0.08,0.08, 24), wireMat); legR.position.set(5, 4, 0); legR.name="stake";
    const bar1 = new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.CylinderGeometry(0.08,0.08, 10), wireMat); bar1.rotation.z=1.57; bar1.position.set(0,8,0); bar1.name="stake";
    const bar2 = new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.CylinderGeometry(0.08,0.08, 10), wireMat); bar2.rotation.z=1.57; bar2.position.set(0,0,0); bar2.name="stake";
    signGroup.add(legL, legR, bar1, bar2);
    const grass = new THREE.Mesh(new THREE.CircleGeometry(25, 32), new THREE.MeshStandardMaterial({ color: 0x4ade80 }));
    grass.rotation.x = -1.57; grass.position.y = -8; grass.receiveShadow = true; grass.name = "Grass_Plane";
    signGroup.add(grass);
    scene.add(signGroup);
}

window.fitCamera = function() { camera.position.set(0, 15, 45); controls.target.set(0, 17, 0); controls.update(); };
function animate() { requestAnimationFrame(animate); controls.update(); renderer.render(scene, camera); }
window.update3DState = function() {
    const sides = document.getElementById('sides').value;
    const hasStakes = document.getElementById('stakes').checked;
    signGroup.traverse(c => { if(c.name==='stake') c.visible = hasStakes; });
    const btnB = document.getElementById('btn-edit-b');
    if(sides === "2") btnB.classList.remove('hidden');
    else { btnB.classList.add('hidden'); matBack.map=null; matBack.needsUpdate=true; }
};

// Canvas & Editor Logic (Simplified)
const canvas = document.getElementById('editor-canvas'); const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
canvas.width = 1200; canvas.height = 900;
window.openEditor = function(side) {
    activeSide = side; currentState = savedStates[side];
    document.getElementById('editor-side-label').innerText = "SIDE " + side;
    document.getElementById('editor-bg-color').value = currentState.bgColor;
    drawEditor(); document.getElementById('editor-modal').classList.remove('hidden');
};
window.closeEditor = function() { document.getElementById('editor-modal').classList.add('hidden'); };
window.resetCanvas = function() { currentState.img=null; currentState.bgColor="#ffffff"; drawEditor(); };
function drawEditor() {
    ctx.fillStyle = currentState.bgColor; ctx.fillRect(0,0,1200,900);
    if(currentState.img) {
        ctx.save(); ctx.translate(currentState.x, currentState.y);
        ctx.rotate(currentState.rot * Math.PI/180); ctx.scale(currentState.flipX, currentState.flipY);
        ctx.drawImage(currentState.img, -currentState.w/2, -currentState.h/2, currentState.w, currentState.h);
        ctx.restore();
    }
}
// Listeners
document.getElementById('editor-upload').addEventListener('change', (e) => {
    if(e.target.files && e.target.files) {
        const r = new FileReader();
        r.onload = (evt) => {
            const img = new Image();
            img.onload = () => { currentState.img = img; currentState.x=600; currentState.y=450; currentState.h=900; currentState.w=900*(img.width/img.height); drawEditor(); };
            img.src = evt.target.result;
        };
        r.readAsDataURL(e.target.files);
    }
});
document.getElementById('editor-bg-color').addEventListener('input', (e) => { currentState.bgColor = e.target.value; drawEditor(); });
window.rotateImg = () => { currentState.rot = (currentState.rot+90)%360; drawEditor(); };
window.flipImg = (ax) => { if(ax==='h') currentState.flipX*=-1; else currentState.flipY*=-1; drawEditor(); };
window.setSizing = (mode) => { if(!currentState.img) return; currentState.x=600; currentState.y=450; if(mode==='fill'){currentState.w=1200; currentState.h=900;} else if(mode==='fit'){const r=currentState.img.width/currentState.img.height; if(r>1.33){currentState.w=1200; currentState.h=1200/r;}else{currentState.h=900; currentState.w=900*r;}} else{currentState.w=1200; currentState.h=900;} drawEditor(); };
window.alignImg = (p) => { if(!currentState.img)return; if(p==='center'){currentState.x=600;currentState.y=450;} drawEditor(); }; // Simplified alignment for brevity

// Interactions
let isDrag=false, lastX, lastY;
function getPos(e) { const r = canvas.getBoundingClientRect(); const cx = e.touches?e.touches.clientX:e.clientX; const cy = e.touches?e.touches.clientY:e.clientY; return {x:(cx-r.left)*(1200/r.width), y:(cy-r.top)*(900/r.height)}; }
canvas.addEventListener('mousedown', e=>{if(currentState.img){isDrag=true; const p=getPos(e); lastX=p.x; lastY=p.y;}});
window.addEventListener('mousemove', e=>{if(isDrag){const p=getPos(e); currentState.x+=(p.x-lastX); currentState.y+=(p.y-lastY); lastX=p.x; lastY=p.y; drawEditor();}});
window.addEventListener('mouseup', ()=>isDrag=false);

document.getElementById('btn-editor-save').addEventListener('click', () => {
    const dataUrl = canvas.toDataURL('image/png'); savedStates[activeSide].previewUrl = dataUrl;
    new THREE.TextureLoader().load(dataUrl, (t) => { t.colorSpace = THREE.SRGBColorSpace; if(activeSide==='A'){matFront.map=t; matFront.needsUpdate=true;}else{matBack.map=t; matBack.needsUpdate=true;} });
    closeEditor();
});

// Cart
window.addToCart = function() {
    renderer.render(scene, camera);
    const thumb3D = renderer.domElement.toDataURL('image/png');
    const item = {
        id: Date.now(),
        product: "Yard Sign",
        desc: document.getElementById('qty').value + "x Yard Signs. " + (document.getElementById('stakes').checked ? "w/ Stakes" : "Sign Only"),
        qty: document.getElementById('qty').value,
        price: document.getElementById('total-price').innerText,
        img3D: thumb3D,
        imgFront: savedStates.A.previewUrl || null,
        imgBack: savedStates.B.previewUrl || null
    };
    let cart = JSON.parse(sessionStorage.getItem('signos_cart')) || [];
    cart.push(item);
    sessionStorage.setItem('signos_cart', JSON.stringify(cart));
    window.location.href = 'Cart_Viewer.html'; // Direct to Cart
};

window.onload = async function() {
    initThree();
    const st = document.getElementById("status-text");
    try {
        // TELEMETRY & DATA
        const r = await fetch(`${SCRIPT_URL}?tab=PROD_Yard_Signs&ip=${clientIP}&user=${uName}&role=${sessionStorage.getItem('signos_role')}&req=view_module`);
        backend = await r.json();
        st.innerText = "ONLINE"; st.classList.replace("text-gray-500", "text-green-500");
        calculate();
    } catch(e) { st.innerText = "OFFLINE"; st.classList.replace("text-gray-500", "text-red-500"); }
};
</script>
</body>
</html>

<script>
    const user = sessionStorage.getItem('signos_user') || 'Guest';
    document.getElementById('date').innerText = new Date().toLocaleDateString();
    document.getElementById('cart-user').innerText = user;

    const cart = JSON.parse(sessionStorage.getItem('signos_cart')) || [];
    const tbody = document.getElementById('cart-body');
    let total = 0;

    if(cart.length === 0) {
        tbody.innerHTML = `<tr><td colspan="4" class="p-8 text-center text-gray-400 italic">Cart is empty.</td></tr>`;
    } else {
        cart.forEach((item, idx) => {
            total += parseFloat(item.price.replace('$','')) || 0;
            
            let visuals = `<div class="flex gap-2">`;
            if(item.img3D) visuals += `<div class="w-16 h-16 bg-gray-100 border rounded p-1"><img src="${item.img3D}" class="w-full h-full object-contain" title="3D View"></div>`;
            if(item.imgFront) visuals += `<div class="w-16 h-16 bg-white border rounded p-1"><img src="${item.imgFront}" class="w-full h-full object-contain" title="Front Art"></div>`;
            if(item.imgBack) visuals += `<div class="w-16 h-16 bg-white border rounded p-1"><img src="${item.imgBack}" class="w-full h-full object-contain" title="Back Art"></div>`;
            visuals += `</div>`;

            const row = document.createElement('tr');
            row.innerHTML = `
                <td class="p-4 align-top">${visuals}</td>
                <td class="p-4 align-top">
                    <div class="font-bold text-gray-900 text-lg">${item.product}</div>
                    <div class="text-sm text-gray-600 mt-1">${item.desc}</div>
                    <div class="inline-block bg-blue-100 text-blue-800 text-[10px] font-bold px-2 py-1 rounded mt-2">QTY: ${item.qty}</div>
                </td>
                <td class="p-4 text-right align-top font-bold text-gray-900 text-lg">${item.price}</td>
                <td class="p-4 text-center align-top no-print"><button onclick="removeItem(${idx})" class="text-red-400 hover:text-red-600 font-bold">×</button></td>
            `;
            tbody.appendChild(row);
        });
    }

    document.getElementById('cart-total').innerText = "$" + total.toFixed(2);

    function removeItem(i) {
        cart.splice(i, 1);
        sessionStorage.setItem('signos_cart', JSON.stringify(cart));
        location.reload();
    }

    function goBack() { window.location.href = 'menu.html?mode=sales'; }

    function printOrder() {
        // TELEMETRY: Log the Checkout
        fetch(`${SCRIPT_URL}?req=log_event&action=PRINT_ORDER&user=${user}&ip=${clientIP}&cart_size=${cart.length}&total=${total}`, {mode: 'no-cors'});
        window.print();
    }
</script>
</body>
</html>

    <script>
        const SCRIPT_URL = "https://script.google.com/a/macros/signstoremacon.com/s/AKfycbzEEf1lQ4xkXdSqcLgfLJ3FmNbLGUyElTzmac7U-t1msxLvJL8iSZ30R3bm5dCpmlKqPA/exec";
        const TAB_NAME = "PROD_Decals"; 
        let backend = {};

        // --- AUTH & VIEW LOGIC ---
        let currentUser = { name: "Guest", role: "VIEW", mode: "sales" };

        function initSession() {
            const params = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
            const urlMode = params.get('mode');
            const storeUser = sessionStorage.getItem('signos_user');
            const storeRole = sessionStorage.getItem('signos_role');

            if(storeUser) currentUser.name = storeUser;
            if(storeRole) currentUser.role = storeRole;
            
            if(urlMode) currentUser.mode = urlMode;
            else if(currentUser.role === 'ADMIN') currentUser.mode = 'admin';
            else if(currentUser.role === 'PROD') currentUser.mode = 'production';
            else currentUser.mode = 'sales';

            document.getElementById('auth-user').innerText = currentUser.name;
            document.getElementById('auth-role').innerText = currentUser.role;

            const body = document.body;
            body.classList.remove('mode-sales', 'mode-prod', 'mode-admin');
            
            if(currentUser.mode === 'sales') {
                body.classList.add('mode-sales');
                switchTab('retail'); 
            } else if (currentUser.mode === 'production') {
                body.classList.add('mode-prod');
                switchTab('cost');
            } else {
                body.classList.add('mode-admin');
            }
        }

        function logout() {
            sessionStorage.clear();
            window.location.href = 'index.html';
        }

        function goBack() {
            window.location.href = `menu.html?mode=${currentUser.mode}`;
        }

        window.onload = async function() {
            initSession();
            const statusText = document.getElementById("status-text");
            const statusDot = document.getElementById("status-dot");
            try {
                const response = await fetch(`${SCRIPT_URL}?tab=${TAB_NAME}`);
                const data = await response.json();
                if (data.error) throw new Error(data.error);
                backend = data;
                
                statusText.innerText = "ONLINE";
                statusText.classList.replace("text-gray-400", "text-green-500");
                statusDot.classList.replace("bg-red-500", "bg-green-500");
                statusDot.classList.remove("animate-pulse");
                
                if(backend.Item_Name) document.getElementById("product-label").innerText = backend.Item_Name;
                calculate();
            } catch (e) {
                statusText.innerText = "OFFLINE";
                statusText.classList.replace("text-gray-400", "text-red-500");
                document.getElementById("error-msg").innerText = e.message;
                document.getElementById("error-msg").classList.remove("hidden");
            }
        };

        function switchTab(id) {
            document.querySelectorAll('.tab-content').forEach(el => el.classList.remove('active'));
            document.querySelectorAll('.tab-btn').forEach(el => el.classList.remove('active'));
            document.getElementById('tab-'+id).classList.add('active');
            document.getElementById('btn-'+id).classList.add('active');
        }

        function toggleDiscounts() {
            document.getElementById('discount-table').classList.toggle('hidden');
        }

        function toggleOpt(id) {
            const el = document.getElementById(id);
            if(el.classList.contains('hidden')) el.classList.remove('hidden');
            else el.classList.add('hidden');
        }

        function calculate() {
            if (!backend.Item_Name) return;

            // Inputs
            const w = parseFloat(document.getElementById('width').value) || 0;
            const h = parseFloat(document.getElementById('height').value) || 0;
            const qty = parseFloat(document.getElementById('qty').value) || 1;
            const mat = document.getElementById('material').value; // Cal vs Cast
            const cutType = document.getElementById('cut-type').value;
            const hasLam = document.getElementById('has-lam').checked;
            const incDesign = document.getElementById('inc-design').checked;
            
            // Weeding Inputs
            const hasWeed = document.getElementById('has-weed').checked;
            const weedMode = document.querySelector('input[name="weed-mode"]:checked').value;

            const sqft = (w*h)/144;
            const totalSqFt = sqft * qty;
            const perimeterFt = ((w+h)*2/12) * qty;

            // --- 1. RETAIL ---
            const baseRate = mat === 'Cast' ? parseFloat(backend.Retail_Price_Cast_SqFt || 0) : parseFloat(backend.Retail_Price_Cal_SqFt || 0);
            
            // Dynamic Discounts
            let discPct = 0;
            let currentBestTier = 0;
            let i = 1;
            const tiers = []; 
            while(backend[`Tier_${i}_Qty`]) {
                const tQty = parseFloat(backend[`Tier_${i}_Qty`]);
                const tDisc = parseFloat(backend[`Tier_${i}_Disc`] || 0);
                tiers.push({ q: tQty, d: tDisc });
                if (qty >= tQty) currentBestTier = tDisc;
                i++;
            }
            discPct = currentBestTier;
            
            const unitRate = baseRate * (1 - discPct);
            let retailPrint = unitRate * totalSqFt;

            const minPrice = parseFloat(backend.Retail_Min_Order || 0);
            if (retailPrint < minPrice) retailPrint = minPrice;

            // Markup for Machine Cut (Kiss/Contour)
            let retailContour = 0;
            if (cutType === 'KissThru') {
                retailContour = retailPrint * parseFloat(backend.Retail_Cut_Contour_Add || 0);
            }

            // Markup for Complex Weeding only
            let retailWeed = 0;
            if (hasWeed && weedMode === 'Complex') {
                retailWeed = totalSqFt * parseFloat(backend.Retail_Weed_Complex || 0);
            }

            let feeDesign = incDesign ? parseFloat(backend.Retail_Fee_Design || 0) : 0;
            let feeSetup = parseFloat(backend.Retail_Fee_Setup || 0);

            const totalQuote = retailPrint + retailContour + retailWeed + feeDesign + feeSetup;
            
            // MINIMUM APPLIED BADGE
            const minBadge = document.getElementById('min-badge');
            if (totalQuote < minPrice) { // Re-check total vs min
                totalQuote = minPrice;
                minBadge.classList.remove('hidden');
            } else {
                minBadge.classList.add('hidden');
            }

            // --- DISCOUNT TABLE GENERATOR ---
            let rowsHtml = "";
            tiers.forEach(tier => {
                const trRate = baseRate * (1 - tier.d);
                const trPrint = trRate * (sqft * tier.q);
                // Scale variable costs
                const trContour = cutType === 'KissThru' ? (trPrint * parseFloat(backend.Retail_Cut_Contour_Add || 0)) : 0;
                const trWeed = (hasWeed && weedMode === 'Complex') ? (sqft * tier.q * parseFloat(backend.Retail_Weed_Complex || 0)) : 0;
                
                const trTotalRaw = trPrint + trContour + trWeed + feeSetup + feeDesign;
                const trFinal = Math.max(trTotalRaw, minPrice);
                const trUnit = trFinal / tier.q;
                
                const discDisplay = tier.d > 0 ? `<span class="text-[9px] bg-green-100 text-green-700 px-1 rounded ml-1">-${(tier.d*100).toFixed(0)}%</span>` : "";
                
                rowsHtml += `<tr>
                    <td class="pr-4 py-1 text-gray-500">${tier.q}${discDisplay}</td>
                    <td class="pr-4 py-1 text-blue-600 font-bold">$${trUnit.toFixed(2)}</td>
                    <td class="py-1 text-green-600 font-bold">${(tier.d*100).toFixed(0)}% Off</td>
                </tr>`;
            });
            document.getElementById('discount-rows').innerHTML = rowsHtml;

            // --- 2. IN-HOUSE COST ---
            const waste = parseFloat(backend.Waste_Factor || 1.20);
            
            // Materials
            const costVinylRaw = mat === 'Cast' ? parseFloat(backend.Cost_Vin_Cast || 0) : parseFloat(backend.Cost_Vin_Cal || 0);
            const costLamRaw = hasLam ? (mat === 'Cast' ? parseFloat(backend.Cost_Lam_Cast || 0) : parseFloat(backend.Cost_Lam_Cal || 0)) : 0;
            const costInkRaw = parseFloat(backend.Cost_Ink_Latex || 0);
            
            const costVinyl = totalSqFt * costVinylRaw * waste;
            const costLam = totalSqFt * costLamRaw * waste;
            const costInk = totalSqFt * costInkRaw;

            // Labor Rates (VLOOKUPs)
            const rateOp = parseFloat(backend.Rate_Labor_Op || 25);
            const rateShop = parseFloat(backend.Rate_Labor_Shop || 20);
            const ratePrint = parseFloat(backend.Rate_Machine_Print || 15);
            const rateCut = parseFloat(backend.Rate_Machine_Cut || 5);

            // Setup
            const setupMins = parseFloat(backend.Time_Setup_Job || 20);
            const setupCost = (setupMins/60) * rateOp;

            // Print
            const speedPrint = parseFloat(backend.Speed_Print_Roll || 150);
            const timePrint = totalSqFt / speedPrint;
            const costPrint = timePrint * (ratePrint + (rateOp * 0.1)); // 10% attendance

            // Laminate
            let timeLam = 0;
            let costLamRun = 0;
            if (hasLam) {
                const speedLam = parseFloat(backend.Speed_Lam_Roll || 300);
                timeLam = totalSqFt / speedLam;
                costLamRun = timeLam * rateShop; // Shop labor for laminator
            }

            // CUT LOGIC
            let timeCut = 0;
            let costCut = 0;
            let cutLabel = "Hand";
            if (cutType === 'Thru') {
                // Hand Cut Only
                cutLabel = "Hand Thru";
                const timeHand = (perimeterFt * parseFloat(backend.Time_Cut_Hand || 0.25)) / 60;
                timeCut = timeHand;
                costCut = timeHand * rateShop; // Hand cutting is shop labor
            } else {
                // Kiss Cut (Machine) + Thru Cut (Sheet)
                cutLabel = "Kiss+Thru";
                const speedKiss = parseFloat(backend.Speed_Cut_Graphtec || 50); // SqFt/Hr
                const timeKiss = totalSqFt / speedKiss;
                // Assume Sheet Cutting Time (Roughly equal to perimeter cut but faster)
                const timeSheetCut = (perimeterFt * parseFloat(backend.Time_Cut_Hand || 0.25) * 0.5) / 60;
                timeCut = timeKiss + timeSheetCut;
                costCut = (timeKiss * rateCut) + (timeSheetCut * rateShop); 
            }

            // WEEDING LOGIC
            let timeWeed = 0;
            let costWeed = 0;
            if (hasWeed) {
                const speedWeed = weedMode === 'Simple' ? parseFloat(backend.Time_Weed_Simple || 2.0) : parseFloat(backend.Time_Weed_Complex || 8.0);
                timeWeed = (totalSqFt * speedWeed) / 60;
                costWeed = timeWeed * rateShop; // Weeding is shop labor
            }

            const subtotal = costVinyl + costLam + costInk + setupCost + costPrint + costLamRun + costCut + costWeed + feeDesign;
            const riskCost = subtotal * (waste - 1);
            const totalInHouse = subtotal + riskCost;

            // --- 3. VENDED (Signs365) ---
            const vendRate = mat === 'Cast' ? parseFloat(backend.S365_Decal_Cast_SqFt || 0) : parseFloat(backend.S365_Decal_Cal_SqFt || 0);
            const vendMin = parseFloat(backend.S365_Decal_Min || 0);
            
            let vendPrint = totalSqFt * vendRate;
            if (vendPrint < vendMin) vendPrint = vendMin;

            // Add Markup ONLY for "KissThru" (Which S365 calls Contour)
            if (cutType === 'KissThru') {
                vendPrint = vendPrint * (1 + parseFloat(backend.S365_Add_Contour || 0));
            }

            // Shipping Logic
            let vendShip = parseFloat(backend.S365_Ship_Std || 10);
            const freightTrigger = parseFloat(backend.S365_Freight_Trigger || 1000);
            if (totalSqFt >= freightTrigger) {
                vendShip = parseFloat(backend.S365_Ship_Freight || 199);
            }

            const totalVended = vendPrint + vendShip;

            // Check if vendor data is missing
            if (vendRate === 0) document.getElementById('vend-data-warn').classList.remove('hidden');
            else document.getElementById('vend-data-warn').classList.add('hidden');

            // --- UI UPDATE ---
            const fmt = (n) => new Intl.NumberFormat('en-US', {style:'currency', currency:'USD'}).format(n);
            const fmtTime = (h) => { if(h<0.01) return "0m"; const hrs = Math.floor(h); const mins = Math.round((h-hrs)*60); return `${hrs}h ${mins}m`; };
            const pct = (n) => (n * 100).toFixed(1) + "%";

            // Retail
            document.getElementById('unit-price').innerText = fmt(totalQuote/qty);
            document.getElementById('lbl-sqft').innerText = totalSqFt.toFixed(1);
            document.getElementById('ret-print').innerText = fmt(retailPrint);
            
            if (retailContour > 0) {
                document.getElementById('row-ret-contour').classList.remove('hidden');
                document.getElementById('ret-contour').innerText = fmt(retailContour);
            } else document.getElementById('row-ret-contour').classList.add('hidden');

            if (retailWeed > 0) {
                document.getElementById('row-ret-weed').classList.remove('hidden');
                document.getElementById('ret-weed').innerText = fmt(retailWeed);
            } else document.getElementById('row-ret-weed').classList.add('hidden');

            document.getElementById('ret-setup').innerText = fmt(feeSetup);
            if (feeDesign > 0) {
                document.getElementById('row-ret-design').classList.remove('hidden');
                document.getElementById('ret-design').innerText = fmt(feeDesign);
            } else document.getElementById('row-ret-design').classList.add('hidden');

            document.getElementById('total-price').innerText = fmt(totalQuote);

            // Cost
            document.getElementById('cost-mat-vinyl').innerText = fmt(costVinyl);
            document.getElementById('cost-mat-lam').innerText = fmt(costLam);
            document.getElementById('cost-mat-ink').innerText = fmt(costInk);
            
            document.getElementById('time-setup').innerText = fmtTime(setupMins/60);
            document.getElementById('cost-setup').innerText = fmt(setupCost);
            
            document.getElementById('time-print').innerText = fmtTime(timePrint);
            document.getElementById('cost-print').innerText = fmt(costPrint);
            
            document.getElementById('time-lam').innerText = fmtTime(timeLam);
            document.getElementById('cost-lam').innerText = fmt(costLamRun);
            
            document.getElementById('lbl-cut-type').innerText = cutLabel;
            document.getElementById('time-cut').innerText = fmtTime(timeCut);
            document.getElementById('cost-cut').innerText = fmt(costCut);

            if (costWeed > 0) {
                document.getElementById('row-cost-weed').classList.remove('hidden');
                document.getElementById('time-weed').innerText = fmtTime(timeWeed);
                document.getElementById('cost-weed').innerText = fmt(costWeed);
            } else document.getElementById('row-cost-weed').classList.add('hidden');

            document.getElementById('cost-waste').innerText = fmt(riskCost);
            document.getElementById('cost-total').innerText = fmt(totalInHouse);

            const profIn = totalQuote - totalInHouse;
            document.getElementById('profit-inhouse').innerText = fmt(profIn);
            if(totalQuote>0) document.getElementById('margin-inhouse').innerText = pct(profIn/totalQuote);

            // Vend
            document.getElementById('vend-print').innerText = fmt(vendPrint);
            document.getElementById('vend-ship').innerText = fmt(vendShip);
            document.getElementById('vend-total').innerText = fmt(totalVended);

            const profVend = totalQuote - totalVended;
            document.getElementById('profit-vend').innerText = fmt(profVend);
            if(totalQuote>0) document.getElementById('margin-vend').innerText = pct(profVend/totalQuote);

            // Warnings
            const profitWarn = document.getElementById('profit-warn');
            if (profIn < 0 && profVend < 0) {
                profitWarn.classList.remove('hidden');
                profitWarn.classList.add('warn-pulse');
            } else {
                profitWarn.classList.add('hidden');
                profitWarn.classList.remove('warn-pulse');
            }
        }
    </script>
</body>
</html>

<script>
// SW Color DB logic brought from old file
const SW_COLORS = [
{code:"SW7005", name:"Pure White", hex:"#EDECE6"}, {code:"SW6258", name:"Tricorn Black", hex:"#2F2F30"},
{code:"SW7069", name:"Iron Ore", hex:"#434341"}, {code:"SW7048", name:"Urbane Bronze", hex:"#54504A"},
{code:"SW6244", name:"Naval", hex:"#2F3D4C"}, {code:"SW6883", name:"Raucous Orange", hex:"#D66032"},
{code:"SW6868", name:"Real Red", hex:"#C92E39"}, {code:"SW6902", name:"Decisive Yellow", hex:"#F3CF3C"},
{code:"SW6711", name:"Parakeet", hex:"#80BD4E"}, {code:"SW6501", name:"Manitou Blue", hex:"#4C6A89"}
];

let backendData = {};

window.onload = async function() {
    injectHeader("Acrylic Signs");
    initColors();

    const u = sessionStorage.getItem('signos_user') || 'Guest';
    const r = sessionStorage.getItem('signos_role') || 'VIEW';

    const statusText = document.getElementById("status-text");
    const statusDot = document.getElementById("status-dot");
    const verDisplay = document.getElementById("version-display");

    try {
        const res = await fetch(`${SCRIPT_URL}?tab=PROD_Acrylic_Signs&ip=${clientIP}&user=${u}&role=${r}&req=view_module`);
        const data = await res.json();

        if(data.error) throw new Error(data.error);
        backendData = data;

        if(statusText) {
            statusText.innerText = "ONLINE";
            statusText.className = "font-bold text-green-500";
            statusDot.className = "w-2 h-2 rounded-full bg-green-500";
            statusDot.classList.remove("animate-pulse");
        }

        if(verDisplay) {
            verDisplay.innerText = `(v4.0)`;
            verDisplay.classList.remove('hidden');
        }

        runCalc();

    } catch(e) {
        if(statusText) {
            statusText.innerText = "OFFLINE";
            statusText.className = "font-bold text-red-500";
        }
        console.error(e);
    }
};

function initColors() {
    const list = document.getElementById('sw-colors');
    SW_COLORS.forEach(c => {
        let opt = document.createElement('option');
        opt.value = c.code; opt.innerText = c.name; list.appendChild(opt);
    });
}

function updateSwatch(type) {
    if(type === 'paint') {
        const code = document.getElementById('paint-code').value.toUpperCase();
        const swatch = document.getElementById('paint-swatch');
        const nameLabel = document.getElementById('paint-name');
        const match = SW_COLORS.find(c => c.code === code);
        if (match) { swatch.value = match.hex; nameLabel.innerText = match.name; }
        else { nameLabel.innerText = "Custom/Unknown"; }
    }
}

function toggleBox(id) {
    document.getElementById(id).classList.toggle('hidden');
}

function toggleDiscounts() {
    const table = document.getElementById('disc-table');
    const arrow = document.getElementById('disc-arrow');
    table.classList.toggle('hidden');
    if (table.classList.contains('hidden')) {
        arrow.classList.add('rotate-90');
    } else {
        arrow.classList.remove('rotate-90');
    }
}

function runCalc() {
    if(!backendData.Item_Name) return;

    const inputs = {
        qty: parseFloat(document.getElementById('qty').value) || 1,
        w: parseFloat(document.getElementById('w').value) || 24,
        h: parseFloat(document.getElementById('h').value) || 18,
        thickness: document.getElementById('thickness').value,
        mode: document.getElementById('mode').value,
        hasPaint: document.getElementById('paint').checked,
        hasPMS: document.getElementById('pms').checked,
        hasStandoffs: document.getElementById('hw').checked,
        standoffQty: parseInt(document.getElementById('hw-qty').value),
        isContour: document.getElementById('contour').checked,
        incDesign: document.getElementById('design').checked
    };

    const ret = calculateRetail(inputs, backendData);

    const fmt = (n) => "$" + n.toFixed(2);
    const toggleRow = (id, val) => {
        if(val > 0) { document.getElementById(id).classList.remove('hidden'); }
        else { document.getElementById(id).classList.add('hidden'); }
    }

    document.getElementById('ui-unit').innerText = fmt(ret.unitPrice);
    document.getElementById('ui-total').innerText = fmt(ret.grandTotal);
    document.getElementById('ui-print').innerText = fmt(ret.printTotal);
    
    toggleRow('row-paint', ret.paintTotal);
    document.getElementById('ui-paint').innerText = fmt(ret.paintTotal);

    toggleRow('row-pms', ret.pmsTotal);
    document.getElementById('ui-pms').innerText = fmt(ret.pmsTotal);

    toggleRow('row-contour', ret.contourTotal);
    document.getElementById('ui-contour').innerText = fmt(ret.contourTotal);

    toggleRow('row-hw', ret.standoffTotal);
    document.getElementById('ui-hw').innerText = fmt(ret.standoffTotal);

    toggleRow('row-design', ret.feeDesign);
    document.getElementById('ui-design').innerText = fmt(ret.feeDesign);
    
    document.getElementById('ui-setup').innerText = fmt(ret.feeSetup);
    
    document.getElementById('ui-min-text').innerText = `Shop Minimum: $${ret.minOrderValue}`;
    document.getElementById('min-badge').classList.toggle('hidden', !ret.isMinApplied);

    let rowsHtml = "";
    ret.tiers.forEach(tier => {
        const pctDisplay = tier.pct > 0 ? `<span class="text-[9px] bg-green-100 text-green-700 px-1 rounded ml-1">-${(tier.pct*100).toFixed(0)}%</span>` : "";
        rowsHtml += `<tr><td class="pr-4 py-1 text-gray-500">${tier.q}+ ${pctDisplay}</td><td class="pr-4 py-1 text-gray-400">$${(ret.printTotal/inputs.qty).toFixed(2)}</td><td class="py-1 text-blue-600 font-bold">$${tier.unit.toFixed(2)}</td></tr>`;
    });
    document.getElementById('tier-rows').innerHTML = rowsHtml;

    // Generate Text
    const finishTxt = [];
    if(inputs.mode === '2nd_Std') finishTxt.push("2nd Surface Print (Color+White)");
    else if(inputs.mode === '2nd_Block') finishTxt.push("2nd Surface Blockout (Day/Night)");
    else finishTxt.push("1st Surface Direct Print");

    if(inputs.hasPaint) finishTxt.push(`Painted Background (${document.getElementById('paint-code').value || 'Custom'})`);
    if(inputs.hasPMS) finishTxt.push(`PMS Match (${document.getElementById('pms-code').value || 'TBD'})`);
    if(inputs.isContour) finishTxt.push("Contour Cut Shape");
    if(inputs.hasStandoffs) finishTxt.push(`${document.getElementById('hw-qty').value} ${document.getElementById('hw-col').value} Standoffs`);

    const desc = `(x${inputs.qty}) ${inputs.w}" x ${inputs.h}" ${inputs.thickness === '187' ? '3/16"' : '1/8"'} Acrylic Sign.\n${finishTxt.join(". ")}.`;
    document.getElementById('job-desc').value = desc;
}
</script>
</body>
</html>


========================================
FILE: Calculator_Nameplate_SVGTest.html
========================================
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">

                <div><label class="block text-[10px] font-bold text-gray-500 uppercase mb-1">Width (in)</label><input type="number" id="w" value="10" min="0.5" step="0.5" class="w-full border p-2 rounded font-bold text-gray-800 text-lg text-center bg-white shadow-inner focus:border-blue-500 outline-none" oninput="runCalc()"></div>
                <div><label class="block text-[10px] font-bold text-gray-500 uppercase mb-1">Height (in)</label><input type="number" id="h" value="2" min="0.5" step="0.5" class="w-full border p-2 rounded font-bold text-gray-800 text-lg text-center bg-white shadow-inner focus:border-blue-500 outline-none" oninput="runCalc()"></div>

                        </div>

                </div>
            </div>
            
            <div id="text-layout-content" class="px-3 pb-3">

                <!-- Replaced nested tags with SVG injection target -->
                <div id="preview-canvas" class="shadow-2xl rounded-sm flex flex-col items-center justify-center overflow-hidden border border-black/20 relative" style="background-color: #000;">
                    <span class="absolute inset-0 flex flex-col items-center justify-center text-gray-500 text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest text-center pointer-events-none">Awaiting Text</span>
                </div>
            </div>
            <div id="overflow-warn-box" class="hidden w-full mt-3 bg-orange-100 border border-orange-300 p-1.5 rounded shadow-sm text-center">
                <span class="text-[9px] text-orange-900 font-bold uppercase tracking-widest">⚠️ Layout Overflow / Text Too Large</span>
            </div>
            <div id="bright-warn-box" class="hidden w-full mt-3 bg-amber-100 border border-amber-300 p-1.5 rounded shadow-sm text-center">
                <span class="text-[9px] text-amber-900 font-bold uppercase tracking-widest">⚠️ Bright Face Selected - Verify Contrast</span>

        <!-- 4. ENGRAVE STYLE & MATERIALS -->

            </div>

            <button id="btn-tab-paint" onclick="setReverseTab('paint')" class="flex-1 py-1.5 text-[10px] font-black rounded text-gray-500 hover:text-gray-800 transition border border-transparent uppercase tracking-widest">Step 2: Paint Color</button>
        </div>

        <div id="mat-container" class="space-y-2">
            <div id="selected-color-label" class="text-[10px] font-bold text-blue-600 bg-blue-50 px-2 py-1 rounded border border-blue-100 truncate">Loading...</div>
            <div id="rowmark-grid" class="flex flex-wrap gap-2 max-h-32 overflow-y-auto pr-2 color-scroll p-3 border rounded-lg bg-gray-50 shadow-inner"></div>
        </div>

        <div id="paint-container" class="hidden space-y-2 relative z-20">
            <div class="flex bg-orange-100 p-1 rounded-lg">
                <button id="btn-pms" onclick="setPaintSystem('PMS')" class="flex-1 py-1.5 text-[10px] font-black rounded bg-white shadow-sm text-orange-700 transition uppercase tracking-widest border border-orange-200">PMS Match</button>
                <button id="btn-sw" onclick="setPaintSystem('SW')" class="flex-1 py-1.5 text-[10px] font-black rounded text-orange-600 hover:text-orange-800 transition border border-transparent uppercase tracking-widest">Sherwin Williams</button>
            </div>
            <input type="text" id="paint-search" placeholder="Search colors..." oninput="SignOS_UI.filterGrid('paint-grid', 'paint-search')" class="w-full bg-white border border-gray-300 rounded p-2 text-xs font-bold text-gray-800 outline-none focus:border-orange-500 shadow-sm transition">
            <div id="selected-paint-label" class="text-[10px] font-bold text-orange-600 bg-orange-50 px-2 py-1 rounded border border-orange-200 truncate">None Selected</div>

                <input type="text" id="pms-code" placeholder="e.g. Custom Match To Sample" oninput="updateCustomPMS()" class="w-full bg-white border border-gray-300 rounded p-1.5 text-xs font-bold outline-none focus:border-blue-500 shadow-inner">
            </div>
        </div>

    </div>

    <!-- RESULTS -->

    <!-- TICKET GENERATOR -->
    <div class="bg-gray-50 p-4 border-t border-gray-200">
        <label class="block text-[10px] font-bold text-gray-400 uppercase mb-2">Production Ticket Details</label>
        <textarea id="job-desc" class="w-full text-xs p-3 border border-gray-300 rounded bg-white h-24 text-gray-700 font-mono outline-none leading-snug custom-scroll shadow-inner" readonly></textarea>
        
        <button onclick="copyTicket(this)" class="w-full mt-3 bg-white hover:bg-gray-100 text-gray-700 font-bold py-2 px-4 border border-gray-300 rounded shadow-sm text-[10px] uppercase tracking-widest transition flex items-center justify-center gap-2">
            <svg class="w-4 h-4 text-gray-500" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2" d="M8 5H6a2 2 0 00-2 2v12a2 2 0 002 2h10a2 2 0 002-2v-1M8 5a2 2 0 002 2h2a2 2 0 002-2M8 5a2 2 0 012-2h2a2 2 0 012 2m0 0h2a2 2 0 012 2v3m2 4H10m0 0l3-3m-3 3l3 3"></path></svg>
            Copy Ticket Details

            Download Production SVG

<script>
let backendData = {}, rowmarkData = [], pmsData = [], swData = [], systemFonts = [];
let activePaintSystem = 'PMS', selectedMat = null, selectedPaint = null, currentMode = 'front';

let lineSettings = [
    { text: 'SAMPLE', family: '', style: '', height: 0.625, caseType: 'upper' },
    { text: '', family: '', style: '', height: 0.375, caseType: 'title' },
    { text: '', family: '', style: '', height: 0.375, caseType: 'title' }
];

// --- UI ACCORDION & BUTTONS ---
function toggleAccordion(contentId, arrowId) {
    document.getElementById(contentId).classList.toggle('hidden');
    document.getElementById(arrowId).classList.toggle('rotate-180');
}

function setLineCount(num) {
    document.getElementById('lines-per-sign').value = num;
    for(let i=1; i<=3; i++) {
        const btn = document.getElementById('btn-line-'+i);
        btn.className = i === num 
            ? "px-2 py-0.5 text-[10px] font-black rounded bg-white text-indigo-700 shadow-sm transition outline-none" 
            : "px-2 py-0.5 text-[10px] font-black rounded text-indigo-600 hover:text-indigo-800 transition outline-none";
    }
    updateLineControls();
}

function updateLineControls() {
    const count = parseInt(document.getElementById('lines-per-sign').value) || 1;
    const container = document.getElementById('line-controls-container');
    container.innerHTML = '';

    const uniqueFamilies = [...new Set(systemFonts.map(f => {
        if (!f.File_Name) return '';
        const parts = f.File_Name.split('-');
        return parts.shift(); 
    }).filter(Boolean))];

    for (let i = 0; i < count; i++) {
        const ls = lineSettings[i];

        if (!uniqueFamilies.includes(ls.family)) {
            ls.family = uniqueFamilies.includes('Arimo') ? 'Arimo' : (uniqueFamilies.slice().shift() || '');
        }

        let familyOpts = uniqueFamilies.map(fam => 
            `<option value="${fam}" ${ls.family === fam ? 'selected' : ''}>${fam.replace(/_/g, ' ')}</option>`
        ).join('');

        const availableStyles = systemFonts
            .filter(f => f.File_Name && f.File_Name.startsWith(ls.family + '-'))
            .map(f => {
                const parts = f.File_Name.split('-');
                const styleWithExt = parts.pop(); 
                return styleWithExt ? styleWithExt.replace('.ttf', '') : '';
            }).filter(Boolean);

        if (!availableStyles.includes(ls.style)) {
            ls.style = availableStyles.includes('Bold') ? 'Bold' : (availableStyles.slice().shift() || '');
        }

        let styleOpts = availableStyles.map(st => 
            `<option value="${st}" ${ls.style === st ? 'selected' : ''}>${st.replace(/([A-Z])/g, ' $1').trim()}</option>`
        ).join('');

        // FIX: Two-tier flex layout prevents overflow
        container.innerHTML += `
        <div class="flex flex-col gap-1.5 bg-white border border-indigo-200 p-2 rounded shadow-sm mb-2">
            <div class="flex items-center gap-2 w-full">
                <span class="text-[10px] font-black text-indigo-700 w-6 text-center uppercase shrink-0">L${i+1}</span>
                <input type="text" value="${ls.text}" placeholder="Enter text..." oninput="updateLineSetting(${i}, 'text', this.value)" class="flex-1 w-full bg-gray-50 border border-gray-200 rounded p-1 text-xs font-bold text-gray-800 outline-none focus:border-indigo-500 shadow-inner">
            </div>
            <div class="flex flex-wrap items-center gap-1.5 w-full justify-end pl-8">
                <select onchange="updateLineSetting(${i}, 'family', this.value)" class="flex-1 min-w-[80px] border border-gray-200 rounded text-[9px] font-bold text-gray-700 outline-none focus:border-indigo-500 p-1 bg-white">
                    ${familyOpts}
                </select>
                <select onchange="updateLineSetting(${i}, 'style', this.value)" class="w-20 border border-gray-200 rounded text-[9px] font-bold text-gray-700 outline-none focus:border-indigo-500 p-1 bg-white">
                    ${styleOpts}
                </select>
                <select onchange="updateLineSetting(${i}, 'caseType', this.value)" class="w-16 border border-gray-200 rounded text-[9px] font-bold text-gray-700 outline-none focus:border-indigo-500 p-1 bg-white">
                    <option value="upper" ${ls.caseType === 'upper' ? 'selected' : ''}>UPPER</option>
                    <option value="title" ${ls.caseType === 'title' ? 'selected' : ''}>Title</option>
                    <option value="lower" ${ls.caseType === 'lower' ? 'selected' : ''}>lower</option>
                    <option value="exact" ${ls.caseType === 'exact' ? 'selected' : ''}>Typed</option>
                </select>
                <div class="flex items-center gap-1 bg-gray-50 border border-gray-200 p-0.5 rounded shadow-inner w-[70px] justify-between">
                    <input type="number" step="0.125" min="0.125" value="${ls.height}" onchange="updateLineSetting(${i}, 'height', this.value)" class="w-12 bg-transparent font-black text-indigo-900 text-[10px] text-center outline-none pl-1">
                    <span class="text-indigo-800 font-black text-[9px] pr-1.5">"</span>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>`;
    }
    runCalc();
}

function updateLineSetting(index, field, val) {
    if (field === 'height') lineSettings[index].height = isNaN(parseFloat(val)) || parseFloat(val) < 0.125 ? 0.125 : parseFloat(val);
    else lineSettings[index][field] = val;
    runCalc();
}

function formatLineCase(str, mode) {
    if (!str) return "";
    if (mode === 'upper') return str.toUpperCase();
    if (mode === 'lower') return str.toLowerCase();
    if (mode === 'title') return str.replace(/\w\S*/g, txt => txt.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + txt.substr(1).toLowerCase());
    return str;
}

// --- UI TOGGLES ---
function setReverseTab(tab) {
    const isMat = tab === 'mat';
    document.getElementById('btn-tab-mat').className = `flex-1 py-1.5 text-[10px] font-black rounded transition uppercase tracking-widest ${isMat ? 'bg-white shadow-sm text-blue-700' : 'text-gray-500 hover:text-gray-800 border border-transparent'}`;
    document.getElementById('btn-tab-paint').className = `flex-1 py-1.5 text-[10px] font-black rounded transition uppercase tracking-widest ${!isMat ? 'bg-white shadow-sm text-blue-700' : 'text-gray-500 hover:text-gray-800 border border-transparent'}`;
    document.getElementById('mat-container').classList.toggle('hidden', !isMat);
    document.getElementById('paint-container').classList.toggle('hidden', isMat);
}

function setMode(mode) {
    currentMode = mode;
    const isFront = mode === 'front';
    document.getElementById('btn-front').className = `flex-1 py-2 text-xs font-bold rounded transition-all ${isFront ? 'bg-white shadow-sm border border-gray-200 text-blue-700' : 'text-gray-500 hover:text-gray-800 border border-transparent'}`;
    document.getElementById('btn-reverse').className = `flex-1 py-2 text-xs font-bold rounded transition-all ${!isFront ? 'bg-white shadow-sm border border-gray-200 text-blue-700' : 'text-gray-500 hover:text-gray-800 border border-transparent'}`;
    document.getElementById('reverse-tabs').classList.toggle('hidden', isFront);
    if(isFront) {
        document.getElementById('mat-container').classList.remove('hidden');
        document.getElementById('paint-container').classList.add('hidden');
    } else {
        setReverseTab('mat');
    }
    updateSwatches();
}

function setPaintSystem(sys) {
    activePaintSystem = sys;
    document.getElementById('btn-pms').className = `flex-1 py-1.5 text-[10px] font-black rounded transition uppercase tracking-widest ${sys === 'PMS' ? 'bg-white shadow-sm text-orange-700 border border-orange-200' : 'text-orange-600 hover:text-orange-800 border border-transparent'}`;
    document.getElementById('btn-sw').className = `flex-1 py-1.5 text-[10px] font-black rounded transition uppercase tracking-widest ${sys === 'SW' ? 'bg-white shadow-sm text-orange-700 border border-orange-200' : 'text-orange-600 hover:text-orange-800 border border-transparent'}`;
    document.getElementById('paint-search').placeholder = sys === 'PMS' ? "Search PMS Colors..." : "Search SW Colors...";
    document.getElementById('paint-search').value = "";
    buildPaintSwatches();
}

function handleReverseAutoPaint(mat) {
    const isBlack = mat.Cap_Color.toLowerCase().includes('black');
    const isWhite = mat.Cap_Color.toLowerCase().includes('white');
    if (isBlack || isWhite) {
        const targetCode = isBlack ? 'STD-WHT' : 'STD-BLK';
        const list = activePaintSystem === 'PMS' ? pmsData : swData;
        const defaultPaint = list.find(p => p.Code === targetCode);
        if (defaultPaint) {
            selectedPaint = defaultPaint;
            document.getElementById('custom-pms-wrap').classList.add('hidden');
            document.getElementById('pms-code').value = '';
            document.getElementById('selected-paint-label').innerText = `[${selectedPaint.Code}] ${selectedPaint.Name}`;
            buildPaintSwatches();
        }
    }
}

// --- GLOBAL UI BUILDERS (Phase 4) ---
function updateSwatches() {
    const filtered = rowmarkData.filter(c => currentMode === 'reverse' ? c.Series.includes('Reverse') : !c.Series.includes('Reverse'));
    SignOS_UI.buildColorGrid({
        containerId: 'rowmark-grid',
        data: filtered,
        type: 'rowmark',
        isReverse: currentMode === 'reverse',
        onSelect: (item) => {
            selectedMat = item;
            if (currentMode === 'reverse') handleReverseAutoPaint(item);
            updateMaterialLabel();
            runCalc();
        }
    });

    // Force default selection to [1-181] Black Face / White Text
    setTimeout(() => {
        const targetBtn = document.querySelector('#rowmark-grid button[data-code="222-402"]') || document.querySelector('#rowmark-grid button');
        if(targetBtn) targetBtn.click();
    }, 50);
}

function buildPaintSwatches() {
    SignOS_UI.buildColorGrid({
        containerId: 'paint-grid',
        data: activePaintSystem === 'PMS' ? pmsData : swData,
        type: 'paint',
        activeRingClass: 'ring-orange-500',
        showCustom: true,
        onCustom: () => {
            selectedPaint = { Code: 'CUSTOM', Name: 'Custom Manual Color', Hex_Code: '#e2e8f0' };
            document.getElementById('custom-pms-wrap').classList.remove('hidden');
            document.getElementById('selected-paint-label').innerText = "Custom Color Mode Active";
            updateMaterialLabel();
            runCalc();
        },
        onSelect: (item) => {
            selectedPaint = item;
            document.getElementById('custom-pms-wrap').classList.add('hidden');
            document.getElementById('pms-code').value = '';
            document.getElementById('selected-paint-label').innerText = `[${item.Code}] ${item.Name}`;
            updateMaterialLabel();
            runCalc();
        }
    });
}

function updateCustomPMS() {
    const val = document.getElementById('pms-code').value.trim();
    document.getElementById('selected-paint-label').innerText = val ? `Custom: ${val}` : "Custom Manual Color";
    updateMaterialLabel();
    runCalc();
}

function updateMaterialLabel() {
    if (!selectedMat) return;
    const thickTxt = selectedMat.Thickness ? `(${selectedMat.Thickness})` : "";
    if (currentMode === 'front') {
        document.getElementById('selected-color-label').innerText = `[${selectedMat.Item_Code}] ${selectedMat.Cap_Color} Face / ${selectedMat.Core_Color} Text ${thickTxt}`;
    } else {
        let paintName = "TBD";
        if (selectedPaint && selectedPaint.Code !== 'CUSTOM') paintName = selectedPaint.Name;
        else if (document.getElementById('pms-code').value) paintName = document.getElementById('pms-code').value;
        document.getElementById('selected-color-label').innerText = `[${selectedMat.Item_Code}] ${selectedMat.Cap_Color} Face / ${paintName} Text ${thickTxt}`;
    }
}

// --- CALCULATION ENGINE (Updated to Async Physics-First) ---
async function runCalc() {
    if(!backendData.Retail_Min_Order || !selectedMat) return;

    SignOS_Canvas.enforceSheetLimits('w', 'h', 'sheet-warn', 24, 48);

    try {
        const pmsCode = document.getElementById('pms-code').value.trim();
        const isReverse = currentMode === 'reverse';
        let finalPaintName = "";
        let activePaintHex = "#FFFFFF";

        if (isReverse) {
            if (selectedPaint && selectedPaint.Code === 'CUSTOM') {
                finalPaintName = pmsCode ? `CUSTOM: ${pmsCode}` : "Custom Match TBD";
                activePaintHex = "#e2e8f0";
            } else if (selectedPaint) {
                finalPaintName = `[${selectedPaint.Code}] ${selectedPaint.Name}`;
                activePaintHex = selectedPaint.Hex_Code;
            } else {
                finalPaintName = "TBD / None Selected";
            }
        }

        const inputs = {
            qty: parseFloat(document.getElementById('qty').value) || 1,
            w: parseFloat(document.getElementById('w').value) || 10,
            h: parseFloat(document.getElementById('h').value) || 2,
            isReverse: isReverse,
            mat: selectedMat,
            paint: finalPaintName
        };

        const result = calculateNameplate(inputs, backendData);
        if (!result || !result.retail) return;

        const ret = result.retail;
        const fmt = (n) => "$" + (n || 0).toFixed(2);
        const totalSqin = (inputs.w * inputs.h) * inputs.qty;

        document.getElementById('lbl-sqin').innerText = totalSqin.toFixed(1);
        document.getElementById('ui-unit').innerText = fmt(ret.unitPrice);
        document.getElementById('ui-total').innerText = fmt(ret.grandTotal);
        document.getElementById('ui-print').innerText = fmt(ret.printTotal);

        const minOrder = parseFloat(backendData.Retail_Min_Order || 35);
        document.getElementById('ui-min-text').innerText = `Shop Minimum: $${minOrder}`;
        document.getElementById('min-badge').classList.toggle('hidden', !ret.isMinApplied);

        // --- THE PHYSICS-FIRST BRIDGE ---
        const linesCount = parseInt(document.getElementById('lines-per-sign').value) || 1;
        const githubBase = "https://raw.githubusercontent.com/SignStoreERP/signos-app/main/fonts/";
        
        inputs.gap = parseFloat(document.getElementById('line-spacing').value) || 0;
        inputs.paintHex = activePaintHex;

        // Apply formatting and dynamically construct the filename from the new dropdowns
        let formattedLines = lineSettings.slice(0, linesCount).map(ls => {
            return { 
                text: formatLineCase(ls.text, ls.caseType),
                fileName: `${ls.family}-${ls.style}.ttf`,
                height: ls.height 
            };
        });

        // Create the virtual manifest (Notice we removed 'systemFonts' from the arguments here!)
        const manifest = await SignOS_Builder.buildManifest(inputs, formattedLines, githubBase);

        // Render to Screen (The "Monitor")
        renderPhysicsToScreen(manifest, 'preview-canvas');

        // Warnings
        const availableH = inputs.h - 0.5;
        document.getElementById('overflow-warn-box').classList.toggle('hidden', 
            (manifest.totalHeight > availableH && document.getElementById('overflow-mode').value === 'strict'));

        document.getElementById('bright-warn-box').classList.toggle('hidden', !selectedMat.Cap_Color.includes('Bright'));
        
        // --- TICKET GENERATION ---
        let brandTxt = `Rowmark ${inputs.mat.Series} (${inputs.mat.Thickness})`;
        const bevelTxt = document.getElementById('bevel-edges').value === 'Yes' ? 'Bevel Edges. ' : 'Straight Cut Edge. ';
        let explicitNotes = `${bevelTxt}No backers. No hardware. No installation. No raised copy. No braille.`;

        let combinedText = formattedLines.map(ls => ls.text).filter(Boolean).join(' / ');

        document.getElementById('job-desc').value = inputs.isReverse 
            ? `(x${inputs.qty}) ${inputs.w}" x ${inputs.h}" ADA Nameplates - ${brandTxt} Reverse Engraved [${inputs.mat.Item_Code}] ${inputs.mat.Cap_Color} face with ${inputs.paint} painted text.\nCopy: ${combinedText}\n\n${explicitNotes}`
            : `(x${inputs.qty}) ${inputs.w}" x ${inputs.h}" ADA Nameplates - ${brandTxt} Front Engraved [${inputs.mat.Item_Code}] ${inputs.mat.Cap_Color} face with ${inputs.mat.Core_Color} text.\nCopy: ${combinedText}\n\n${explicitNotes}`;

    } catch(e) { console.error(e); }
}

function copyTicket(btn) {
    const desc = document.getElementById('job-desc');
    desc.select();
    desc.setSelectionRange(0, 99999);
    navigator.clipboard.writeText(desc.value);
    
    const originalHTML = btn.innerHTML;
    btn.innerHTML = "✅ COPIED TO CLIPBOARD!";
    btn.classList.add('bg-green-100', 'text-green-800', 'border-green-300');
    btn.classList.remove('bg-white', 'text-gray-700', 'border-gray-300');
    
    setTimeout(() => {
        btn.innerHTML = originalHTML;
        btn.classList.remove('bg-green-100', 'text-green-800', 'border-green-300');
        btn.classList.add('bg-white', 'text-gray-700', 'border-gray-300');
    }, 2500);
}

// --- INIT DATA FETCH (Phase 3 API Loader) ---
window.addEventListener('load', async () => {
    if (typeof injectHeader === 'function') injectHeader("ADA Etch Nameplates");
    
    // 1. TRIGGER THE NEW CENTRALIZED LOADER
    SignOS_UI.showLoader('preview-wrapper', 'Connecting to Source Data...<br>Downloading Custom Fonts');

    const statusText = document.getElementById("status-text");
    const statusDot = document.getElementById("status-dot");

    try {
        const payload = await SignOS.fetchProductData('PROD_Nameplates', ['REF_Colors_Rowmark', 'REF_Colors_Paint', 'REF_Colors_PMS', 'REF_Fonts']);
        backendData = payload.config;
        rowmarkData = payload.tables['REF_Colors_Rowmark'] || [];
        
        // Format payload arrays into standard {Code, Name, Hex_Code} for UI Builder
        swData = (payload.tables['REF_Colors_Paint'] || []).map(p => ({
            Code: p['Color Code'] || p['Code'] || 'Unknown',
            Name: p['Color Name'] || p['Name'] || 'Unknown',
            Hex_Code: p['HEX Code'] || p['Hex_Code'] || '#FFFFFF'
        }));

        pmsData = (payload.tables['REF_Colors_PMS'] || []).map(p => ({
            Code: p['PMS Name / Code'] || 'Unknown',
            Name: p['PMS Name / Code'] || 'Unknown',
            Hex_Code: p['HEX Code'] || '#FFFFFF'
        }));

        // Load custom fonts to DOM via Phase 4 Canvas Engine
        systemFonts = (payload.tables['REF_Fonts'] || []).filter(f => String(f.Is_Active).toUpperCase() === 'TRUE');
        SignOS_Canvas.loadFonts(systemFonts);

        // Fallback to ensure it pulls a valid font object instead of returning an Array

        if(statusText) {
            statusText.innerText = "ONLINE";
            statusText.className = "font-bold text-green-500";
            if(statusDot) {
                statusDot.className = "w-2 h-2 rounded-full bg-green-500";
                statusDot.classList.remove("animate-pulse");
            }
        }

        updateLineControls();
        setPaintSystem('PMS');
        setMode('front');
        
        // DISMISS THE LOADER ON SUCCESS
        SignOS_UI.hideLoader('preview-wrapper');

    } catch(e) {
        if(statusText) {
            statusText.innerText = "OFFLINE (API FAILED)";
            statusText.className = "font-bold text-red-500";
        }
        // SHOW ERROR STATE ON LOADER
        SignOS_UI.hideLoader('preview-wrapper', true);
        console.error("API Load Failed:", e);
    }
});
</script>

let backendData = {};
function enforceLimits(maxShort) {
    let wEl = document.getElementById('w'); let hEl = document.getElementById('h'); let warnEl = document.getElementById('sheet-warn');
    if (!wEl || !hEl) return;
    let w = parseFloat(wEl.value) || 0; let h = parseFloat(hEl.value) || 0; let didClamp = false;
    if (w > maxShort && h > maxShort) { if (w > h) { h = maxShort; hEl.value = h; } else { w = maxShort; wEl.value = w; } didClamp = true; }
    if (warnEl) { if (didClamp) { warnEl.classList.remove('hidden'); clearTimeout(warnEl.timeoutId); warnEl.timeoutId = setTimeout(() => warnEl.classList.add('hidden'), 3000); } }
}
function runCalc() {
    if(!backendData.Retail_Min_Order) return;
    enforceLimits(52);
    try {
        const inputs = {
            qty: parseFloat(document.getElementById('qty').value) || 1, w: parseFloat(document.getElementById('w').value) || 12, h: parseFloat(document.getElementById('h').value) || 12,
            material: document.getElementById('material').value, shape: document.getElementById('shape').value, weeding: document.getElementById('weeding').value, masking: document.getElementById('masking').value
        };
        const result = calculateDecal(inputs, backendData);
        if (!result || !result.retail) return;
        const ret = result.retail; const fmt = (n) => "$" + (n || 0).toFixed(2);
        document.getElementById('lbl-sqft').innerText = (((inputs.w * inputs.h) / 144) * inputs.qty).toFixed(1);
        document.getElementById('ui-unit').innerText = fmt(ret.unitPrice);
        document.getElementById('ui-total').innerText = fmt(ret.grandTotal);
        document.getElementById('ui-print').innerText = fmt(ret.printTotal);
        document.getElementById('ui-min-text').innerText = `Shop Minimum: $${parseFloat(backendData.Retail_Min_Order || 35)}`;
        document.getElementById('min-badge').classList.toggle('hidden', !ret.isMinApplied);
        
        const matTxt = document.getElementById('material').options[document.getElementById('material').selectedIndex].text;
        const cutTxt = inputs.shape === 'Rectangle' ? 'Square Cut' : 'Contour Cut';
        const weedTxt = inputs.weeding === 'Complex' ? ' (Complex Weeding)' : '';
        const maskTxt = inputs.masking === 'Yes' ? 'Pre-Masked with Transfer Tape.' : 'No Transfer Tape.';
        document.getElementById('job-desc').value = `(x${inputs.qty}) ${inputs.w}" x ${inputs.h}" ${matTxt}.\n${cutTxt}${weedTxt}. ${maskTxt}`;
    } catch(e) { console.error(e); }
}

});
