<script>
let backendData = {};

function enforceSheetLimits(maxShort, maxLong) {
    let wEl = document.getElementById('w');
    let hEl = document.getElementById('h');
    let warnEl = document.getElementById('sheet-warn');
    if (!wEl || !hEl) return;
    
    let w = parseFloat(wEl.value) || 0;
    let h = parseFloat(hEl.value) || 0;
    let didClamp = false;

    if (w > maxLong) { w = maxLong; wEl.value = w; didClamp = true; }
    if (h > maxLong) { h = maxLong; hEl.value = h; didClamp = true; }
    if (w > maxShort && h > maxShort) {
        if (w > h) { h = maxShort; hEl.value = h; } else { w = maxShort; wEl.value = w; }
        didClamp = true;
    }

    if (warnEl) {
        if (didClamp) {
            warnEl.classList.remove('hidden');
            clearTimeout(warnEl.timeoutId);
            warnEl.timeoutId = setTimeout(() => warnEl.classList.add('hidden'), 3000);
        }
    }
}

// SAFE UI CONSTRAINT (Waits for page load)
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    const thickDropdown = document.getElementById('thickness');
    if (thickDropdown) {
        thickDropdown.addEventListener('change', function(e) {
            const colorDropdown = document.getElementById('color');
            if (!colorDropdown) return;

            const isQuarterInch = e.target.value.includes('1/4') || e.target.value.includes('0.25') || e.target.value.includes('.25');
            
            for (let i = 0; i < colorDropdown.options.length; i++) {
                if (colorDropdown.options[i].value === 'Black') {
                    colorDropdown.options[i].disabled = !isQuarterInch;
                }
            }
            
            if (!isQuarterInch && colorDropdown.value === 'Black') {
                colorDropdown.value = 'White'; 
            }
            
            if (typeof runCalc === 'function') runCalc(); 
        });
    }
});

function runCalc() {
    if(!backendData.Retail_Min_Order) return;
    enforceSheetLimits(48, 96);

    try {
        const inputs = {
            qty: parseFloat(document.getElementById('qty').value) || 1,
            w: parseFloat(document.getElementById('w').value) || 24,
            h: parseFloat(document.getElementById('h').value) || 18,
            thickness: document.getElementById('thickness').value, 
            color: document.getElementById('color').value,
            shape: document.getElementById('shape').value
        };

        const result = calculateAcrylic(inputs, backendData);
        if (!result || !result.retail) return;

        const ret = result.retail;
        const fmt = (n) => "$" + (n || 0).toFixed(2);
        const totalSqFt = ((inputs.w * inputs.h) / 144) * inputs.qty;

        document.getElementById('lbl-sqft').innerText = totalSqFt.toFixed(1);
        document.getElementById('ui-unit').innerText = fmt(ret.unitPrice);
        document.getElementById('ui-total').innerText = fmt(ret.grandTotal);
        document.getElementById('ui-print').innerText = fmt(ret.printTotal);

        if (ret.routerFee > 0) {
            document.getElementById('row-router').classList.remove('hidden');
            document.getElementById('ui-router').innerText = fmt(ret.routerFee);
        } else { document.getElementById('row-router').classList.add('hidden'); }

        const minOrder = parseFloat(backendData.Retail_Min_Order || 75);
        document.getElementById('ui-min-text').innerText = `Shop Minimum: $${minOrder}`;
        document.getElementById('min-badge').classList.toggle('hidden', !ret.isMinApplied);

        const cutTxt = inputs.shape === 'Rectangle' ? 'Square/Rectangle Cut' : 'CNC Custom Profile Cut';
        const thkTxt = document.getElementById('thickness').options[document.getElementById('thickness').selectedIndex].text;

        document.getElementById('job-desc').value = `(x${inputs.qty}) ${inputs.w}" x ${inputs.h}" ${thkTxt} ${inputs.color} Acrylic Signs.\n${cutTxt}.`;

    } catch(e) {
        console.error(e);
    }
}

// 4. API FETCH & NATIVE STATUS BAR UPDATER
window.addEventListener('load', async () => {
    if (typeof injectHeader === 'function') injectHeader("Acrylic Signs");
    
    const statusText = document.getElementById("status-text");
    const statusDot = document.getElementById("status-dot");

    try {
        const req = await fetch(`${SCRIPT_URL}?req=view_module&tab=PROD_Acrylic_Signs`);
        backendData = await req.json();
        
        if(backendData.error) throw new Error(backendData.error);
        
        if(statusText) {
            statusText.innerText = "ONLINE";
            statusText.className = "font-bold text-green-500";
            if(statusDot) {
                statusDot.className = "w-2 h-2 rounded-full bg-green-500";
                statusDot.classList.remove("animate-pulse");
            }
        }
        
        runCalc(); 
    } catch(e) {
        if(statusText) {
            statusText.innerText = "OFFLINE";
            statusText.className = "font-bold text-red-500";
        }
        console.error(e);
    }
});
</script>
</body>
</html>

function runCalc() {
    if(!backendData.Retail_Min_Order) return;

    try {
        const inputs = {
            qty: parseFloat(document.getElementById('qty').value) || 1,
            sides: parseInt(document.getElementById('sides').value) || 1,
            stakes: document.getElementById('stakes').value === 'true'
        };

        const result = calculateYardSign(inputs, backendData);
        if (!result || !result.retail) return;

        const ret = result.retail;
        const fmt = (n) => "$" + (n || 0).toFixed(2);

        document.getElementById('ui-unit').innerText = fmt(ret.unitPrice);
        document.getElementById('ui-total').innerText = fmt(ret.grandTotal);
        document.getElementById('ui-print').innerText = fmt(ret.printTotal);

        if (ret.stakeTotal > 0) {
            document.getElementById('row-stakes').classList.remove('hidden');
            document.getElementById('ui-stakes').innerText = fmt(ret.stakeTotal);
        } else { document.getElementById('row-stakes').classList.add('hidden'); }

        const minOrder = parseFloat(backendData.Retail_Min_Order || 50);
        document.getElementById('ui-min-text').innerText = `Shop Minimum: $${minOrder}`;
        document.getElementById('min-badge').classList.toggle('hidden', !ret.isMinApplied);

        const sideTxt = inputs.sides === 2 ? "Double-Sided" : "Single-Sided";
        const stakeTxt = inputs.stakes ? "w/ H-Stakes" : "No Hardware";

        document.getElementById('job-desc').value = `(x${inputs.qty}) 24" x 18" 4mm Coroplast Yard Signs.\n${sideTxt} Print. ${stakeTxt}.`;

    } catch(e) {
        console.error(e);
    }
}

    <script>
        let backendData = {}, rowmarkData = [], pmsData = [], swData = [], systemFonts = [];
        let activePaintSystem = 'PMS', selectedMat = null, selectedPaint = null, currentMode = 'front';
        
        let lineSettings = [
            { text: 'SAMPLE', font: '', height: 1.0, caseType: 'upper' },
            { text: '', font: '', height: 0.375, caseType: 'title' },
            { text: '', font: '', height: 0.375, caseType: 'title' }
        ];

        // --- UI ACCORDION & BUTTONS ---
        function toggleAccordion(contentId, arrowId) {
            document.getElementById(contentId).classList.toggle('hidden');
            document.getElementById(arrowId).classList.toggle('rotate-180');
        }

        function setLineCount(num) {
            document.getElementById('lines-per-sign').value = num;
            for(let i=1; i<=3; i++) {
                const btn = document.getElementById('btn-line-'+i);
                btn.className = i === num 
                    ? "px-2 py-0.5 text-[10px] font-black rounded bg-white text-indigo-700 shadow-sm transition outline-none" 
                    : "px-2 py-0.5 text-[10px] font-black rounded text-indigo-600 hover:text-indigo-800 transition outline-none";
            }
            updateLineControls();
        }

        function updateLineControls() {
            const count = parseInt(document.getElementById('lines-per-sign').value) || 1;
            const container = document.getElementById('line-controls-container');
            container.innerHTML = '';

            for (let i = 0; i < count; i++) {
                const ls = lineSettings[i];
                let fontOpts = systemFonts.map(f => `<option value="${f.CSS_Family}" ${ls.font === f.CSS_Family ? 'selected' : ''}>${f.Font_Name}</option>`).join('');
                if(fontOpts === '') fontOpts = '<option value="sans-serif">System Default</option>';

                container.innerHTML += `
                    <div class="flex flex-col sm:flex-row items-center gap-1.5 bg-white border border-indigo-200 p-1.5 rounded shadow-sm">
                        <span class="text-[9px] font-black text-indigo-700 w-full sm:w-6 text-left sm:text-center uppercase shrink-0">L${i+1}</span>
                        <input type="text" value="${ls.text}" placeholder="Enter text..." oninput="updateLineSetting(${i}, 'text', this.value)" class="flex-1 w-full sm:w-auto bg-gray-50 border border-gray-200 rounded p-1 text-xs font-bold text-gray-800 outline-none focus:border-indigo-500 shadow-inner">
                        <div class="flex items-center gap-1.5 w-full sm:w-auto shrink-0 justify-end">
                            <select onchange="updateLineSetting(${i}, 'font', this.value)" class="w-20 border border-gray-200 rounded text-[9px] font-bold text-gray-700 outline-none focus:border-indigo-500 p-1 bg-white">${fontOpts}</select>
                            <select onchange="updateLineSetting(${i}, 'caseType', this.value)" class="w-20 border border-gray-200 rounded text-[9px] font-bold text-gray-700 outline-none focus:border-indigo-500 p-1 bg-white">
                                <option value="upper" ${ls.caseType === 'upper' ? 'selected' : ''}>UPPER</option>
                                <option value="title" ${ls.caseType === 'title' ? 'selected' : ''}>Title</option>
                                <option value="lower" ${ls.caseType === 'lower' ? 'selected' : ''}>lower</option>
                                <option value="exact" ${ls.caseType === 'exact' ? 'selected' : ''}>As Typed</option>
                            </select>
                            <div class="flex items-center gap-1 bg-gray-50 border border-gray-200 p-0.5 rounded shadow-inner">
                                <input type="number" step="0.125" min="0.125" value="${ls.height}" onchange="updateLineSetting(${i}, 'height', this.value)" class="w-12 bg-transparent font-black text-indigo-900 text-[10px] text-center outline-none">
                                <span class="text-indigo-800 font-black text-[9px] pr-1">"</span>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </div>`;
            }
            runCalc();
        }

        function updateLineSetting(index, field, val) {
            if (field === 'height') lineSettings[index].height = isNaN(parseFloat(val)) || parseFloat(val) < 0.125 ? 0.125 : parseFloat(val);
            else lineSettings[index][field] = val;
            runCalc();
        }

        function formatLineCase(str, mode) {
            if (!str) return "";
            if (mode === 'upper') return str.toUpperCase();
            if (mode === 'lower') return str.toLowerCase();
            if (mode === 'title') return str.replace(/\w\S*/g, txt => txt.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + txt.substr(1).toLowerCase());
            return str;
        }

        // --- UI TOGGLES ---
        function setReverseTab(tab) {
            const isMat = tab === 'mat';
            document.getElementById('btn-tab-mat').className = `flex-1 py-1.5 text-[10px] font-black rounded transition uppercase tracking-widest ${isMat ? 'bg-white shadow-sm text-blue-700' : 'text-gray-500 hover:text-gray-800 border border-transparent'}`;
            document.getElementById('btn-tab-paint').className = `flex-1 py-1.5 text-[10px] font-black rounded transition uppercase tracking-widest ${!isMat ? 'bg-white shadow-sm text-blue-700' : 'text-gray-500 hover:text-gray-800 border border-transparent'}`;
            document.getElementById('mat-container').classList.toggle('hidden', !isMat);
            document.getElementById('paint-container').classList.toggle('hidden', isMat);
        }

        function setMode(mode) {
            currentMode = mode;
            const isFront = mode === 'front';
            document.getElementById('btn-front').className = `flex-1 py-2 text-xs font-bold rounded transition-all ${isFront ? 'bg-white shadow-sm border border-gray-200 text-blue-700' : 'text-gray-500 hover:text-gray-800 border border-transparent'}`;
            document.getElementById('btn-reverse').className = `flex-1 py-2 text-xs font-bold rounded transition-all ${!isFront ? 'bg-white shadow-sm border border-gray-200 text-blue-700' : 'text-gray-500 hover:text-gray-800 border border-transparent'}`;
            
            document.getElementById('reverse-tabs').classList.toggle('hidden', isFront);
            if(isFront) {
                document.getElementById('mat-container').classList.remove('hidden');
                document.getElementById('paint-container').classList.add('hidden');
            } else {
                setReverseTab('mat');
            }
            updateSwatches();
        }

        function setPaintSystem(sys) {
            activePaintSystem = sys;
            document.getElementById('btn-pms').className = `flex-1 py-1.5 text-[10px] font-black rounded transition uppercase tracking-widest ${sys === 'PMS' ? 'bg-white shadow-sm text-orange-700 border border-orange-200' : 'text-orange-600 hover:text-orange-800 border border-transparent'}`;
            document.getElementById('btn-sw').className = `flex-1 py-1.5 text-[10px] font-black rounded transition uppercase tracking-widest ${sys === 'SW' ? 'bg-white shadow-sm text-orange-700 border border-orange-200' : 'text-orange-600 hover:text-orange-800 border border-transparent'}`;
            document.getElementById('paint-search').placeholder = sys === 'PMS' ? "Search PMS Colors..." : "Search SW Colors...";
            document.getElementById('paint-search').value = ""; 
            buildPaintSwatches();
        }

        function handleReverseAutoPaint(mat) {
            const isBlack = mat.Cap_Color.toLowerCase().includes('black');
            const isWhite = mat.Cap_Color.toLowerCase().includes('white');
            if (isBlack || isWhite) {
                const targetCode = isBlack ? 'STD-WHT' : 'STD-BLK';
                const list = activePaintSystem === 'PMS' ? pmsData : swData;
                const defaultPaint = list.find(p => p.Code === targetCode);
                if (defaultPaint) {
                    selectedPaint = defaultPaint;
                    document.getElementById('custom-pms-wrap').classList.add('hidden');
                    document.getElementById('pms-code').value = '';
                    document.getElementById('selected-paint-label').innerText = `[${selectedPaint.Code}] ${selectedPaint.Name}`;
                    buildPaintSwatches(); 
                }
            }
        }

        // --- GLOBAL UI BUILDERS (Phase 4) ---
        function updateSwatches() {
            const filtered = rowmarkData.filter(c => currentMode === 'reverse' ? c.Series.includes('Reverse') : !c.Series.includes('Reverse'));
            SignOS_UI.buildColorGrid({
                containerId: 'rowmark-grid',
                data: filtered,
                type: 'rowmark',
                isReverse: currentMode === 'reverse',
                onSelect: (item) => {
                    selectedMat = item;
                    if (currentMode === 'reverse') handleReverseAutoPaint(item);
                    updateMaterialLabel();
                    runCalc();
                }
            });

            // Force default selection to [1-181] Black Face / White Text
            setTimeout(() => { 
                const targetBtn = document.querySelector('#rowmark-grid button[data-code="222-402"]') || document.querySelector('#rowmark-grid button'); 
                if(targetBtn) targetBtn.click(); 
            }, 50);
        }

        function buildPaintSwatches() {
            SignOS_UI.buildColorGrid({
                containerId: 'paint-grid',
                data: activePaintSystem === 'PMS' ? pmsData : swData,
                type: 'paint',
                activeRingClass: 'ring-orange-500',
                showCustom: true,
                onCustom: () => {
                    selectedPaint = { Code: 'CUSTOM', Name: 'Custom Manual Color', Hex_Code: '#e2e8f0' };
                    document.getElementById('custom-pms-wrap').classList.remove('hidden');
                    document.getElementById('selected-paint-label').innerText = "Custom Color Mode Active";
                    updateMaterialLabel();
                    runCalc();
                },
                onSelect: (item) => {
                    selectedPaint = item;
                    document.getElementById('custom-pms-wrap').classList.add('hidden');
                    document.getElementById('pms-code').value = '';
                    document.getElementById('selected-paint-label').innerText = `[${item.Code}] ${item.Name}`;
                    updateMaterialLabel();
                    runCalc();
                }
            });
        }

        function updateCustomPMS() {
            const val = document.getElementById('pms-code').value.trim();
            document.getElementById('selected-paint-label').innerText = val ? `Custom: ${val}` : "Custom Manual Color";
            updateMaterialLabel();
            runCalc();
        }

        function updateMaterialLabel() {
            if (!selectedMat) return;
            const thickTxt = selectedMat.Thickness ? `(${selectedMat.Thickness})` : "";
            if (currentMode === 'front') {
                document.getElementById('selected-color-label').innerText = `[${selectedMat.Item_Code}] ${selectedMat.Cap_Color} Face / ${selectedMat.Core_Color} Text ${thickTxt}`;
            } else {
                let paintName = "TBD";
                if (selectedPaint && selectedPaint.Code !== 'CUSTOM') paintName = selectedPaint.Name;
                else if (document.getElementById('pms-code').value) paintName = document.getElementById('pms-code').value;
                document.getElementById('selected-color-label').innerText = `[${selectedMat.Item_Code}] ${selectedMat.Cap_Color} Face / ${paintName} Text ${thickTxt}`;
            }
        }

        // --- CALCULATION ENGINE ---
        function runCalc() {
            if(!backendData.Retail_Min_Order || !selectedMat) return;

            SignOS_Canvas.enforceSheetLimits('w', 'h', 'sheet-warn', 24, 48);

            try {
                const pmsCode = document.getElementById('pms-code').value.trim();
                const isReverse = currentMode === 'reverse';

                let finalPaintName = "";
                let activePaintHex = "#FFFFFF"; 

                if (isReverse) {
                    if (selectedPaint && selectedPaint.Code === 'CUSTOM') {
                        finalPaintName = pmsCode ? `CUSTOM: ${pmsCode}` : "Custom Match TBD";
                        activePaintHex = "#e2e8f0";
                    } else if (selectedPaint) {
                        finalPaintName = `[${selectedPaint.Code}] ${selectedPaint.Name}`;
                        activePaintHex = selectedPaint.Hex_Code;
                    } else {
                        finalPaintName = "TBD / None Selected";
                    }
                }

                const inputs = {
                    qty: parseFloat(document.getElementById('qty').value) || 1,
                    w: parseFloat(document.getElementById('w').value) || 10,
                    h: parseFloat(document.getElementById('h').value) || 2,
                    isReverse: isReverse,
                    mat: selectedMat,
                    paint: finalPaintName
                };

                const result = calculateNameplate(inputs, backendData);
                if (!result || !result.retail) return;

                const ret = result.retail;
                const fmt = (n) => "$" + (n || 0).toFixed(2);
                
                const totalSqin = (inputs.w * inputs.h) * inputs.qty;
                document.getElementById('lbl-sqin').innerText = totalSqin.toFixed(1);
                document.getElementById('ui-unit').innerText = fmt(ret.unitPrice);
                document.getElementById('ui-total').innerText = fmt(ret.grandTotal);
                document.getElementById('ui-print').innerText = fmt(ret.printTotal);

                const minOrder = parseFloat(backendData.Retail_Min_Order || 35);
                document.getElementById('ui-min-text').innerText = `Shop Minimum: $${minOrder}`;
                document.getElementById('min-badge').classList.toggle('hidden', !ret.isMinApplied);

                // --- BOUNDED TEXT PREVIEW MATH (Phase 4 Canvas Abstraction) ---
                const linesCount = parseInt(document.getElementById('lines-per-sign').value) || 1;
                const mode = document.getElementById('overflow-mode').value;
                const canvas = document.getElementById('preview-canvas');
                const warn = document.getElementById('overflow-warn-box');
                const warnBright = document.getElementById('bright-warn-box');
                const gapInches = parseFloat(document.getElementById('line-spacing').value) || 0;
                
                let hasOverflowWarn = false;
                const availableW = inputs.w - 0.5;
                const availableH = inputs.h - 0.5;

                const containerW = document.getElementById('preview-wrapper').clientWidth || 400;
                const maxAllowedH = 160; 
                let scale = Math.min((containerW * 0.9) / inputs.w, maxAllowedH / inputs.h);
                
                canvas.style.width = `${inputs.w * scale}px`;
                canvas.style.height = `${inputs.h * scale}px`;
                canvas.style.backgroundColor = selectedMat.Cap_Hex;
                
                let textColor = currentMode === 'front' ? selectedMat.Core_Hex : activePaintHex;
                let renderedLines = [];
                
                for(let i=0; i<linesCount; i++){
                    let ls = lineSettings[i];
                    let formattedText = formatLineCase(ls.text, ls.caseType);
                    if(!formattedText) continue;
                    
                    let targetH = ls.height;
                    let absoluteMax = SignOS_Canvas.calcMaxHeightForText(formattedText, ls.font, availableW);

                    if(mode === 'shrink') {
                        if (targetH > absoluteMax) targetH = Math.max(0.125, Math.floor(absoluteMax / 0.125) * 0.125);
                    }

                    if (targetH > absoluteMax) hasOverflowWarn = true;

                    renderedLines.push({
                        text: formattedText,
                        fontFam: ls.font,
                        cssCqh: `${(targetH / inputs.h) * 100}cqh` 
                    });
                }

                let totalTextH = renderedLines.reduce((sum, line) => sum + (parseFloat(line.cssCqh) * inputs.h / 100 / 0.72 * 1.2), 0);
                let totalGapH = renderedLines.length > 1 ? (renderedLines.length - 1) * gapInches : 0;
                if ((totalTextH + totalGapH) > availableH && mode === 'strict') hasOverflowWarn = true;

                let linesHtml = renderedLines.map(line => `<span class="whitespace-nowrap font-bold" style="color: ${textColor}; font-family: '${line.fontFam}', sans-serif; font-size: ${line.cssCqh}; line-height: 0.85; margin: 0; padding: 0; display: block;">${line.text}</span>`).join('');
                
                canvas.innerHTML = `<div class="absolute inset-0 flex flex-col items-center justify-center text-center pointer-events-none" style="gap: ${(gapInches / inputs.h) * 100}cqh;">${linesHtml}</div>`;

                warn.classList.toggle('hidden', !hasOverflowWarn);
                warnBright.classList.toggle('hidden', !selectedMat.Cap_Color.includes('Bright'));

                // --- TICKET GENERATION ---
                let brandTxt = `Rowmark ${inputs.mat.Series} (${inputs.mat.Thickness})`;
                const bevelTxt = document.getElementById('bevel-edges').value === 'Yes' ? 'Bevel Edges. ' : 'Straight Cut Edge. ';
                let explicitNotes = `${bevelTxt}No backers. No hardware. No installation. No raised copy. No braille.`;
                let combinedText = lineSettings.slice(0, linesCount).map(ls => formatLineCase(ls.text, ls.caseType)).filter(Boolean).join(' / ');

                document.getElementById('job-desc').value = inputs.isReverse 
                    ? `(x${inputs.qty}) ${inputs.w}" x ${inputs.h}" ADA Nameplates - ${brandTxt} Reverse Engraved [${inputs.mat.Item_Code}] ${inputs.mat.Cap_Color} face with ${inputs.paint} painted text.\nCopy: ${combinedText}\n\n${explicitNotes}`
                    : `(x${inputs.qty}) ${inputs.w}" x ${inputs.h}" ADA Nameplates - ${brandTxt} Front Engraved [${inputs.mat.Item_Code}] ${inputs.mat.Cap_Color} face with ${inputs.mat.Core_Color} text.\nCopy: ${combinedText}\n\n${explicitNotes}`;

            } catch(e) { console.error(e); }
        }

        function copyTicket(btn) {
            const desc = document.getElementById('job-desc');
            desc.select();
            desc.setSelectionRange(0, 99999);
            navigator.clipboard.writeText(desc.value);
            const originalHTML = btn.innerHTML;
            btn.innerHTML = "✅ COPIED TO CLIPBOARD!";
            btn.classList.add('bg-green-100', 'text-green-800', 'border-green-300');
            btn.classList.remove('bg-white', 'text-gray-700', 'border-gray-300');
            setTimeout(() => {
                btn.innerHTML = originalHTML;
                btn.classList.remove('bg-green-100', 'text-green-800', 'border-green-300');
                btn.classList.add('bg-white', 'text-gray-700', 'border-gray-300');
            }, 2500);
        }

        // --- INIT DATA FETCH (Phase 3 API Loader) ---
        window.addEventListener('load', async () => {
            if (typeof injectHeader === 'function') injectHeader("ADA Etch Nameplates");
            
            // 1. TRIGGER THE NEW CENTRALIZED LOADER
            SignOS_UI.showLoader('preview-wrapper', 'Connecting to Source Data...<br>Downloading Custom Fonts');

            const statusText = document.getElementById("status-text");
            const statusDot = document.getElementById("status-dot");

            try {
                const payload = await SignOS.fetchProductData('PROD_Nameplates', ['REF_Colors_Rowmark', 'REF_Colors_Paint', 'REF_Colors_PMS', 'REF_Fonts']);

                backendData = payload.config;
                rowmarkData = payload.tables['REF_Colors_Rowmark'] || [];
                
                // Format payload arrays into standard {Code, Name, Hex_Code} for UI Builder
                swData = (payload.tables['REF_Colors_Paint'] || []).map(p => ({
                    Code: p['Color Code'] || p['Code'] || 'Unknown',
                    Name: p['Color Name'] || p['Name'] || 'Unknown',
                    Hex_Code: p['HEX Code'] || p['Hex_Code'] || '#FFFFFF'
                }));
                
                pmsData = (payload.tables['REF_Colors_PMS'] || []).map(p => ({
                    Code: p['PMS Name / Code'] || 'Unknown',
                    Name: p['PMS Name / Code'] || 'Unknown',
                    Hex_Code: p['HEX Code'] || '#FFFFFF'
                }));

                // Load custom fonts to DOM via Phase 4 Canvas Engine
                systemFonts = (payload.tables['REF_Fonts'] || []).filter(f => String(f.Is_Active).toUpperCase() === 'TRUE');
                SignOS_Canvas.loadFonts(systemFonts);
                
                // Fallback to ensure it pulls a valid font object instead of returning an Array
                let defaultFont = systemFonts.find(f => f.CSS_Family === 'Arimo') || systemFonts.at(0);
                lineSettings.forEach(ls => ls.font = defaultFont ? defaultFont.CSS_Family : 'sans-serif');

                if(statusText) {
                    statusText.innerText = "ONLINE";
                    statusText.className = "font-bold text-green-500";
                    if(statusDot) {
                        statusDot.className = "w-2 h-2 rounded-full bg-green-500";
                        statusDot.classList.remove("animate-pulse");
                    }
                }

                updateLineControls();
                setPaintSystem('PMS'); 
                setMode('front');      

                // 2. DISMISS THE LOADER ON SUCCESS
                SignOS_UI.hideLoader('preview-wrapper');
                
            } catch(e) {
                if(statusText) {
                    statusText.innerText = "OFFLINE (API FAILED)";
                    statusText.className = "font-bold text-red-500";
                }
                
                // 3. SHOW ERROR STATE ON LOADER
                SignOS_UI.hideLoader('preview-wrapper', true);
                
                console.error("API Load Failed:", e);
            }
        });
    </script>
</body>
</html>

            <div><label class="block text-[10px] font-bold text-gray-500 uppercase mb-1">Height</label><input type="number" id="h" value="18" min="1" class="w-full border p-2 rounded font-bold text-gray-800 text-lg text-center bg-gray-50 focus:border-blue-500 outline-none" oninput="runCalc()"></div>
        </div>

        <div id="sheet-warn" class="hidden bg-yellow-50 text-yellow-700 text-[10px] font-bold px-3 py-1.5 rounded border border-yellow-200 transition-opacity">
            ⚠️ Parent sheet size limit reached. Dimensions auto-adjusted.

                    <option value="1">1-Sided</option>

                    <option value="Rectangle">Standard (Square/Rectangle)</option>
                    <option value="CNC Simple">CNC (Simple Shape)</option>
                    <option value="CNC Complex">CNC (Complex Shape)</option>
                </select>

            <span id="ui-unit" class="text-2xl font-black text-blue-900 tracking-tight">$0.00</span>
        </div>

        <!-- LINE ITEMS -->
        <div class="space-y-1 text-xs text-blue-900/70 pt-1">

            <div class="flex justify-between text-orange-700 hidden" id="row-router"><span>CNC Router Fee:</span><span id="ui-router" class="font-bold">$0.00</span></div>
        </div>

        <div class="flex justify-between items-end border-t-2 border-blue-800 my-3 pt-2">
            <div>
                <span class="text-xs font-bold text-blue-800 uppercase block">Total Quote</span>
                <span class="text-[9px] font-bold text-blue-600 uppercase block mt-1" id="ui-min-text">Shop Minimum: $50</span>
                <div id="min-badge" class="hidden bg-red-100 text-red-600 border border-red-200 text-[9px] font-bold px-1 rounded inline-block mt-1">MINIMUM APPLIED</div>

<script>
let backendData = {};

function enforceSheetLimits(maxShort, maxLong) {
    let wEl = document.getElementById('w');
    let hEl = document.getElementById('h');
    let warnEl = document.getElementById('sheet-warn');
    if (!wEl || !hEl) return;
    
    let w = parseFloat(wEl.value) || 0;
    let h = parseFloat(hEl.value) || 0;
    let didClamp = false;

    if (w > maxLong) { w = maxLong; wEl.value = w; didClamp = true; }
    if (h > maxLong) { h = maxLong; hEl.value = h; didClamp = true; }
    if (w > maxShort && h > maxShort) {
        if (w > h) { h = maxShort; hEl.value = h; } else { w = maxShort; wEl.value = w; }
        didClamp = true;
    }

    if (warnEl) {
        if (didClamp) {
            warnEl.classList.remove('hidden');
            clearTimeout(warnEl.timeoutId);
            warnEl.timeoutId = setTimeout(() => warnEl.classList.add('hidden'), 3000);
        }
    }
}

function runCalc() {
    if(!backendData.Retail_Min_Order) return;
    enforceSheetLimits(48, 96); // Foam Core max sheet

    try {
        const inputs = {
            qty: parseFloat(document.getElementById('qty').value) || 1,
            w: parseFloat(document.getElementById('w').value) || 24,
            h: parseFloat(document.getElementById('h').value) || 18,
            sides: parseInt(document.getElementById('sides').value) || 1,
            shape: document.getElementById('shape').value
        };

        const result = calculateFoam(inputs, backendData);
        if (!result || !result.retail) return;

        const ret = result.retail;
        const fmt = (n) => "$" + (n || 0).toFixed(2);
        const totalSqFt = ((inputs.w * inputs.h) / 144) * inputs.qty;

        document.getElementById('lbl-sqft').innerText = totalSqFt.toFixed(1);
        document.getElementById('ui-unit').innerText = fmt(ret.unitPrice);
        document.getElementById('ui-total').innerText = fmt(ret.grandTotal);
        document.getElementById('ui-print').innerText = fmt(ret.printTotal);

        if (ret.routerFee > 0) {
            document.getElementById('row-router').classList.remove('hidden');
            document.getElementById('ui-router').innerText = fmt(ret.routerFee);
        } else { 
            document.getElementById('row-router').classList.add('hidden'); 
        }

        const minOrder = parseFloat(backendData.Retail_Min_Order || 50);
        document.getElementById('ui-min-text').innerText = `Shop Minimum: $${minOrder}`;
        document.getElementById('min-badge').classList.toggle('hidden', !ret.isMinApplied);

        const sideTxt = inputs.sides === 2 ? "Double-Sided" : "Single-Sided";
        const cutTxt = inputs.shape === 'Rectangle' ? 'Square/Rectangle Cut' : 'Custom CNC Cut';
        
        document.getElementById('job-desc').value = `(x${inputs.qty}) ${inputs.w}" x ${inputs.h}" 3/16" Foam Core Boards.\n${sideTxt}. ${cutTxt}.`;

    } catch(e) {
        console.error(e);
    }
}

// API FETCH & NATIVE STATUS BAR UPDATER
window.addEventListener('load', async () => {
    if (typeof injectHeader === 'function') injectHeader("Foam Core Boards");
    
    const statusText = document.getElementById("status-text");
    const statusDot = document.getElementById("status-dot");

    try {
        const req = await fetch(`${SCRIPT_URL}?req=view_module&tab=PROD_Foam_Signs`);
        backendData = await req.json();
        
        if(backendData.error) throw new Error(backendData.error);
        
        if(statusText) {
            statusText.innerText = "ONLINE";
            statusText.className = "font-bold text-green-500";
            if(statusDot) {
                statusDot.className = "w-2 h-2 rounded-full bg-green-500";
                statusDot.classList.remove("animate-pulse");
            }
        }
        
        runCalc(); 
    } catch(e) {
        if(statusText) {
            statusText.innerText = "OFFLINE";
            statusText.className = "font-bold text-red-500";
        }
        console.error(e);
    }
});
</script>
</body>
</html>

<script>
    const TAB_NAME = "PROD_Vinyl_Banners";
    let backend = {};
    let currentUser = { name: "Guest", role: "VIEW", mode: "sales" };

    function initSession() {
        const params = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
        const urlMode = params.get('mode');
        const storeUser = sessionStorage.getItem('signos_user');
        const storeRole = sessionStorage.getItem('signos_role');

        if(storeUser) currentUser.name = storeUser;
        if(storeRole) currentUser.role = storeRole;

        if (currentUser.role === 'ADMIN') currentUser.mode = urlMode || 'dev';
        else if (currentUser.role === 'PROD') currentUser.mode = 'production';
        else currentUser.mode = 'sales';

        document.getElementById('auth-user').innerText = currentUser.name;
        document.getElementById('auth-role').innerText = currentUser.role;

        const body = document.body;
        body.classList.remove('mode-sales', 'mode-prod', 'mode-admin');
        
        if(currentUser.mode === 'sales') { body.classList.add('mode-sales'); switchTab('retail'); }
        else if (currentUser.mode === 'production') { body.classList.add('mode-prod'); switchTab('cost'); }
        else { body.classList.add('mode-admin'); }
    }

    function goBack() { window.location.href = `menu.html?mode=${currentUser.mode}`; }
    function switchTab(id) { document.querySelectorAll('.tab-content').forEach(el => el.classList.remove('active')); document.querySelectorAll('.tab-btn').forEach(el => el.classList.remove('active')); document.getElementById('tab-'+id).classList.add('active'); document.getElementById('btn-'+id).classList.add('active'); }
    function toggleDiscounts() { document.getElementById('discount-table').classList.toggle('hidden'); }
    function togglePockets() { document.getElementById('opt-pockets').classList.toggle('hidden'); }
    function setSides(n) { document.getElementById('sides').value = n; document.querySelectorAll('.side-btn').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('selected')); document.getElementById('btn-side-' + n).classList.add('selected'); calculate(); }

    function checkSides() {
        const mat = document.getElementById('material').value;
        const btnDouble = document.getElementById('btn-side-2');
        const allowDouble = (mat === '18oz');
        if (!allowDouble) { setSides(1); btnDouble.classList.add('disabled'); btnDouble.title = "2-Sided Print available on 18oz Blockout Only"; } 
        else { btnDouble.classList.remove('disabled'); btnDouble.title = ""; }
    }

    window.onload = async function() {
        initSession();
        const statusText = document.getElementById("status-text");
        const statusDot = document.getElementById("status-dot");
        const vDisplay = document.getElementById("version-display");
        
        try {
            // TELEMETRY
            const response = await fetch(`${SCRIPT_URL}?tab=${TAB_NAME}&ip=${clientIP}&user=${currentUser.name}&role=${currentUser.role}&req=view_module`);
            const data = await response.json();
            if (data.error) throw new Error(data.error);
            backend = data;

            // Kill Switch
            const isLive = (backend.Is_Live === undefined) ? true : (backend.Is_Live === true || backend.Is_Live === "TRUE");
            if (!isLive && currentUser.role !== 'ADMIN') {
                document.getElementById('main-card').innerHTML = `<div class="p-10 text-center"><h1 class="text-xl font-black text-gray-400">MODULE OFFLINE</h1><button onclick="goBack()" class="mt-6 bg-blue-600 text-white px-4 py-2 rounded font-bold text-xs">Return to Menu</button></div>`;
                return;
            }

            const isDev = currentUser.mode === 'dev';
            statusText.innerText = isDev ? "DEV MODE" : "ONLINE";
            statusText.className = isDev ? "font-bold text-orange-500" : "font-bold text-green-500";
            statusDot.className = isDev ? "w-2 h-2 rounded-full bg-orange-500" : "w-2 h-2 rounded-full bg-green-500";
            statusDot.classList.remove("animate-pulse");

            const ver = isDev ? (backend.Sys_Version_Dev || 'v0.0') : (backend.Sys_Version_Live || 'v0.0');
            vDisplay.innerText = isDev ? `(Beta ${ver})` : `Live ${ver}`;
            vDisplay.classList.remove('hidden');

            if(backend.Item_Name) document.getElementById("product-label").innerText = backend.Item_Name;
            checkSides();
            calculate();

        } catch (e) {
            statusText.innerText = "OFFLINE";
            statusText.className = "font-bold text-red-500";
            document.getElementById("error-msg").innerText = e.message;
            document.getElementById("error-msg").classList.remove("hidden");
        }
    };

    function calculate() {
        if (!backend.Item_Name) return;

        const w = parseFloat(document.getElementById('width').value) || 0;
        const h = parseFloat(document.getElementById('height').value) || 0;
        const qty = parseFloat(document.getElementById('qty').value) || 1;
        const mat = document.getElementById('material').value;
        const sides = parseInt(document.getElementById('sides').value);
        const numFiles = parseFloat(document.getElementById('files').value) || 1;
        const hasHems = document.getElementById('has-hems').checked;
        const hasGrommets = document.getElementById('has-grommets').checked;
        const hasWindSlits = document.getElementById('has-windslits').checked;
        const hasPockets = document.getElementById('has-pockets').checked;
        const incDesign = document.getElementById('inc-design').checked;
        const setupPerFile = document.getElementById('setup-per-file').checked;

        const sqft = (w * h) / 144;
        const totalSqFt = sqft * qty;

        // --- MACHINE CONSTRAINT ---
        const minDim = Math.min(w, h);
        const maxWidth = parseFloat(backend.Constraint_Max_Width || 62);
        const warnBanner = document.getElementById('size-warn');
        const inHouseTab = document.getElementById('tab-cost');
        const costBtn = document.getElementById('btn-cost');
        let isOversized = false;

        if (minDim > maxWidth) {
            isOversized = true;
            warnBanner.classList.remove('hidden');
            inHouseTab.classList.add('blur-section');
            costBtn.classList.add('text-red-300', 'cursor-not-allowed');
            if(inHouseTab.classList.contains('active')) switchTab('vend');
        } else {
            warnBanner.classList.add('hidden');
            inHouseTab.classList.remove('blur-section');
            costBtn.classList.remove('text-red-300', 'cursor-not-allowed');
        }

        // --- 1. RETAIL ---
        let baseRate = 0;
        if (mat === '13oz') {
            if (minDim <= 12) baseRate = parseFloat(backend.Retail_Price_1ft_13oz || 6.50);
            else if (sqft < parseFloat(backend.Retail_Trigger_Small || 10)) baseRate = parseFloat(backend.Retail_Price_Small_13oz || 6.00);
            else baseRate = parseFloat(backend.Retail_Price_Base_13oz || 5.00);
        }
        else if (mat === '15oz') baseRate = parseFloat(backend.Retail_Price_Base_15oz || 6.50);
        else if (mat === '18oz') baseRate = parseFloat(backend.Retail_Price_Base_18oz || 8.00);
        else if (mat === 'Mesh') baseRate = parseFloat(backend.Retail_Price_Base_Mesh || 7.00);

        if (sides === 2) { baseRate += parseFloat(backend.Retail_Adder_DS_SqFt || 3.00); }

        let discPct = 0;
        let currentBestTier = 0;
        const tiers = [];
        let i = 1;
        while(backend[`Tier_${i}_Qty`]) {
            const tQty = parseFloat(backend[`Tier_${i}_Qty`]);
            const tDisc = parseFloat(backend[`Tier_${i}_Disc`] || 0);
            tiers.push({ q: tQty, d: tDisc });
            if (qty >= tQty) currentBestTier = tDisc;
            i++;
        }
        discPct = currentBestTier;

        const unitRate = baseRate * (1 - discPct);
        const retailPrint = unitRate * totalSqFt;

        let retailPockets = 0;
        if (hasPockets) {
            const pocketLF = (w / 12) * 2;
            retailPockets = pocketLF * qty * parseFloat(backend.Retail_Fin_PolePkt_LF || 3.00);
            document.getElementById('row-ret-pockets').classList.remove('hidden');
            document.getElementById('ret-pockets').innerText = "$" + retailPockets.toFixed(2);
        } else {
            document.getElementById('row-ret-pockets').classList.add('hidden');
        }

        let retailSlits = 0;
        if (hasWindSlits) {
            retailSlits = totalSqFt * parseFloat(backend.Retail_Price_WindSlits_SqFt || 1.00);
            document.getElementById('row-ret-slits').classList.remove('hidden');
            document.getElementById('ret-slits').innerText = "$" + retailSlits.toFixed(2);
        } else {
            document.getElementById('row-ret-slits').classList.add('hidden');
        }

        let feeSetup = parseFloat(backend.Retail_Fee_Setup || 15);
        if (setupPerFile) feeSetup *= numFiles;
        const feeDesign = incDesign ? parseFloat(backend.Retail_Fee_Design || 45) * numFiles : 0;

        let quoteTotal = retailPrint + retailPockets + retailSlits + feeSetup + feeDesign;
        const minOrder = parseFloat(backend.Retail_Min_Order || 50);
        if (quoteTotal < minOrder) { quoteTotal = minOrder; document.getElementById('min-badge').classList.remove('hidden'); }
        else { document.getElementById('min-badge').classList.add('hidden'); }

        // Discount Rows
        let rowsHtml = "";
        tiers.forEach(tier => {
            const trRate = baseRate * (1 - tier.d);
            const trPrint = trRate * (sqft * tier.q);
            const trPocket = hasPockets ? ((w/12)*2 * tier.q * parseFloat(backend.Retail_Fin_PolePkt_LF || 3)) : 0;
            const trSlits = hasWindSlits ? ((sqft * tier.q) * parseFloat(backend.Retail_Price_WindSlits_SqFt || 1)) : 0;
            const trTotalRaw = trPrint + trPocket + trSlits + feeSetup + feeDesign;
            const trFinal = Math.max(trTotalRaw, minOrder);
            const trUnit = trFinal / tier.q;
            const discDisplay = tier.d > 0 ? `<span class="text-[9px] bg-green-100 text-green-700 px-1 rounded ml-1">-${(tier.d*100).toFixed(0)}%</span>` : "";
            rowsHtml += `<tr><td class="pr-4 py-1 text-gray-500">${tier.q}${discDisplay}</td><td class="pr-4 py-1 text-blue-600 font-bold">$${trUnit.toFixed(2)}</td><td class="py-1 text-green-600 font-bold">${(tier.d*100).toFixed(0)}% Off</td></tr>`;
        });
        document.getElementById('discount-rows').innerHTML = rowsHtml;

        // --- 2. IN-HOUSE COST ---
        if (!isOversized) {
            const prodW = hasHems ? w + 2 : w;
            const prodH = hasHems ? h + 2 : h;
            const prodSqFt = (prodW * prodH) / 144;
            const totalProdSqFt = prodSqFt * qty;

            let matCostSqFt = 0; let skuLabel = "";
            if (mat === '13oz') { matCostSqFt = parseFloat(backend.Cost_Media_13oz || 0.26); skuLabel = "VIN_ROL_BAN_13"; }
            else if (mat === '15oz') { matCostSqFt = parseFloat(backend.Cost_Media_15oz || 0.46); skuLabel = "VIN_ROL_BAN_15"; }
            else if (mat === '18oz') { matCostSqFt = parseFloat(backend.Cost_Media_18oz || 0.39); skuLabel = "VIN_ROL_BAN_18"; }
            else { matCostSqFt = parseFloat(backend.Cost_Media_Mesh || 0.33); skuLabel = "VIN_ROL_BAN_MESH"; }
            document.getElementById('lbl-sku-media').innerText = skuLabel;

            const waste = parseFloat(backend.Waste_Factor || 1.15);
            const costMedia = totalProdSqFt * matCostSqFt * waste;
            const costInk = totalProdSqFt * parseFloat(backend.Cost_Ink_Base || 0.16) * sides;
            const perimLF = ((w+h)*2)/12 * qty;
            const costTape = hasHems ? (perimLF * parseFloat(backend.Cost_Hem_Tape || 0.08)) : 0;

            let costGrom = 0; let gromCount = 0;
            if (hasGrommets) {
                gromCount = Math.ceil(perimLF / 2) * qty;
                if (gromCount < 4*qty) gromCount = 4*qty;
                costGrom = gromCount * parseFloat(backend.Cost_Grommet || 0.13);
            }

            const rateOp = parseFloat(backend.Rate_Operator || 25);
            const setupHrs = parseFloat(backend.Retail_Fee_Setup || 15) / 60;
            const costSetup = setupHrs * rateOp;
            const speed = parseFloat(backend.Speed_Print_LF || 18);
            const feedLen = (h < 62) ? w : h;
            const totalFeedFt = (feedLen * qty) / 12;
            const runHrs = (totalFeedFt / speed) * sides;
            const rateMachine = 15;
            const costRun = runHrs * (rateMachine + (rateOp * 0.1));

            const hemMins = hasHems ? (perimLF * parseFloat(backend.Time_Hem_LF || 0.5)) : 0;
            const gromMins = hasGrommets ? (gromCount * parseFloat(backend.Time_Grommet_Per || 1.0)) : 0;
            const slitMins = hasWindSlits ? (totalSqFt * parseFloat(backend.Time_WindSlits_SqFt || 0.1)) : 0;
            const finishHrs = (hemMins + gromMins + slitMins) / 60;
            const costFinish = finishHrs * rateOp;

            const subTotal = costMedia + costInk + costTape + costGrom + costSetup + costRun + costFinish;
            const risk = subTotal * 0.15;
            const totalCost = subTotal + risk;

            const fmt = (n) => new Intl.NumberFormat('en-US', {style:'currency', currency:'USD'}).format(n);
            const fmtTime = (h) => { const hrs = Math.floor(h); const mins = Math.round((h - hrs) * 60); return hrs > 0 ? `${hrs}h ${mins}m` : `${mins}m`; };
            const pct = (n) => (n * 100).toFixed(1) + "%";

            document.getElementById('cost-media').innerText = fmt(costMedia);
            document.getElementById('cost-ink').innerText = fmt(costInk);
            document.getElementById('cost-tape').innerText = fmt(costTape);
            document.getElementById('cost-grom').innerText = fmt(costGrom);
            document.getElementById('time-setup').innerText = fmtTime(setupHrs);
            document.getElementById('cost-setup').innerText = fmt(costSetup);
            document.getElementById('time-run').innerText = fmtTime(runHrs);
            document.getElementById('cost-run').innerText = fmt(costRun);
            document.getElementById('time-finish').innerText = fmtTime(finishHrs);
            document.getElementById('cost-finish').innerText = fmt(costFinish);
            document.getElementById('cost-waste').innerText = fmt(risk);
            document.getElementById('cost-total').innerText = fmt(totalCost);

            const profIn = quoteTotal - totalCost;
            document.getElementById('profit-inhouse').innerText = fmt(profIn);
            if(quoteTotal>0) document.getElementById('margin-inhouse').innerText = pct(profIn/quoteTotal);
        } else {
            document.getElementById('cost-total').innerText = "---";
        }

        // --- 3. VENDED ---
        let vendRate = 0;
        if (mat === '13oz') vendRate = parseFloat(backend.Vend_Cost_13oz || 1.25);
        else if (mat === '15oz') vendRate = parseFloat(backend.Vend_Cost_15oz || 1.75);
        else if (mat === '18oz') vendRate = sides === 2 ? parseFloat(backend.Vend_Cost_18oz_DS || 4.25) : parseFloat(backend.Vend_Cost_18oz_SS || 2.25);
        else vendRate = parseFloat(backend.Vend_Cost_Mesh || 2.44);

        let vendPrint = totalSqFt * vendRate;
        if (hasWindSlits) { vendPrint += (totalSqFt * parseFloat(backend.S365_Add_WindSlits_SqFt || 0.50)); }

        let vendFinish = 0;
        if (hasPockets) vendFinish += (qty * ((w/12)*2) * parseFloat(backend.Vend_PolePkt_LF || 1.00));

        let vendShip = parseFloat(backend.Vend_Shipping || 10);
        if (totalSqFt > 200 || minDim > 48) vendShip = 50;

        const totalVend = vendPrint + vendFinish + vendShip;
        const fmt = (n) => new Intl.NumberFormat('en-US', {style:'currency', currency:'USD'}).format(n);
        const pct = (n) => (n * 100).toFixed(1) + "%";

        document.getElementById('vend-print').innerText = fmt(vendPrint);
        document.getElementById('vend-finish').innerText = fmt(vendFinish);
        document.getElementById('vend-ship').innerText = fmt(vendShip);
        document.getElementById('vend-total').innerText = fmt(totalVend);
        const profVend = quoteTotal - totalVend;
        document.getElementById('profit-vend').innerText = fmt(profVend);
        if(quoteTotal>0) document.getElementById('margin-vend').innerText = pct(profVend/quoteTotal);

        // UI RETAIL
        document.getElementById('lbl-sqft').innerText = totalSqFt.toFixed(1);
        document.getElementById('ret-print').innerText = fmt(retailPrint);
        document.getElementById('ret-setup').innerText = fmt(feeSetup);
        document.getElementById('ret-design').innerText = fmt(feeDesign);
        if(incDesign) document.getElementById('row-design').classList.remove('hidden'); else document.getElementById('row-design').classList.add('hidden');
        document.getElementById('unit-price').innerText = fmt(quoteTotal/qty);
        document.getElementById('total-price').innerText = fmt(quoteTotal);

        // DESC
        const finishTxt = [];
        if(hasHems) finishTxt.push("Hemmed");
        if(hasGrommets) finishTxt.push("Grommeted");
        if(hasPockets) finishTxt.push("Pole Pockets");
        if(hasWindSlits) finishTxt.push("Wind Slits");
        const sideLabel = sides === 2 ? "DOUBLE-SIDED" : "Single-Sided";
        const desc = `(x${qty}) ${w}" x ${h}" ${mat} Vinyl Banner (${sideLabel}). ${finishTxt.join(", ")}. Full Color Print.`;
        document.getElementById('job-desc').value = desc;
    }
</script>
</body>
</html>


========================================
FILE: admin_analytics.html

                        </div>

                <div id="canvas-area" class="flex-1 relative flex flex-col p-4 overflow-hidden min-h-[400px]">

                        <span class="text-5xl mb-4 text-blue-500">📊</span>
                        <h2 class="text-xl font-black text-gray-800 uppercase tracking-widest">Pricing Analytics</h2>
                        <p class="text-sm text-gray-500 font-bold mt-2 uppercase">Select a product from the left menu to load data matrix.</p>
                    </div>

                    <div id="loader" class="absolute inset-0 bg-gray-900/60 z-50 hidden flex flex-col items-center justify-center backdrop-blur-sm transition-all rounded-xl">
                        <div class="animate-spin rounded-full h-14 w-14 border-4 border-white border-t-blue-500 mb-4"></div>
                        <span class="text-xs font-black text-white tracking-widest uppercase">Computing Matrix...</span>
                    </div>

                    <!-- CHART -->
                    <div id="view-chart" class="flex-1 bg-white rounded-2xl border border-gray-200 shadow-sm p-4 relative min-h-0">
                        <canvas id="physicsChart"></canvas>
                    </div>

                    <!-- HEATMAP -->
                    <div id="view-heatmap" class="hidden flex-1 overflow-auto custom-scrollbar bg-white rounded-2xl border border-gray-200 shadow-sm relative min-h-0">
                        <table class="border-collapse text-[11px] w-full table-fixed">

                        </table>
