<script>
const user = sessionStorage.getItem('signos_user') || 'Admin';
let currentTicketId = null;
let allRoadmapData = [];

window.onload = function() { 
    if(typeof injectHeader === 'function') injectHeader("Master Strategy", false);
    loadData(); 
};

function toggleForm() { document.getElementById('side-form').classList.toggle('translate-x-full'); }
function goBack() { window.history.back(); }
function val(obj, key) { if(!obj) return ""; return obj[key] || obj[key.toUpperCase()] || obj[key.toLowerCase()] || ""; }

async function loadData() {
    try {
        const response = await fetch(`${SCRIPT_URL}?req=table&tab=SYS_Roadmap&ip=${clientIP}&user=${user}`);
        const data = await response.json();
        if(data.error) throw new Error(data.error);
        allRoadmapData = data;
        renderSilos(data);
    } catch(e) { console.error(e); }
}

function renderSilos(data) {
    const container = document.getElementById('board-container');
    container.innerHTML = "";

    // Find all unique Silos (Contexts)
    let silos = [...new Set(data.map(i => val(i, 'Context')))].filter(Boolean);
    
    // Sort to push "Completed/Foundation" silos to the right, active to the left
    silos.sort((a, b) => {
        if(a.includes('Completed') || a.includes('Foundation')) return 1;
        if(b.includes('Completed') || b.includes('Foundation')) return -1;
        return a.localeCompare(b);
    });

    if(silos.length === 0) {
        container.innerHTML = "<div class='text-gray-400 p-10'>No silos defined yet. Add a mini-goal!</div>";
        return;
    }

    silos.forEach(siloName => {
        const items = data.filter(i => val(i, 'Context') === siloName);
        
        // Calculate Progress
        const total = items.length;
        const liveCount = items.filter(i => String(val(i, 'Status')).toLowerCase().includes('live') || String(val(i, 'Status')).toLowerCase().includes('done')).length;
        const progressPct = total > 0 ? Math.round((liveCount / total) * 100) : 0;

        const col = document.createElement('div');
        col.className = "flex flex-col bg-slate-200/50 rounded-xl border border-slate-300 shadow-sm w-80 shrink-0 h-full overflow-hidden";
        
        // Silo Header
        col.innerHTML = `
            <div class="p-4 border-b border-slate-300 bg-slate-200 shrink-0">
                <h3 class="font-black text-slate-800 text-sm uppercase tracking-wide truncate" title="${siloName}">${siloName}</h3>
                <div class="flex items-center gap-2 mt-2">
                    <div class="w-full bg-slate-300 rounded-full h-1.5 overflow-hidden">
                        <div class="bg-indigo-500 h-1.5 rounded-full" style="width: ${progressPct}%"></div>
                    </div>
                    <span class="text-[9px] font-bold text-slate-500">${progressPct}%</span>
                </div>
            </div>
            <div class="kanban-col p-3 space-y-3 custom-scroll flex-1"></div>
        `;
        
        const cardContainer = col.querySelector('.kanban-col');

        // Draw Cards (Mini-Goals)
        items.forEach(item => {
            const id = val(item, 'ID');
            const statusRaw = String(val(item, 'Status')).toLowerCase();
            let stateClass = "card-pending";
            let dotColor = "bg-gray-400";
            let statusText = "Pending";

            if(statusRaw.includes('live') || statusRaw.includes('done')) {
                stateClass = "card-live";
                dotColor = "bg-green-500";
                statusText = "Completed";
            } else if (statusRaw.includes('progress') || statusRaw.includes('doing') || statusRaw.includes('staging')) {
                stateClass = "card-progress";
                dotColor = "bg-blue-500";
                statusText = "In Progress";
            }

            const card = document.createElement('div');
            card.className = `p-4 rounded-lg border cursor-pointer hover:-translate-y-0.5 transition transform ${stateClass}`;
            card.onclick = () => openTicket(id);

            card.innerHTML = `
                <div class="flex justify-between items-start mb-2">
                    <div class="flex items-center gap-1.5 bg-white/80 px-2 py-0.5 rounded border border-gray-200/50">
                        <span class="w-1.5 h-1.5 rounded-full ${dotColor}"></span>
                        <span class="text-[8px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest text-gray-600">${statusText}</span>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <h4 class="font-bold text-sm text-gray-900 leading-snug mb-1">${val(item, 'Title')}</h4>
                <p class="text-[10px] text-gray-500 line-clamp-2">${val(item, 'Description')}</p>
            `;
            cardContainer.appendChild(card);
        });

        container.appendChild(col);
    });
}

// --- MODAL & TASK LOGIC ---
async function openTicket(id) {
    currentTicketId = id; 
    document.getElementById('ticket-modal').classList.remove('hidden'); 
    document.body.classList.add('modal-active');
    
    document.getElementById('t-title').innerText = "Loading..."; 
    document.getElementById('t-history').innerHTML = '<div class="text-center text-gray-400 text-xs py-4 animate-pulse">Fetching tasks...</div>';
    
    try {
        const res = await fetch(`${SCRIPT_URL}?req=get_ticket&id=${id}`); 
        const data = await res.json();
        
        if(data.status === 'success') {
            const t = data.ticket; 
            document.getElementById('t-title').innerText = val(t, 'Title'); 
            document.getElementById('t-desc').innerText = val(t, 'Description') || "No definition provided."; 
            document.getElementById('t-silo').innerText = val(t, 'Context') || "Unassigned Silo";
            
            const currentStatus = val(t, 'Status').toLowerCase();
            const badge = document.getElementById('t-status-badge');
            if(currentStatus.includes('live')) { badge.innerText = "COMPLETED"; badge.className = "text-[10px] font-bold uppercase tracking-wide px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-white bg-green-500"; }
            else if(currentStatus.includes('progress') || currentStatus.includes('staging')) { badge.innerText = "IN PROGRESS"; badge.className = "text-[10px] font-bold uppercase tracking-wide px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-white bg-blue-500"; }
            else { badge.innerText = "PENDING"; badge.className = "text-[10px] font-bold uppercase tracking-wide px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-gray-600 bg-gray-200"; }

            // Sync Dropdown
            document.getElementById('t-new-status').value = "";

            const histDiv = document.getElementById('t-history'); 
            histDiv.innerHTML = "";
            
            if(!data.history || data.history.length === 0) {
                histDiv.innerHTML = '<div class="text-center text-gray-400 italic text-xs py-4 bg-gray-50 rounded border border-dashed">No tasks or updates logged yet.</div>';
            } else {
                data.history.forEach(act => {
                    const d = new Date(val(act, 'Timestamp')).toLocaleDateString(); 
                    const row = document.createElement('div'); 
                    row.className = "flex gap-3 text-xs bg-white p-3 rounded-lg border border-gray-200 shadow-sm";
                    
                    const isStatusChange = val(act, 'Type') === 'Status Update';
                    const icon = isStatusChange ? '🔄' : '✅';
                    
                    row.innerHTML = `
                        <div class="text-lg pt-1 opacity-80">${icon}</div>
                        <div class="flex-1">
                            <p class="font-medium text-gray-800 text-sm">${val(act, 'Details')}</p>
                            <div class="mt-1 text-[9px] font-bold text-gray-400 uppercase tracking-widest">
                                Logged by ${val(act, 'User')} • ${d}
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    `;
                    histDiv.appendChild(row);
                });
            }
        }
    } catch(e) { alert("Error: " + e.message); closeTicket(); }
}

function closeTicket() { document.getElementById('ticket-modal').classList.add('hidden'); document.body.classList.remove('modal-active'); }

async function postUpdate() {
    const msg = document.getElementById('t-comment').value; 
    const newStatus = document.getElementById('t-new-status').value;
    
    if(!msg && !newStatus) return;
    
    const type = newStatus ? "Status Update" : "Task Completed"; 
    const txt = newStatus && msg ? `${msg} (Moved to ${newStatus})` : (newStatus ? `Status advanced to ${newStatus}` : msg);
    
    document.getElementById('t-comment').value = "Saving...";
    document.getElementById('t-comment').disabled = true;

    try { 
        await fetch(`${SCRIPT_URL}?req=add_action&id=${currentTicketId}&user=${user}&type=${type}&msg=${encodeURIComponent(txt)}&new_status=${newStatus}`); 
        document.getElementById('t-comment').value = ""; 
        document.getElementById('t-comment').disabled = false;
        document.getElementById('t-new-status').value = ""; 
        
        // Soft update local data so we don't have to reload entire board immediately if just adding a task
        if(newStatus) { 
            const item = allRoadmapData.find(i => val(i,'ID') === currentTicketId); 
            if(item) item.Status = newStatus; 
            renderSilos(allRoadmapData); 
        } 
        openTicket(currentTicketId); 
    } catch(e) { 
        alert("Post failed"); 
        document.getElementById('t-comment').disabled = false;
    }
}

async function submitItem() {
    const title = document.getElementById('inp-title').value; 
    const desc = document.getElementById('inp-desc').value; 
    const ctx = document.getElementById('inp-ctx').value || "General";
    const btn = document.getElementById('btn-submit');
    
    if(!title) { alert("Title Required"); return; } 
    btn.disabled = true;
    btn.innerText = "CREATING...";

    try { 
        const res = await fetch(`${SCRIPT_URL}?req=add_roadmap&user=${user}&title=${encodeURIComponent(title)}&desc=${encodeURIComponent(desc)}&prio=Med&cat=Feature&target=APP&source=Internal&context=${encodeURIComponent(ctx)}`); 
        const data = await res.json(); 
        if(data.status === 'success') { 
            toggleForm(); 
            document.getElementById('inp-title').value = ""; 
            document.getElementById('inp-desc').value = ""; 
            loadData(); 
        } 
    } catch(e) { 
        alert("Error"); 
    } finally { 
        btn.disabled = false; 
        btn.innerText = "CREATE GOAL";
    }
}
</script>
</body>
</html>

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
    <title>SignOS Secure Login</title>
    <script src="https://cdn.tailwindcss.com"></script>
    <style>
        .key-btn { 
            transition: all 0.1s; 
            user-select: none; 
            touch-action: manipulation;
        }
        .key-btn:active { transform: scale(0.95); background-color: #e5e7eb; }
        .shake { animation: shake 0.5s; }
        @keyframes shake {
            0% { transform: translateX(0); }
            25% { transform: translateX(-5px); }
            50% { transform: translateX(5px); }
            75% { transform: translateX(-5px); }
            100% { transform: translateX(0); }
        }
    </style>

<body class="bg-gray-100 min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center p-4 font-sans">

    <div class="max-w-sm w-full bg-white rounded-xl shadow-2xl overflow-hidden border border-gray-200" id="login-card">
        
        <!-- HEADER (Standard SignOS Header) -->
        <div class="bg-gray-900 px-6 py-6 text-center">
            <h1 class="text-2xl font-black text-white tracking-tight">SignOS ERP</h1>
            <p class="text-gray-400 text-[10px] mt-1 uppercase tracking-widest">Secure Access Gateway</p>
        </div>

        <!-- KEYPAD SECTION -->
        <div class="p-6">
            
            <!-- PIN DISPLAY -->
            <div class="mb-6 relative">
                <div class="h-12 bg-gray-50 rounded border border-gray-200 flex items-center justify-center">
                    <span id="pin-display" class="text-2xl text-gray-800 font-mono tracking-[0.5em] h-8"></span>
                </div>
                <div class="absolute inset-0 flex items-center justify-center pointer-events-none opacity-0" id="loading-overlay">
                    <svg class="animate-spin h-6 w-6 text-blue-600" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><circle class="opacity-25" cx="12" cy="12" r="10" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="4"></circle><path class="opacity-75" fill="currentColor" d="M4 12a8 8 0 018-8V0C5.373 0 0 5.373 0 12h4zm2 5.291A7.962 7.962 0 014 12H0c0 3.042 1.135 5.824 3 7.938l3-2.647z"></path></svg>
                </div>
            </div>

            <!-- KEYS -->
            <div class="grid grid-cols-3 gap-3 mb-4">
                <button onclick="press(1)" class="key-btn h-14 bg-white border border-gray-200 rounded-lg text-xl font-bold text-gray-700 hover:bg-gray-50 hover:border-gray-300 shadow-sm">1</button>
                <button onclick="press(2)" class="key-btn h-14 bg-white border border-gray-200 rounded-lg text-xl font-bold text-gray-700 hover:bg-gray-50 hover:border-gray-300 shadow-sm">2</button>
                <button onclick="press(3)" class="key-btn h-14 bg-white border border-gray-200 rounded-lg text-xl font-bold text-gray-700 hover:bg-gray-50 hover:border-gray-300 shadow-sm">3</button>
                
                <button onclick="press(4)" class="key-btn h-14 bg-white border border-gray-200 rounded-lg text-xl font-bold text-gray-700 hover:bg-gray-50 hover:border-gray-300 shadow-sm">4</button>
                <button onclick="press(5)" class="key-btn h-14 bg-white border border-gray-200 rounded-lg text-xl font-bold text-gray-700 hover:bg-gray-50 hover:border-gray-300 shadow-sm">5</button>
                <button onclick="press(6)" class="key-btn h-14 bg-white border border-gray-200 rounded-lg text-xl font-bold text-gray-700 hover:bg-gray-50 hover:border-gray-300 shadow-sm">6</button>
                
                <button onclick="press(7)" class="key-btn h-14 bg-white border border-gray-200 rounded-lg text-xl font-bold text-gray-700 hover:bg-gray-50 hover:border-gray-300 shadow-sm">7</button>
                <button onclick="press(8)" class="key-btn h-14 bg-white border border-gray-200 rounded-lg text-xl font-bold text-gray-700 hover:bg-gray-50 hover:border-gray-300 shadow-sm">8</button>
                <button onclick="press(9)" class="key-btn h-14 bg-white border border-gray-200 rounded-lg text-xl font-bold text-gray-700 hover:bg-gray-50 hover:border-gray-300 shadow-sm">9</button>
                
                <button onclick="clearPin()" class="key-btn h-14 bg-red-50 border border-red-100 rounded-lg text-sm font-bold text-red-500 hover:bg-red-100">CLR</button>
                <button onclick="press(0)" class="key-btn h-14 bg-white border border-gray-200 rounded-lg text-xl font-bold text-gray-700 hover:bg-gray-50 hover:border-gray-300 shadow-sm">0</button>
                <button onclick="submitPin()" class="key-btn h-14 bg-blue-600 rounded-lg text-sm font-bold text-white hover:bg-blue-700 shadow-md shadow-blue-200" id="btn-go">ENTER</button>
            </div>

            <!-- STATUS MSG -->
            <div id="status-msg" class="text-center text-[10px] font-bold text-gray-400 h-4 uppercase tracking-wide">
                Authorized Personnel Only
            </div>
        </div>
        
        <!-- FOOTER -->
        <div class="bg-gray-50 border-t border-gray-100 p-3 text-center">
            <p class="text-[9px] text-gray-400">v3.2 | System Status: <span class="text-green-500 font-bold">ONLINE</span></p>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        // *** VERIFY THIS URL MATCHES YOUR DEPLOYMENT ***
        const SCRIPT_URL = "https://script.google.com/macros/s/AKfycbw57SS-MiuDv0ZUnRaf4jRNiSfpQJMknY82467HvZtzMKgMNZcLtTy0Vb-amX7TaY8svg/exec";
        
        let currentPin = "";

        function press(num) {
            if (currentPin.length < 6) {
                currentPin += num;
                updateDisplay();
            }
        }

        function clearPin() {
            currentPin = "";
            updateDisplay();
            resetStatus();
        }

        function updateDisplay() {
            const display = document.getElementById("pin-display");
            display.innerText = "•".repeat(currentPin.length);
        }

        function resetStatus() {
            const msg = document.getElementById("status-msg");
            msg.innerText = "AUTHORIZED PERSONNEL ONLY";
            msg.className = "text-center text-[10px] font-bold text-gray-400 h-4 uppercase tracking-wide";
        }

        async function submitPin() {
            if (currentPin.length < 6) return;

            const msg = document.getElementById("status-msg");
            const btn = document.getElementById("btn-go");
            const card = document.getElementById("login-card");
            const load = document.getElementById("loading-overlay");

            // UI Loading State
            msg.innerText = "AUTHENTICATING...";
            msg.className = "text-center text-[10px] font-bold text-blue-500 h-4 uppercase tracking-wide animate-pulse";
            btn.disabled = true;
            btn.classList.add("opacity-50");
            load.classList.remove("opacity-0");

            try {
                // Call API with ?req=auth
                const response = await fetch(`${SCRIPT_URL}?req=auth&pin=${currentPin}`);
                const data = await response.json();

                if (data.status === "success") {
                    // SUCCESS
                    msg.innerText = `WELCOME, ${data.name.toUpperCase()}`;
                    msg.className = "text-center text-[10px] font-bold text-green-600 h-4 uppercase tracking-wide";
                    
                    // Route Logic
                    let mode = "sales"; // Default
                    if (data.role === "PROD") mode = "production";
                    if (data.role === "ADMIN") mode = "admin";

                    // Store Session
                    sessionStorage.setItem("signos_user", data.name);
                    sessionStorage.setItem("signos_role", data.role);

                    // Redirect
                    setTimeout(() => {
                        window.location.href = `index.html?mode=${mode}`;
                    }, 800);

                } else {
                    // FAIL
                    throw new Error("Invalid PIN");
                }

            } catch (e) {
                // ERROR UI
                msg.innerText = "ACCESS DENIED";
                msg.className = "text-center text-[10px] font-bold text-red-500 h-4 uppercase tracking-wide";
                
                // Shake Animation
                card.classList.add("shake");
                setTimeout(() => card.classList.remove("shake"), 500);
                
                currentPin = "";
                updateDisplay();
                btn.disabled = false;
                btn.classList.remove("opacity-50");
                load.classList.add("opacity-0");
            }
        }
    </script>
</body>
</html>

FILE: Legacy_YardSign_Calculator.html

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
    <title>Yard Sign Calculator v21.8</title>
    <script src="https://cdn.tailwindcss.com"></script>
    <script src="signos-core.js"></script>
    <style>
        /* CORE STYLES */
        .tab-btn.active { border-bottom: 2px solid #2563eb; color: #2563eb; background: #eff6ff; }
        .tab-content { display: none; }
        .tab-content.active { display: block; }
        input[type=number]::-webkit-inner-spin-button { -webkit-appearance: none; margin: 0; }
        
        .toggle-checkbox:checked { right: 0; border-color: #68D391; }
        .toggle-checkbox:checked + .toggle-label { background-color: #68D391; }
        
        /* VIEW MODE LOGIC */
        .mode-sales #btn-cost, .mode-sales #btn-vend { display: none !important; }
        .mode-prod #btn-retail, .mode-prod #btn-vend { display: none !important; }
        .mode-prod .prod-hidden { display: none !important; }
        .mode-prod .prod-width { width: 100% !important; text-align: right; }
        
        .warn-pulse { animation: pulse-red 2s infinite; }

    </style>

                        </thead>
                        <tbody class="font-bold text-gray-700" id="discount-rows"></tbody>

                <div class="flex justify-between text-purple-700" id="row-design"><span>Design Fee (<span id="lbl-files-d">1</span> Files):</span><span id="ret-design" class="font-bold">$0.00</span></div>
            </div>

                <div class="flex justify-between items-center"><span>Ink:</span><span class="prod-width text-right text-[10px] bg-yellow-200 px-1 rounded font-bold" id="lbl-ink-sqft">0 ft²</span><span id="cost-ink" class="font-bold prod-hidden">$0.00</span></div>
                <div class="flex justify-between items-center"><span>Stake:</span><span class="prod-width text-right font-bold"><span id="lbl-qty-stake">0</span> units</span><span id="cost-hard" class="font-bold prod-hidden">$0.00</span></div>

                <div class="border-t border-yellow-200 my-1 pt-1"></div>
                <h4 class="font-bold text-yellow-800 uppercase text-[10px] mb-1">Production Time</h4>
                <div class="flex justify-between items-center text-purple-800" id="row-cost-design"><span class="w-1/3">Design:</span><span id="time-design" class="w-1/3 text-right text-[10px] bg-purple-100 rounded px-1 prod-width">0m</span><span id="cost-design" class="w-1/3 text-right font-bold prod-hidden">$0.00</span></div>
                <div class="flex justify-between items-center mt-1"><span class="w-1/3">Setup:</span><span id="time-setup" class="w-1/3 text-right text-[10px] bg-yellow-100 rounded px-1 prod-width">0m</span><span id="cost-setup-internal" class="w-1/3 text-right font-bold prod-hidden">$0.00</span></div>
                <div class="flex justify-between items-center mt-1"><span class="w-1/3">Run:</span><span id="time-machine" class="w-1/3 text-right text-[10px] bg-yellow-100 rounded px-1 prod-width">0m</span><span id="cost-machine" class="w-1/3 text-right font-bold prod-hidden">$0.00</span></div>
                <div class="flex justify-between items-center mt-1"><span class="w-1/3">Labor:</span><span id="time-op" class="w-1/3 text-right text-[10px] bg-yellow-100 rounded px-1 prod-width">0m</span><span id="cost-op" class="w-1/3 text-right font-bold prod-hidden">$0.00</span></div>

                <div class="border-t border-yellow-200 my-2 pt-1"></div>
                <div class="flex justify-between items-center text-gray-400"><span class="w-1/2 text-[10px] uppercase">Risk Buffer:</span><span id="risk-pct" class="w-1/4 text-right text-[10px] bg-gray-100 rounded px-1 font-bold prod-width">0%</span><span id="cost-waste" class="w-1/4 text-right font-bold prod-hidden text-[10px]">$0.00</span></div>

                <div class="border-t-2 border-yellow-300 my-2 prod-hidden"></div>

        <div id="tab-vend" class="tab-content bg-indigo-50 p-6">
            <div class="space-y-2 text-xs text-gray-700">
                <div class="flex justify-between"><span>Vendor Print:</span> <span id="vend-print" class="font-bold">$0.00</span></div>

<script>
    const TAB_NAME = "PROD_Yard_Signs";
    let backend = {};
    let currentUser = { name: "Guest", role: "VIEW", mode: "sales" };

    function initSession() {
        const params = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
        const urlMode = params.get('mode'); 
        const storeUser = sessionStorage.getItem('signos_user');
        const storeRole = sessionStorage.getItem('signos_role');

        if(storeUser) currentUser.name = storeUser;
        if(storeRole) currentUser.role = storeRole;

        // Strict Role Check via Core Logic or manual override here?
        // Let's rely on sessionStorage + simple view switch
        if (currentUser.role === 'ADMIN') currentUser.mode = urlMode || 'dev';
        else if (currentUser.role === 'PROD') currentUser.mode = 'production';
        else currentUser.mode = 'sales';

        document.getElementById('auth-user').innerText = currentUser.name;
        document.getElementById('auth-role').innerText = currentUser.role;

        const body = document.body;
        body.classList.remove('mode-sales', 'mode-prod', 'mode-admin');
        
        if(currentUser.mode === 'sales') { body.classList.add('mode-sales'); switchTab('retail'); }
        else if (currentUser.mode === 'production') { body.classList.add('mode-prod'); switchTab('cost'); }
        else { body.classList.add('mode-admin'); }
    }

    function switchTab(id) { document.querySelectorAll('.tab-content').forEach(el => el.classList.remove('active')); document.querySelectorAll('.tab-btn').forEach(el => el.classList.remove('active')); document.getElementById('tab-'+id).classList.add('active'); document.getElementById('btn-'+id).classList.add('active'); }
    function toggleDiscounts() { document.getElementById('discount-table').classList.toggle('hidden'); }

    function validateInputs() {
        const qty = document.getElementById('qty');
        const files = document.getElementById('files');
        if(parseFloat(qty.value) < 1) qty.value = 1;
        if(parseFloat(files.value) < 1) files.value = 1;
    }

    window.onload = async function() {
        initSession();
        const statusText = document.getElementById("status-text");
        const statusDot = document.getElementById("status-dot");
        const vDisplay = document.getElementById("version-display");
        
        try {
            // TELEMETRY: Pass IP and User params
            const response = await fetch(`${SCRIPT_URL}?tab=${TAB_NAME}&ip=${clientIP}&user=${currentUser.name}&role=${currentUser.role}&req=view_module`);
            const data = await response.json();
            if (data.error) throw new Error(data.error);
            backend = data;

            // Kill Switch
            const isLive = (backend.Is_Live === undefined) ? true : (backend.Is_Live === true || backend.Is_Live === "TRUE");
            if (!isLive && currentUser.role !== 'ADMIN') {
                document.getElementById('main-card').innerHTML = `<div class="p-10 text-center"><h1 class="text-xl font-black text-gray-400">MODULE OFFLINE</h1><button onclick="goBack()" class="mt-6 bg-blue-600 text-white px-4 py-2 rounded font-bold text-xs">Return to Menu</button></div>`;
                return;
            }

            // UI Status
            const isDev = currentUser.mode === 'dev';
            statusText.innerText = isDev ? "DEV MODE" : "ONLINE";
            statusText.className = isDev ? "font-bold text-orange-500" : "font-bold text-green-500";
            statusDot.className = isDev ? "w-2 h-2 rounded-full bg-orange-500" : "w-2 h-2 rounded-full bg-green-500";
            statusDot.classList.remove("animate-pulse");

            const ver = isDev ? (backend.Sys_Version_Dev || 'v0.0') : (backend.Sys_Version_Live || 'v0.0');
            vDisplay.innerText = isDev ? `(Beta ${ver})` : `Live ${ver}`;
            vDisplay.classList.remove('hidden');

            if(backend.Item_Name) document.getElementById("product-label").innerText = backend.Item_Name;
            calculate();

        } catch (e) {
            statusText.innerText = "OFFLINE";
            statusText.className = "font-bold text-red-500";
            document.getElementById("error-msg").innerText = e.message;
            document.getElementById("error-msg").classList.remove("hidden");
        }
    };

    function calculate() {
        if (!backend.Retail_Price_Sign_SS) return;
        validateInputs();

        const qty = parseFloat(document.getElementById('qty').value) || 1;
        const sides = parseInt(document.getElementById('sides').value);
        const numDesigns = parseFloat(document.getElementById('files').value) || 1;
        const hasStakes = document.getElementById('stakes').checked;
        const incDesign = document.getElementById('inc-design').checked;
        const chargeSetupPerFile = document.getElementById('inc-setup-per-file').checked;

        // --- 1. RETAIL PRICING ---
        const defaultBase = parseFloat(backend.Retail_Price_Sign_SS || 15.00);
        const adderDS = parseFloat(backend.Retail_Price_Sign_DS || 3.00);
        const stakePrice = parseFloat(backend.Retail_Price_Stake || 2.50);

        let baseSignPrice = defaultBase;
        let i = 1;
        const tiers = [];
        while(backend[`Tier_${i}_Qty`]) {
            const tQty = parseFloat(backend[`Tier_${i}_Qty`]);
            const tPrice = parseFloat(backend[`Tier_${i}_Price`] || 0);
            tiers.push({ q: tQty, p: tPrice });
            if (qty >= tQty) { baseSignPrice = tPrice; }
            i++;
        }

        let isCustom = (baseSignPrice === 0);
        let unitTotal = baseSignPrice;
        if (sides === 2) unitTotal += adderDS;
        if (hasStakes) unitTotal += stakePrice;

        let totalSignAndStake = unitTotal * qty;
        const feeSetupRate = parseFloat(backend.Retail_Fee_Setup || 15.00);
        const totalSetupPrice = chargeSetupPerFile ? (feeSetupRate * numDesigns) : feeSetupRate;
        const feeDesignRate = parseFloat(backend.Retail_Fee_Design || 45.00);
        const totalDesignPrice = incDesign ? (feeDesignRate * numDesigns) : 0;

        let quoteTotal = totalSignAndStake + totalSetupPrice + totalDesignPrice;
        const minOrder = parseFloat(backend.Retail_Min_Order || 75);
        if (quoteTotal < minOrder) { quoteTotal = minOrder; document.getElementById('min-badge').classList.remove('hidden'); } 
        else { document.getElementById('min-badge').classList.add('hidden'); }

        const fmt = (n) => "$" + n.toFixed(2);
        const pct = (n) => (n * 100).toFixed(1) + "%";
        const fmtTime = (h) => { const hrs = Math.floor(h); const mins = Math.round((h - hrs) * 60); return hrs > 0 ? `${hrs}h ${mins}m` : `${mins}m`; };

        let rowsHtml = "";
        tiers.forEach(tier => {
            if(tier.p === 0) return;
            let rowBase = tier.p + (sides===2 ? adderDS : 0) + (hasStakes ? stakePrice : 0);
            rowsHtml += `<tr><td class="pr-4 py-1 text-gray-500">${tier.q}+</td><td class="pr-4 py-1 text-gray-400">$${tier.p.toFixed(2)}</td><td class="py-1 text-blue-600 font-bold">$${rowBase.toFixed(2)}</td></tr>`;
        });
        document.getElementById('discount-rows').innerHTML = rowsHtml;

        document.getElementById('unit-price').innerText = isCustom ? "CUSTOM" : fmt(unitTotal);
        document.getElementById('total-price').innerText = isCustom ? "CONTACT US" : fmt(quoteTotal);
        document.getElementById('lbl-qty').innerText = qty;
        document.getElementById('ret-print').innerText = fmt(baseSignPrice * qty + (sides===2 ? adderDS*qty : 0));
        document.getElementById('ret-stakes').innerText = fmt(hasStakes ? stakePrice*qty : 0);
        document.getElementById('ret-setup').innerText = fmt(totalSetupPrice);
        document.getElementById('lbl-setup-type').innerText = chargeSetupPerFile ? `${numDesigns} Files` : "Flat";
        document.getElementById('ret-design').innerText = fmt(totalDesignPrice);
        document.getElementById('lbl-files-d').innerText = numDesigns;
        if(incDesign) document.getElementById('row-design').classList.remove('hidden'); else document.getElementById('row-design').classList.add('hidden');

        // --- 2. IN-HOUSE ---
        const bulkTrigger = parseFloat(backend.Bulk_Qty_Trigger || 1100);
        let blankCost = parseFloat(backend.Cost_Blank_Standard || 0.91);
        if (qty >= bulkTrigger) blankCost = parseFloat(backend.Cost_Blank_Bulk || 0.79);
        const wasteFactor = parseFloat(backend.Waste_Factor || 1.05);
        const totalMatCost = (blankCost * wasteFactor) * qty;
        const areaPerSign = (24*18)/144;
        const totalPrintArea = areaPerSign * sides * qty;
        const inkRate = parseFloat(backend.Cost_Ink_Base || 0.16);
        const totalInkCost = totalPrintArea * inkRate;
        const unitStakeCost = hasStakes ? parseFloat(backend.Cost_Stake || 0.93) : 0;
        const totalStakeCost = unitStakeCost * qty;

        let designHrs = incDesign ? ((parseFloat(backend.Time_Design_Per_File || 15) * numDesigns) / 60) : 0;
        let totalDesignCost = designHrs * parseFloat(backend.Rate_Design_Cost || 35);
        if(incDesign) document.getElementById('row-cost-design').classList.remove('hidden'); else document.getElementById('row-cost-design').classList.add('hidden');

        const setupHrs = (parseFloat(backend.Time_Setup_Base || 15) + (parseFloat(backend.Time_Setup_Adder || 2) * numDesigns)) / 60;
        const rateOp = parseFloat(backend.Rate_Operator || 25);
        const setupCost = setupHrs * rateOp;

        const speed = parseFloat(backend.Machine_Speed_LF_Hr || 25);
        const printerBedCap = parseFloat(backend.Printer_Bed_Capacity || 3);
        const rateMachine = parseFloat(backend.Rate_Machine || 45);
        const linearFtPerSign = (2.0 / printerBedCap);
        const totalRunTimeHrs = ((linearFtPerSign / speed) * (sides === 2 ? 2 : 1)) * qty;
        const runCost = totalRunTimeHrs * rateMachine;
        const opRunCost = totalRunTimeHrs * rateOp;

        const riskPct = (sides === 2 ? parseFloat(backend.Rework_Risk_DS || 0.05) : 0) + ((numDesigns > 1) ? (numDesigns-1)*parseFloat(backend.Rework_Risk_File || 0.02) : 0);
        const totalRiskCost = (qty * riskPct) * (blankCost + inkRate + rateMachine + rateOp);
        
        const totalInternalCost = totalMatCost + totalInkCost + totalStakeCost + totalDesignCost + setupCost + runCost + opRunCost;

        document.getElementById('lbl-qty-mat').innerText = qty;
        document.getElementById('cost-mat').innerText = fmt(totalMatCost);
        document.getElementById('lbl-ink-sqft').innerText = totalPrintArea.toFixed(1) + " ft²";
        document.getElementById('cost-ink').innerText = fmt(totalInkCost);
        document.getElementById('lbl-qty-stake').innerText = hasStakes ? qty : 0;
        document.getElementById('cost-hard').innerText = fmt(totalStakeCost);
        
        document.getElementById('time-design').innerText = fmtTime(designHrs);
        document.getElementById('cost-design').innerText = fmt(totalDesignCost);
        document.getElementById('time-setup').innerText = fmtTime(setupHrs);
        document.getElementById('cost-setup-internal').innerText = fmt(setupCost);
        document.getElementById('time-machine').innerText = fmtTime(totalRunTimeHrs);
        document.getElementById('cost-machine').innerText = fmt(runCost);
        document.getElementById('time-op').innerText = fmtTime(totalRunTimeHrs);
        document.getElementById('cost-op').innerText = fmt(opRunCost);
        document.getElementById('risk-pct').innerText = (riskPct * 100).toFixed(1) + "% Buffer";
        document.getElementById('cost-waste').innerText = fmt(totalRiskCost);
        document.getElementById('cost-total').innerText = fmt(totalInternalCost);

        const profitIn = quoteTotal - totalInternalCost;
        document.getElementById('profit-inhouse').innerText = fmt(profitIn);
        if(!isCustom && quoteTotal>0) document.getElementById('margin-inhouse').innerText = pct(profitIn / quoteTotal);

        // --- 3. VENDED ---
        const sheetsNeeded = Math.ceil(qty / 10);
        let sheetPrice = 44.00;
        if (sides === 1) sheetPrice = sheetsNeeded < 10 ? parseFloat(backend.Vend_SS_Sheet_Tier1 || 44) : parseFloat(backend.Vend_SS_Sheet_Tier2 || 33);
        else sheetPrice = sheetsNeeded < 10 ? parseFloat(backend.Vend_DS_Sheet_Tier1 || 55) : parseFloat(backend.Vend_DS_Sheet_Tier2 || 44);
        
        const vendPrintCost = sheetsNeeded * sheetPrice;
        const vendStakeCost = hasStakes ? (qty * parseFloat(backend.Vend_Stake_Cost || 1.38)) : 0;
        let vendShip = parseFloat(backend.Vend_Shipping_Base || 10);
        if (sheetsNeeded >= parseFloat(backend.Vend_Freight_Threshold || 58)) vendShip = parseFloat(backend.Vend_Freight_Flat || 199);
        const totalVendedCost = vendPrintCost + vendStakeCost + vendShip;

        document.getElementById('vend-print').innerText = fmt(vendPrintCost);
        document.getElementById('vend-stakes').innerText = fmt(vendStakeCost);
        document.getElementById('vend-ship').innerText = fmt(vendShip);
        document.getElementById('vend-total').innerText = fmt(totalVendedCost);
        const profitVend = quoteTotal - totalVendedCost;
        document.getElementById('profit-vend').innerText = fmt(profitVend);
        if(!isCustom && quoteTotal>0) document.getElementById('margin-vend').innerText = pct(profitVend / quoteTotal);

        // JOB DESC
        const sideTxt = sides === 1 ? "ONE" : "TWO";
        const stakeTxt = hasStakes ? "with 10\" x 24\" wire H-frame step stakes" : "NO Stakes";
        document.getElementById('job-desc').value = `(x${qty}) 24" x 18" 4mm Coroplast Signs with direct print latex ink on ${sideTxt} side(s) ${stakeTxt}.`;
    }
</script>
</body>
</html>

<script>
    const TAB_NAME = "PROD_Decals";
    let backend = {};
    let currentUser = { name: "Guest", role: "VIEW", mode: "sales" };

    function initSession() {
        const storeUser = sessionStorage.getItem('signos_user');
        const storeRole = sessionStorage.getItem('signos_role');
        const storeMode = sessionStorage.getItem('signos_mode');

        if(storeUser) currentUser.name = storeUser;
        if(storeRole) currentUser.role = storeRole;
        if(storeMode) currentUser.mode = storeMode;

        document.getElementById('auth-user').innerText = currentUser.name;
        document.getElementById('auth-role').innerText = currentUser.role;

        const body = document.body;
        body.classList.remove('mode-sales', 'mode-prod', 'mode-admin');
        
        if(currentUser.mode === 'sales') { body.classList.add('mode-sales'); switchTab('retail'); }
        else if (currentUser.mode === 'production') { body.classList.add('mode-prod'); switchTab('cost'); }
        else { body.classList.add('mode-admin'); }
    }

    function goBack() { window.location.href = `menu.html?mode=${currentUser.mode}`; }
    function switchTab(id) { document.querySelectorAll('.tab-content').forEach(el => el.classList.remove('active')); document.querySelectorAll('.tab-btn').forEach(el => el.classList.remove('active')); document.getElementById('tab-'+id).classList.add('active'); document.getElementById('btn-'+id).classList.add('active'); }
    function toggleDiscounts() { document.getElementById('discount-table').classList.toggle('hidden'); }
    function toggleOpt(id) { document.getElementById(id).classList.toggle('hidden'); }

    window.onload = async function() {
        initSession();
        const statusText = document.getElementById("status-text");
        const statusDot = document.getElementById("status-dot");
        const vDisplay = document.getElementById("version-display");

        try {
            // TELEMETRY
            const response = await fetch(`${SCRIPT_URL}?tab=${TAB_NAME}&ip=${clientIP}&user=${currentUser.name}&role=${currentUser.role}&req=view_module`);
            const data = await response.json();
            if (data.error) throw new Error(data.error);
            backend = data;

            // Kill Switch
            const isLive = (backend.Is_Live === undefined) ? true : (backend.Is_Live === true || backend.Is_Live === "TRUE");
            if (!isLive && currentUser.role !== 'ADMIN') {
                document.getElementById('main-card').innerHTML = `<div class="p-10 text-center"><h1 class="text-xl font-black text-gray-400">MODULE OFFLINE</h1><button onclick="goBack()" class="mt-6 bg-blue-600 text-white px-4 py-2 rounded font-bold text-xs">Return to Menu</button></div>`;
                return;
            }

            // UI
            const isDev = currentUser.mode === 'dev';
            statusText.innerText = isDev ? "DEV MODE" : "ONLINE";
            statusText.className = isDev ? "font-bold text-orange-500" : "font-bold text-green-500";
            statusDot.className = isDev ? "w-2 h-2 rounded-full bg-orange-500" : "w-2 h-2 rounded-full bg-green-500";
            statusDot.classList.remove("animate-pulse");

            const ver = isDev ? (backend.Sys_Version_Dev || 'v0.0') : (backend.Sys_Version_Live || 'v0.0');
            vDisplay.innerText = isDev ? `(Beta ${ver})` : `Live ${ver}`;
            vDisplay.classList.remove('hidden');

            if(backend.Item_Name) document.getElementById("product-label").innerText = backend.Item_Name;
            calculate();

        } catch (e) {
            statusText.innerText = "OFFLINE";
            statusText.className = "font-bold text-red-500";
            document.getElementById("error-msg").innerText = e.message;
            document.getElementById("error-msg").classList.remove("hidden");
        }
    };

    function calculate() {
        if (!backend.Item_Name) return;

        const w = parseFloat(document.getElementById('width').value) || 0;
        const h = parseFloat(document.getElementById('height').value) || 0;
        const qty = parseFloat(document.getElementById('qty').value) || 1;
        const mat = document.getElementById('material').value; // Cal vs Cast
        const cutType = document.getElementById('cut-type').value;
        const hasLam = document.getElementById('has-lam').checked;
        const incDesign = document.getElementById('inc-design').checked;
        const hasWeed = document.getElementById('has-weed').checked;
        const weedMode = document.querySelector('input[name="weed-mode"]:checked').value;

        const sqft = (w*h)/144;
        const totalSqFt = sqft * qty;
        const perimeterFt = ((w+h)*2/12) * qty;

        // --- 1. RETAIL ---
        const baseRate = mat === 'Cast' ? parseFloat(backend.Retail_Price_Cast_SqFt || 0) : parseFloat(backend.Retail_Price_Cal_SqFt || 0);
        
        let discPct = 0;
        let currentBestTier = 0;
        let i = 1;
        const tiers = [];
        while(backend[`Tier_${i}_Qty`]) {
            const tQty = parseFloat(backend[`Tier_${i}_Qty`]);
            const tDisc = parseFloat(backend[`Tier_${i}_Disc`] || 0);
            tiers.push({ q: tQty, d: tDisc });
            if (qty >= tQty) currentBestTier = tDisc;
            i++;
        }
        discPct = currentBestTier;

        const unitRate = baseRate * (1 - discPct);
        let retailPrint = unitRate * totalSqFt;
        const minPrice = parseFloat(backend.Retail_Min_Order || 0);
        if (retailPrint < minPrice) retailPrint = minPrice;

        let retailContour = 0;
        if (cutType === 'KissThru') retailContour = retailPrint * parseFloat(backend.Retail_Cut_Contour_Add || 0);

        let retailWeed = 0;
        if (hasWeed && weedMode === 'Complex') retailWeed = totalSqFt * parseFloat(backend.Retail_Weed_Complex || 0);

        let feeDesign = incDesign ? parseFloat(backend.Retail_Fee_Design || 0) : 0;
        let feeSetup = parseFloat(backend.Retail_Fee_Setup || 0);

        const totalQuote = retailPrint + retailContour + retailWeed + feeDesign + feeSetup;
        if (totalQuote < minPrice) { document.getElementById('min-badge').classList.remove('hidden'); }
        else { document.getElementById('min-badge').classList.add('hidden'); }

        // DISCOUNT TABLE RENDER
        let rowsHtml = "";
        tiers.forEach(tier => {
            const trRate = baseRate * (1 - tier.d);
            const trPrint = trRate * (sqft * tier.q);
            const trContour = cutType === 'KissThru' ? (trPrint * parseFloat(backend.Retail_Cut_Contour_Add || 0)) : 0;
            const trWeed = (hasWeed && weedMode === 'Complex') ? (sqft * tier.q * parseFloat(backend.Retail_Weed_Complex || 0)) : 0;
            const trTotalRaw = trPrint + trContour + trWeed + feeSetup + feeDesign;
            const trFinal = Math.max(trTotalRaw, minPrice);
            const trUnit = trFinal / tier.q;
            const discDisplay = tier.d > 0 ? `<span class="text-[9px] bg-green-100 text-green-700 px-1 rounded ml-1">-${(tier.d*100).toFixed(0)}%</span>` : "";
            rowsHtml += `<tr><td class="pr-4 py-1 text-gray-500">${tier.q}${discDisplay}</td><td class="pr-4 py-1 text-blue-600 font-bold">$${trUnit.toFixed(2)}</td><td class="py-1 text-green-600 font-bold">${(tier.d*100).toFixed(0)}% Off</td></tr>`;
        });
        document.getElementById('discount-rows').innerHTML = rowsHtml;

        // UI RETAIL
        const fmt = (n) => "$" + n.toFixed(2);
        const pct = (n) => (n * 100).toFixed(1) + "%";
        const fmtTime = (h) => { if(h<0.01) return "0m"; const hrs = Math.floor(h); const mins = Math.round((h-hrs)*60); return `${hrs}h ${mins}m`; };

        document.getElementById('unit-price').innerText = fmt(totalQuote/qty);
        document.getElementById('lbl-sqft').innerText = totalSqFt.toFixed(1);
        document.getElementById('ret-print').innerText = fmt(retailPrint);
        
        if (retailContour > 0) { document.getElementById('row-ret-contour').classList.remove('hidden'); document.getElementById('ret-contour').innerText = fmt(retailContour); } 
        else document.getElementById('row-ret-contour').classList.add('hidden');
        
        if (retailWeed > 0) { document.getElementById('row-ret-weed').classList.remove('hidden'); document.getElementById('ret-weed').innerText = fmt(retailWeed); } 
        else document.getElementById('row-ret-weed').classList.add('hidden');
        
        document.getElementById('ret-setup').innerText = fmt(feeSetup);
        if (feeDesign > 0) { document.getElementById('row-ret-design').classList.remove('hidden'); document.getElementById('ret-design').innerText = fmt(feeDesign); } 
        else document.getElementById('row-ret-design').classList.add('hidden');
        
        document.getElementById('total-price').innerText = fmt(totalQuote);

        // --- 2. IN-HOUSE COST ---
        const waste = parseFloat(backend.Waste_Factor || 1.20);
        const costVinylRaw = mat === 'Cast' ? parseFloat(backend.Cost_Vin_Cast || 0) : parseFloat(backend.Cost_Vin_Cal || 0);
        const costLamRaw = hasLam ? (mat === 'Cast' ? parseFloat(backend.Cost_Lam_Cast || 0) : parseFloat(backend.Cost_Lam_Cal || 0)) : 0;
        const costInkRaw = parseFloat(backend.Cost_Ink_Latex || 0);

        const costVinyl = totalSqFt * costVinylRaw * waste;
        const costLam = totalSqFt * costLamRaw * waste;
        const costInk = totalSqFt * costInkRaw;

        const rateOp = parseFloat(backend.Rate_Labor_Op || 25);
        const rateShop = parseFloat(backend.Rate_Labor_Shop || 20);
        const ratePrint = parseFloat(backend.Rate_Machine_Print || 15);
        const rateCut = parseFloat(backend.Rate_Machine_Cut || 5);

        const setupMins = parseFloat(backend.Time_Setup_Job || 20);
        const setupCost = (setupMins/60) * rateOp;

        const speedPrint = parseFloat(backend.Speed_Print_Roll || 150);
        const timePrint = totalSqFt / speedPrint;
        const costPrint = timePrint * (ratePrint + (rateOp * 0.1));

        let timeLam = 0, costLamRun = 0;
        if (hasLam) {
            const speedLam = parseFloat(backend.Speed_Lam_Roll || 300);
            timeLam = totalSqFt / speedLam;
            costLamRun = timeLam * rateShop;
        }

        let timeCut = 0, costCut = 0;
        let cutLabel = "Hand";
        if (cutType === 'Thru') {
            cutLabel = "Hand Thru";
            const timeHand = (perimeterFt * parseFloat(backend.Time_Cut_Hand || 0.25)) / 60;
            timeCut = timeHand;
            costCut = timeHand * rateShop;
        } else {
            cutLabel = "Kiss+Thru";
            const speedKiss = parseFloat(backend.Speed_Cut_Graphtec || 50); 
            const timeKiss = totalSqFt / speedKiss;
            const timeSheetCut = (perimeterFt * parseFloat(backend.Time_Cut_Hand || 0.25) * 0.5) / 60;
            timeCut = timeKiss + timeSheetCut;
            costCut = (timeKiss * rateCut) + (timeSheetCut * rateShop);
        }

        let timeWeed = 0, costWeed = 0;
        if (hasWeed) {
            const speedWeed = weedMode === 'Simple' ? parseFloat(backend.Time_Weed_Simple || 2.0) : parseFloat(backend.Time_Weed_Complex || 8.0);
            timeWeed = (totalSqFt * speedWeed) / 60;
            costWeed = timeWeed * rateShop;
        }

        const subtotal = costVinyl + costLam + costInk + setupCost + costPrint + costLamRun + costCut + costWeed + feeDesign;
        const riskCost = subtotal * (waste - 1);
        const totalInHouse = subtotal + riskCost;

        // UI COST
        document.getElementById('cost-mat-vinyl').innerText = fmt(costVinyl);
        document.getElementById('cost-mat-lam').innerText = fmt(costLam);
        document.getElementById('cost-mat-ink').innerText = fmt(costInk);
        document.getElementById('time-setup').innerText = fmtTime(setupMins/60);
        document.getElementById('cost-setup').innerText = fmt(setupCost);
        document.getElementById('time-print').innerText = fmtTime(timePrint);
        document.getElementById('cost-print').innerText = fmt(costPrint);
        document.getElementById('time-lam').innerText = fmtTime(timeLam);
        document.getElementById('cost-lam').innerText = fmt(costLamRun);
        document.getElementById('lbl-cut-type').innerText = cutLabel;
        document.getElementById('time-cut').innerText = fmtTime(timeCut);
        document.getElementById('cost-cut').innerText = fmt(costCut);
        
        if (costWeed > 0) { document.getElementById('row-cost-weed').classList.remove('hidden'); document.getElementById('time-weed').innerText = fmtTime(timeWeed); document.getElementById('cost-weed').innerText = fmt(costWeed); } 
        else document.getElementById('row-cost-weed').classList.add('hidden');
        
        document.getElementById('cost-waste').innerText = fmt(riskCost);
        document.getElementById('cost-total').innerText = fmt(totalInHouse);
        
        const profIn = totalQuote - totalInHouse;
        document.getElementById('profit-inhouse').innerText = fmt(profIn);
        if(totalQuote>0) document.getElementById('margin-inhouse').innerText = pct(profIn/totalQuote);

        // --- 3. VENDED (Signs365) ---
        const vendRate = mat === 'Cast' ? parseFloat(backend.S365_Decal_Cast_SqFt || 0) : parseFloat(backend.S365_Decal_Cal_SqFt || 0);
        const vendMin = parseFloat(backend.S365_Decal_Min || 0);
        let vendPrint = totalSqFt * vendRate;
        if (vendPrint < vendMin) vendPrint = vendMin;

        if (cutType === 'KissThru') vendPrint = vendPrint * (1 + parseFloat(backend.S365_Add_Contour || 0));

        let vendShip = parseFloat(backend.S365_Ship_Std || 10);
        const freightTrigger = parseFloat(backend.S365_Freight_Trigger || 1000);
        if (totalSqFt >= freightTrigger) vendShip = parseFloat(backend.S365_Ship_Freight || 199);

        const totalVended = vendPrint + vendShip;

        if (vendRate === 0) document.getElementById('vend-data-warn').classList.remove('hidden');
        else document.getElementById('vend-data-warn').classList.add('hidden');

        document.getElementById('vend-print').innerText = fmt(vendPrint);
        document.getElementById('vend-ship').innerText = fmt(vendShip);
        document.getElementById('vend-total').innerText = fmt(totalVended);
        const profVend = totalQuote - totalVended;
        document.getElementById('profit-vend').innerText = fmt(profVend);
        if(totalQuote>0) document.getElementById('margin-vend').innerText = pct(profVend/totalQuote);

        const profitWarn = document.getElementById('profit-warn');
        if (profIn < 0 && profVend < 0) { profitWarn.classList.remove('hidden'); profitWarn.classList.add('warn-pulse'); }
        else { profitWarn.classList.add('hidden'); profitWarn.classList.remove('warn-pulse'); }

        const desc = `(x${qty}) ${w}" x ${h}" Custom Decals. Material: ${mat === 'Cast' ? '3M Cast Air Release' : 'Standard Calendered'}. Cut: ${cutType}. ${hasLam ? 'Laminated.' : ''} ${hasWeed ? 'Weeding Included.' : ''}`;
        document.getElementById('job-desc').value = desc;
    }
</script>
</body>
</html>

                    <div><span class="block text-[10px] font-bold text-gray-400 uppercase mb-1">Target</span><span id="m-target" class="text-gray-600">---</span></div>

                    </div>

    <script>
        function toggleSidebar() {
            const sb = document.getElementById('sidebar');
            const bd = document.getElementById('sidebar-backdrop');
            
            const isClosed = sb.classList.contains('-translate-x-full');
            if (isClosed) {
                sb.classList.remove('-translate-x-full');
                bd.classList.remove('hidden');
                document.getElementById('filter-panel').classList.add('hidden');
            } else {
                closeSidebar();
            }
        }

        function closeSidebar() {
            document.getElementById('sidebar').classList.add('-translate-x-full');
            document.getElementById('sidebar-backdrop').classList.add('hidden');
        }

        function toggleFilters() {
            const fp = document.getElementById('filter-panel');
            fp.classList.toggle('hidden');
            closeSidebar();
        }

        // --- SMART BEHAVIOR: Auto-Close Menu on Selection ---
        document.getElementById('archive-list').addEventListener('click', (e) => {
            // If on mobile (screen < 768px) and user clicked an item
            if(window.innerWidth < 768 && e.target.closest('.archive-item')) {
                // Short timeout to allow the "Active" CSS state to flash briefly
                setTimeout(closeSidebar, 150);
            }
        });

        // --- NAME SYNC ---
        const targetNode = document.getElementById('current-file-name');
        const observer = new MutationObserver(() => {
            document.getElementById('mobile-file-name').innerText = targetNode.innerText;
        });
        if(targetNode) observer.observe(targetNode, { childList: true, subtree: true, characterData: true });
    </script>

</body>
</html>

FILE: Calculator_Wall.html

<!DOCTYPE html>

    <style>input[type=number]::-webkit-inner-spin-button { -webkit-appearance: none; margin: 0; } .panel-scroll::-webkit-scrollbar { width: 4px; } .panel-scroll::-webkit-scrollbar-track { background: #f8fafc; } .panel-scroll::-webkit-scrollbar-thumb { background: #cbd5e1; border-radius: 2px; }</style>

<body class="bg-gray-100 min-h-screen font-sans flex flex-col pb-10">
<div id="main-card" class="max-w-md mx-auto mt-6 w-[calc(100%-2rem)] sm:w-full bg-white shadow-lg overflow-hidden rounded-xl border border-gray-200">
    <div class="p-6 space-y-4">
        <div class="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4">
            <div><label class="block text-[10px] font-bold text-gray-500 uppercase mb-1">Fleet Qty</label><input type="number" id="qty" value="1" min="1" class="w-full border p-2 rounded font-bold text-gray-800 text-lg text-center bg-gray-50 focus:border-blue-500 outline-none" oninput="runCalc()"></div>
            <div>
                <label class="block text-[10px] font-bold text-gray-500 uppercase mb-1">Installation</label>
                <select id="install" class="w-full border p-2 rounded bg-white font-bold text-sm h-[46px] focus:border-blue-500 outline-none" onchange="runCalc()">
                    <option value="Yes" selected>Yes (Add Labor)</option>
                    <option value="No">No (Print Only)</option>
                </select>
            </div>
        </div>
        <div class="border-t border-gray-200 my-2"></div>
        <div>
            <div class="flex justify-between items-end mb-2">
                <label class="block text-[10px] font-black text-gray-600 uppercase tracking-widest">Wall & Window Sections</label>
                <button onclick="addPanel()" class="text-[10px] font-bold bg-blue-50 text-blue-600 border border-blue-200 px-2 py-1 rounded hover:bg-blue-600 hover:text-white transition">+ ADD SECTION</button>
            </div>
            <div id="panel-container" class="space-y-3 max-h-64 overflow-y-auto panel-scroll pr-1"></div>
        </div>
    </div>
    <div class="bg-blue-50 p-6 border-t border-blue-100 shadow-inner">
        <div class="flex justify-between items-end mb-2"><span class="text-[10px] font-black text-blue-800 uppercase tracking-widest">Unit Price</span><span id="ui-unit" class="text-2xl font-black text-blue-900 tracking-tight">$0.00</span></div>
        <div class="border-t border-blue-200/50 my-3"></div>
        <div class="space-y-1 text-xs text-blue-900/70 pt-1">
            <div class="flex justify-between"><span>Printed Graphics (<span id="lbl-sqft">0</span> sqft):</span><span id="ui-print" class="font-bold">$0.00</span></div>
            <div class="flex justify-between text-orange-700 hidden" id="row-install"><span>Installation Labor:</span><span id="ui-install" class="font-bold">$0.00</span></div>

<script>
let backendData = {};
let panels = [{ id: Date.now(), label: 'Main Wall', w: 120, h: 96, material: 'smooth', laminate: 'Matte' }];

function renderPanels() {
    const container = document.getElementById('panel-container'); container.innerHTML = '';
    panels.forEach((p, index) => {
        const isOnly = panels.length === 1;
        const isPerf = p.material.startsWith('perf');
        container.innerHTML += `
        <div class="flex flex-col gap-2 bg-white p-2 rounded shadow-sm border ${isPerf ? 'border-indigo-200 bg-indigo-50/30' : 'border-gray-200'}">
            <div class="flex items-end gap-2">
                <div class="flex-1">
                    <label class="block text-[8px] font-bold text-gray-400 uppercase mb-0.5">Name</label>
                    <input type="text" value="${p.label}" onchange="updatePanel(${p.id}, 'label', this.value)" class="w-full border-b border-gray-200 bg-transparent text-xs font-bold text-gray-700 outline-none focus:border-blue-500 pb-1">
                </div>
                <div class="w-16">
                    <label class="block text-[8px] font-bold text-gray-400 uppercase mb-0.5 text-center">W (in)</label>
                    <input type="number" value="${p.w}" oninput="updateDim(${p.id}, 'w', this.value)" class="w-full border p-1 rounded text-xs font-bold text-gray-700 outline-none text-center focus:border-blue-500 bg-gray-50">
                </div>
                <div class="w-16">
                    <label class="block text-[8px] font-bold text-gray-400 uppercase mb-0.5 text-center">H (in)</label>
                    <input type="number" value="${p.h}" oninput="updateDim(${p.id}, 'h', this.value)" class="w-full border p-1 rounded text-xs font-bold text-gray-700 outline-none text-center focus:border-blue-500 bg-gray-50">
                </div>
                ${!isOnly ? `<button onclick="removePanel(${p.id})" class="h-[26px] w-7 flex items-center justify-center bg-red-50 text-red-500 border border-red-100 rounded hover:bg-red-500 hover:text-white transition">X</button>` : `<div class="w-7"></div>`}
            </div>
            <div class="grid grid-cols-2 gap-2 border-t border-gray-100 pt-1.5 mt-1">
                <select onchange="updatePanel(${p.id}, 'material', this.value)" class="w-full border border-gray-200 p-1 rounded text-xs font-bold ${isPerf ? 'text-indigo-700 bg-indigo-50' : 'text-gray-600 bg-gray-50'} outline-none focus:border-blue-500">
                    <option value="smooth" ${p.material === 'smooth' ? 'selected' : ''}>Smooth (GF 226)</option>
                    <option value="textured" ${p.material === 'textured' ? 'selected' : ''}>Textured (3M IJ8624)</option>
                    <option value="perf6040" ${p.material === 'perf6040' ? 'selected' : ''}>Window Perf (60/40)</option>
                    <option value="perf7030" ${p.material === 'perf7030' ? 'selected' : ''}>Window Perf (70/30)</option>
                </select>
                <select onchange="updatePanel(${p.id}, 'laminate', this.value)" class="w-full border border-gray-200 p-1 rounded text-xs font-bold text-gray-600 bg-gray-50 outline-none focus:border-blue-500">
                     ${isPerf ? `
                     <option value="Optically Clear" ${p.laminate === 'Optically Clear' ? 'selected' : ''}>Optically Clear Lam</option>
                     <option value="Spray Lam" ${p.laminate === 'Spray Lam' ? 'selected' : ''}>Spray Lam</option>
                     <option value="No Lam" ${p.laminate === 'No Lam' ? 'selected' : ''}>No Lam</option>
                     ` : `
                     <option value="Matte" ${p.laminate === 'Matte' ? 'selected' : ''}>Standard Matte Lam</option>
                     <option value="Gloss" ${p.laminate === 'Gloss' ? 'selected' : ''}>Standard Gloss Lam</option>
                     `}
                </select>
            </div>
        </div>`;
    });
    runCalc();
}

function updatePanel(id, field, val) { 
    const p = panels.find(x => x.id === id); 
    if(p) { 
        p[field] = val; 
        if (field === 'material') {
            p.laminate = val.startsWith('perf') ? 'No Lam' : 'Matte'; // Smart Defaulting
        }
        renderPanels(); 
    } 
}

// FIX: Separate function for dimensions so it doesn't redraw the DOM and steal typing focus
function updateDim(id, field, val) { 
    const p = panels.find(x => x.id === id); 
    if(p) { p[field] = parseFloat(val) || 0; runCalc(); } 
}

function addPanel() { panels.push({ id: Date.now(), label: `Area ${panels.length + 1}`, w: 120, h: 96, material: 'smooth', laminate: 'Matte' }); renderPanels(); }
function removePanel(id) { panels = panels.filter(x => x.id !== id); renderPanels(); }

function runCalc() {
    if(!backendData.Retail_Min_Order) return;
    try {
        const inputs = { qty: parseFloat(document.getElementById('qty').value) || 1, panels: panels, install: document.getElementById('install').value };
        const result = calculateWall(inputs, backendData);
        if (!result || !result.retail) return;
        const ret = result.retail; const fmt = (n) => "$" + (n || 0).toFixed(2);
        
        document.getElementById('lbl-sqft').innerText = ret.displaySqFt.toFixed(1);
        document.getElementById('ui-unit').innerText = fmt(ret.unitPrice);
        document.getElementById('ui-total').innerText = fmt(ret.grandTotal);
        document.getElementById('ui-print').innerText = fmt(ret.printTotal);
        
        if (ret.installTotal > 0) { document.getElementById('row-install').classList.remove('hidden'); document.getElementById('ui-install').innerText = fmt(ret.installTotal); } 
        else { document.getElementById('row-install').classList.add('hidden'); }
        
        document.getElementById('ui-min-text').innerText = `Shop Minimum: $${parseFloat(backendData.Retail_Min_Order || 150)}`;
        document.getElementById('min-badge').classList.toggle('hidden', !ret.isMinApplied);
        
        const instTxt = inputs.install === 'Yes' ? 'Installation Labor Included.' : 'Print Only (No Install).';
        const panelTxt = panels.map(p => {
            let matName = p.material === 'textured' ? '3M IJ8624' : (p.material === 'perf6040' ? 'Perf 60/40' : (p.material === 'perf7030' ? 'Perf 70/30' : 'GF 226 Smooth'));
            return ` - ${p.label}: ${p.w}" x ${p.h}" [${matName} | ${p.laminate}]`;
        }).join('\n');
        document.getElementById('job-desc').value = `(x${inputs.qty}) Environmental Graphics Package.\nAreas:\n${panelTxt}\n\n${instTxt}`;
    } catch(e) { console.error(e); }
}
window.addEventListener('load', async () => {
    if (typeof injectHeader === 'function') injectHeader("Interior Wall Wraps");
    renderPanels(); 
    const statusText = document.getElementById("status-text");
    const statusDot = document.getElementById("status-dot");
    try {
        const req = await fetch(`${SCRIPT_URL}?req=view_module&tab=PROD_Vinyl_Wraps`);
        backendData = await req.json();
        if(statusText) {
            statusText.innerText = "ONLINE";
            statusText.className = "font-bold text-green-500";
            if(statusDot) {
                statusDot.className = "w-2 h-2 rounded-full bg-green-500";
                statusDot.classList.remove("animate-pulse");
            }
        }
        runCalc(); 
    } catch(e) { console.error(e); }
});
</script>
</body>
</html>

            </div>
