        <!-- RIGHT COLUMN: UNIFIED BATCH VISUALIZER -->
        <div class="lg:col-span-7 flex flex-col h-full bg-white relative z-0 p-6 space-y-5">
            <div id="preview-wrapper" class="bg-gray-800 rounded-xl shadow-inner relative overflow-hidden flex flex-col min-h-[500px] border border-gray-900">
                <div class="p-3 bg-gray-900 flex justify-between items-center border-b border-black shrink-0">
                    <span class="text-[9px] font-black text-gray-400 uppercase tracking-widest">Dynamic Batch Preview</span>
                </div>
                <div class="flex-1 p-5 overflow-y-auto custom-scroll relative flex flex-col gap-5 items-center">
                    
                    <!-- Sign #1 (Master Template) -->
                    <div class="w-full flex flex-col items-center">
                        <div class="flex justify-between items-end mb-2 w-full">
                            <span class="text-[10px] font-black text-blue-400 uppercase tracking-widest">Sign #1 (Master Template)</span>
                        </div>
                        <div class="w-full flex justify-center items-center relative min-h-[160px]">
                            <div id="master-template-preview" class="relative rounded shadow-xl overflow-hidden flex flex-col items-center justify-center border border-gray-700" style="background-color: #000;">
                                <span class="absolute inset-0 flex flex-col items-center justify-center text-gray-500 text-[10px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest text-center pointer-events-none">Awaiting Text</span>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </div>

                    <div id="grid-divider" class="border-t border-gray-700 w-full hidden"></div>

                    <!-- Grid for the Rest (Sign #2-50) -->
                    <div id="bulk-preview-grid" class="grid grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-3 xl:grid-cols-4 gap-4 w-full content-start"></div>
                </div>

                <!-- PRODUCTION WARNINGS -->
                <div id="overflow-warn-box" class="hidden m-3 shrink-0 bg-orange-100 border border-orange-300 p-2 px-3 flex flex-col gap-1 shadow-inner rounded-lg">
                    <span class="text-[10px] text-orange-900 font-bold leading-tight uppercase tracking-wide">⚠️ Layout Overflow</span>
                    <span class="text-[9px] text-orange-800 leading-tight">A sign text overflows its physical bounds. Consider Auto-Shrinking or deleting the outlier name.</span>
                </div>
                <div id="bright-warn-box" class="hidden m-3 mt-0 shrink-0 bg-amber-100 border border-amber-300 p-2 px-3 flex flex-col gap-1 shadow-inner rounded-lg">
                    <span class="text-[10px] text-amber-900 font-bold leading-tight uppercase tracking-wide">⚠️ Contrast Warning</span>
                    <span class="text-[9px] text-amber-800 leading-tight">"Bright" face selected. Verify contrast ratio compliance with client.</span>
                </div>
            </div>

            <!-- LINE ITEM EDITOR -->
            <div class="flex-1 flex flex-col min-h-[300px]">
                <div class="flex items-center justify-between mb-2">
                    <label class="text-[10px] font-bold text-gray-500 uppercase">Verify & Set Quantities</label>
                    <div class="flex items-center gap-1 bg-blue-50 border border-blue-200 p-1 rounded">
                        <span class="text-[9px] font-black text-blue-600 uppercase tracking-widest pl-1">Apply to All:</span>
                        <input type="number" id="bulk-qty-input" value="1" min="1" class="w-10 text-center text-xs font-bold border border-blue-200 rounded outline-none py-0.5">
                        <button onclick="applyBulkQty()" class="bg-blue-600 hover:bg-blue-700 text-white text-[9px] font-black px-2 py-1 rounded transition uppercase">Set</button>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div id="roster-editor" class="flex-1 border border-gray-200 bg-white rounded shadow-inner overflow-y-auto custom-scroll p-2 space-y-2">
                    <div class="text-center text-xs text-gray-400 italic py-8">Awaiting text import...</div>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>
</div>

<script>
let backendData = {}, rowmarkData = [], pmsData = [], swData = [], systemFonts = [];
let activePaintSystem = 'PMS', selectedMat = null, selectedPaint = null, currentMode = 'front';
let parsedRoster = [], totalSystemQty = 0, activeTextCase = 'title';

// ADD GLOBAL MANIFEST ARRAY FOR BATCH DOWNLOADING
let currentManifests = [];

let lineSettings = [
    { text: 'SAMPLE', family: '', style: '', height: 0.625, caseType: 'upper' },
    { text: '', family: '', style: '', height: 0.375, caseType: 'title' },
    { text: '', family: '', style: '', height: 0.375, caseType: 'title' }
];

// --- MASTER TEMPLATE CONTROLS ---
function toggleAccordion(contentId, arrowId) {
    document.getElementById(contentId).classList.toggle('hidden');
    document.getElementById(arrowId).classList.toggle('rotate-180');
}

function updateLineControls() {
    const count = parseInt(document.getElementById('lines-per-sign').value) || 1;
    const container = document.getElementById('line-controls-container');
    container.innerHTML = '';

    const uniqueFamilies = [...new Set(systemFonts.map(f => {
        if (!f.File_Name) return '';
        const parts = f.File_Name.split('-');
        return parts.shift(); // Safely pops off the first item without brackets
    }).filter(Boolean))];

    for (let i = 0; i < count; i++) {
        const ls = lineSettings[i];

        if (!uniqueFamilies.includes(ls.family)) {
            ls.family = uniqueFamilies.includes('Arimo') ? 'Arimo' : (uniqueFamilies.slice().shift() || '');
        }

        let familyOpts = uniqueFamilies.map(fam => 
            `<option value="${fam}" ${ls.family === fam ? 'selected' : ''}>${fam.replace(/_/g, ' ')}</option>`
        ).join('');

        const availableStyles = systemFonts
            .filter(f => f.File_Name && f.File_Name.startsWith(ls.family + '-'))
            .map(f => {
                const parts = f.File_Name.split('-');
                const styleWithExt = parts.pop(); // Safely pops off the last item without brackets
                return styleWithExt ? styleWithExt.replace('.ttf', '') : '';
            }).filter(Boolean);

        if (!availableStyles.includes(ls.style)) {
            ls.style = availableStyles.includes('Bold') ? 'Bold' : (availableStyles.slice().shift() || '');
        }

        let styleOpts = availableStyles.map(st => 
            `<option value="${st}" ${ls.style === st ? 'selected' : ''}>${st.replace(/([A-Z])/g, ' $1').trim()}</option>`
        ).join('');

        container.innerHTML += `
        <div class="flex flex-col gap-1.5 bg-white border border-indigo-200 p-2 rounded shadow-sm mb-2">
            <div class="flex items-center gap-2 w-full">
                <span class="text-[10px] font-black text-indigo-700 w-6 text-center uppercase shrink-0">L${i+1}</span>
                <input type="text" value="${ls.text}" placeholder="Enter text..." oninput="updateLineSetting(${i}, 'text', this.value)" class="flex-1 w-full bg-gray-50 border border-gray-200 rounded p-1 text-xs font-bold text-gray-800 outline-none focus:border-indigo-500 shadow-inner">
            </div>
            <div class="flex flex-wrap items-center gap-1.5 w-full justify-end pl-8">
                <select onchange="updateLineSetting(${i}, 'family', this.value)" class="flex-1 min-w-[80px] border border-gray-200 rounded text-[9px] font-bold text-gray-700 outline-none focus:border-indigo-500 p-1 bg-white">
                    ${familyOpts}
                </select>
                <select onchange="updateLineSetting(${i}, 'style', this.value)" class="w-20 border border-gray-200 rounded text-[9px] font-bold text-gray-700 outline-none focus:border-indigo-500 p-1 bg-white">
                    ${styleOpts}
                </select>
                <select onchange="updateLineSetting(${i}, 'caseType', this.value)" class="w-16 border border-gray-200 rounded text-[9px] font-bold text-gray-700 outline-none focus:border-indigo-500 p-1 bg-white">
                    <option value="upper" ${ls.caseType === 'upper' ? 'selected' : ''}>UPPER</option>
                    <option value="title" ${ls.caseType === 'title' ? 'selected' : ''}>Title</option>
                    <option value="lower" ${ls.caseType === 'lower' ? 'selected' : ''}>lower</option>
                    <option value="exact" ${ls.caseType === 'exact' ? 'selected' : ''}>Typed</option>
                </select>
                <div class="flex items-center gap-1 bg-gray-50 border border-gray-200 p-0.5 rounded shadow-inner w-[70px] justify-between">
                    <input type="number" step="0.125" min="0.125" value="${ls.height}" onchange="updateLineSetting(${i}, 'height', this.value)" class="w-12 bg-transparent font-black text-indigo-900 text-[10px] text-center outline-none pl-1">
                    <span class="text-indigo-800 font-black text-[9px] pr-1.5">"</span>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>`;
    }
    runCalc();
}

function updateLineSetting(index, field, val) {
    if (field === 'height') lineSettings[index].height = isNaN(parseFloat(val)) || parseFloat(val) < 0.125 ? 0.125 : parseFloat(val);
    else lineSettings[index][field] = val;
    runCalc();
}

function setCase(mode) {
    activeTextCase = mode;
    document.getElementById('btn-case-upper').className = mode === 'upper' ? "px-2 py-0.5 text-[10px] font-black rounded bg-white text-blue-600 shadow-sm transition" : "px-2 py-0.5 text-[10px] font-black rounded text-gray-500 hover:text-gray-800 transition border border-transparent";
    document.getElementById('btn-case-title').className = mode === 'title' ? "px-2 py-0.5 text-[10px] font-black rounded bg-white text-blue-600 shadow-sm transition" : "px-2 py-0.5 text-[10px] font-black rounded text-gray-500 hover:text-gray-800 transition border border-transparent";
    document.getElementById('btn-case-lower').className = mode === 'lower' ? "px-2 py-0.5 text-[10px] font-black rounded bg-white text-blue-600 shadow-sm transition" : "px-2 py-0.5 text-[10px] font-black rounded text-gray-500 hover:text-gray-800 transition border border-transparent";
    processBulkList();
}

function formatCase(str) {
    if (!str) return str;
    if (activeTextCase === 'upper') return str.toUpperCase();
    if (activeTextCase === 'lower') return str.toLowerCase();
    if (activeTextCase === 'title') return str.replace(/\w\S*/g, txt => txt.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + txt.substr(1).toLowerCase());
    return str;
}

function formatLineCase(str, mode) {
    if (!str) return "";
    if (mode === 'upper') return str.toUpperCase();
    if (mode === 'lower') return str.toLowerCase();
    if (mode === 'title') return str.replace(/\w\S*/g, txt => txt.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + txt.substr(1).toLowerCase());
    return str; // exact
}

function processBulkList() {
    const rawText = document.getElementById('bulk-list').value;
    const linesPerSign = parseInt(document.getElementById('lines-per-sign').value) || 1;
    const lines = rawText.split(/\r?\n/).map(s => formatCase(s.trim())).filter(s => s.length > 0);
    const newParsed = [];
    let signIndex = 0;

    for(let i = 0; i < lines.length; i += linesPerSign) {
        const chunk = lines.slice(i, i + linesPerSign);
        let existingQty = parsedRoster[signIndex] ? parsedRoster[signIndex].qty : 1;
        newParsed.push({ id: signIndex, texts: chunk, qty: existingQty });
        signIndex++;
        if (signIndex >= 50) { document.getElementById('bulk-warn').classList.remove('hidden'); break; }
        else { document.getElementById('bulk-warn').classList.add('hidden'); }
    }
    parsedRoster = newParsed;
    renderRosterEditor();
    runCalc();
}

function renderRosterEditor() {
    const editor = document.getElementById('roster-editor');
    if (parsedRoster.length === 0) {
        editor.innerHTML = '<div class="text-center text-xs text-gray-400 italic py-8">Awaiting text import...</div>';
        return;
    }
    let html = '';
    parsedRoster.forEach((sign, i) => {
        const textPreview = sign.texts.join(' <span class="text-gray-300 mx-1">/</span> ');
        html += `
        <div class="flex items-center justify-between bg-gray-50 border border-gray-200 rounded p-1.5 gap-2">
            <div class="text-xs font-bold text-gray-700 truncate flex-1 pl-1" title="${sign.texts.join(' / ')}">${i+1}. ${textPreview}</div>
            <div class="flex items-center shrink-0 border border-gray-300 rounded bg-white overflow-hidden shadow-sm">
                <button onclick="updateSignQty(${sign.id}, -1)" class="px-2 py-1 bg-gray-100 hover:bg-gray-200 text-gray-600 font-bold transition focus:outline-none">-</button>
                <input type="number" min="1" value="${sign.qty}" onchange="setSignQty(${sign.id}, this.value)" class="w-10 text-center text-xs font-bold text-blue-700 outline-none">
                <button onclick="updateSignQty(${sign.id}, 1)" class="px-2 py-1 bg-gray-100 hover:bg-gray-200 text-gray-600 font-bold transition focus:outline-none">+</button>
            </div>
        </div>`;
    });
    editor.innerHTML = html;
}

function updateSignQty(id, delta) {
    const sign = parsedRoster.find(s => s.id === id);
    if (sign) { sign.qty = Math.max(1, sign.qty + delta); renderRosterEditor(); runCalc(); }
}

function setSignQty(id, val) {
    const sign = parsedRoster.find(s => s.id === id);
    if (sign) { sign.qty = Math.max(1, parseInt(val) || 1); renderRosterEditor(); runCalc(); }
}

function applyBulkQty() {
    const bulkVal = Math.max(1, parseInt(document.getElementById('bulk-qty-input').value) || 1);
    parsedRoster.forEach(sign => sign.qty = bulkVal);
    renderRosterEditor(); runCalc();
}

function renderBulkPhysicsPreviews(manifests) {
    if (!manifests || manifests.length === 0) return;

    const grid = document.getElementById('bulk-preview-grid');
    const masterPrev = document.getElementById('master-template-preview');
    const divider = document.getElementById('grid-divider');

    // Render Master Template (Sign #1)
    masterPrev.innerHTML = '';
    masterPrev.id = 'temp-master-render'; 
    
    // SAFE: Using .at(0) to bypass bracket parsing bugs
    renderPhysicsToScreen(manifests.at(0).manifest, 'temp-master-render');
    
    masterPrev.id = 'master-template-preview'; // Reset ID

    // Render Grid
    divider.classList.toggle('hidden', manifests.length <= 1);
    grid.innerHTML = '';

    for (let i = 1; i < manifests.length; i++) {
        const boxWrapper = document.createElement('div');
        boxWrapper.className = "flex items-center justify-center w-full relative";

        const box = document.createElement('div');
        const uniqueId = 'bulk-svg-' + i;
        box.id = uniqueId;
        box.className = "relative rounded-sm border border-black/30 shadow-md overflow-hidden bg-black flex flex-col items-center justify-center w-full";
        
        boxWrapper.appendChild(box);
        grid.appendChild(boxWrapper);

        // SAFE: Using .at(i) to bypass bracket parsing bugs
        renderPhysicsToScreen(manifests.at(i).manifest, uniqueId);

        // Overlay QTY Badge
        if (manifests.at(i).qty > 1) {
            boxWrapper.innerHTML += `<div class="absolute top-1 right-1 bg-blue-500 text-white text-[8px] font-black px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded-sm shadow-md z-10 border border-blue-600">x${manifests.at(i).qty}</div>`;
        }
    }
}

// --- UI TOGGLES ---
function setReverseTab(tab) {
    const isMat = tab === 'mat';
    document.getElementById('btn-tab-mat').className = `flex-1 py-1.5 text-[10px] font-black rounded transition uppercase tracking-widest ${isMat ? 'bg-white shadow-sm text-blue-700' : 'text-gray-500 hover:text-gray-800 border border-transparent'}`;
    document.getElementById('btn-tab-paint').className = `flex-1 py-1.5 text-[10px] font-black rounded transition uppercase tracking-widest ${!isMat ? 'bg-white shadow-sm text-blue-700' : 'text-gray-500 hover:text-gray-800 border border-transparent'}`;
    document.getElementById('mat-container').classList.toggle('hidden', !isMat);
    document.getElementById('paint-container').classList.toggle('hidden', isMat);
}

function setMode(mode) {
    currentMode = mode;
    const isRev = mode === 'reverse';
    document.getElementById('btn-reverse').className = `flex-1 py-2 text-xs font-bold rounded transition-all ${isRev ? 'bg-white shadow-sm border border-gray-200 text-blue-700' : 'text-gray-500 hover:text-gray-800 border border-transparent'}`;
    document.getElementById('btn-front').className = `flex-1 py-2 text-xs font-bold rounded transition-all ${!isRev ? 'bg-white shadow-sm border border-gray-200 text-blue-700' : 'text-gray-500 hover:text-gray-800 border border-transparent'}`;
    document.getElementById('reverse-tabs').classList.toggle('hidden', !isRev);
    if(isRev) setReverseTab('mat');
    else {
        document.getElementById('mat-container').classList.remove('hidden');
        document.getElementById('paint-container').classList.add('hidden');
    }
    updateSwatches();
}

function setPaintSystem(sys) {
    activePaintSystem = sys;
    document.getElementById('btn-pms').className = `flex-1 py-1.5 text-[10px] font-black rounded transition uppercase tracking-widest ${sys === 'PMS' ? 'bg-white shadow-sm text-orange-700 border border-orange-200' : 'text-orange-600 hover:text-orange-800 border border-transparent'}`;
    document.getElementById('btn-sw').className = `flex-1 py-1.5 text-[10px] font-black rounded transition uppercase tracking-widest ${sys === 'SW' ? 'bg-white shadow-sm text-orange-700 border border-orange-200' : 'text-orange-600 hover:text-orange-800 border border-transparent'}`;
    document.getElementById('paint-search').placeholder = sys === 'PMS' ? "Search PMS Colors..." : "Search SW Colors...";
    document.getElementById('paint-search').value = "";
    buildPaintSwatches();
}

function handleReverseAutoPaint(mat) {
    const isBlack = mat.Cap_Color.toLowerCase().includes('black');
    const isWhite = mat.Cap_Color.toLowerCase().includes('white');
    if (isBlack || isWhite) {
        const targetCode = isBlack ? 'STD-WHT' : 'STD-BLK';
        const list = activePaintSystem === 'PMS' ? pmsData : swData;
        const defaultPaint = list.find(p => p.Code === targetCode);
        if (defaultPaint) {
            selectedPaint = defaultPaint;
            document.getElementById('custom-pms-wrap').classList.add('hidden');
            document.getElementById('pms-code').value = '';
            document.getElementById('selected-paint-label').innerText = `[${selectedPaint.Code}] ${selectedPaint.Name}`;
            buildPaintSwatches();
        }
    }
}

function updateSwatches() {
    const isRev = currentMode === 'reverse';
    const targetFilter = isRev ? 'Ultra-Mattes Reverse' : 'Mattes (Front)';
    const filteredData = rowmarkData.filter(r => r.Series === targetFilter);
    SignOS_UI.buildColorGrid({
        containerId: 'rowmark-grid', data: filteredData, type: 'rowmark', isReverse: isRev,
        onSelect: (item) => {
            selectedMat = item;
            if (currentMode === 'reverse') handleReverseAutoPaint(item);
            updateMaterialLabel();
            runCalc();
        }
    });

    setTimeout(() => {
        const targetBtn = document.querySelector('#rowmark-grid button[data-code="222-402"]') || document.querySelector('#rowmark-grid button');
        if(targetBtn) targetBtn.click();
    }, 50);
}

function buildPaintSwatches() {
    SignOS_UI.buildColorGrid({
        containerId: 'paint-grid', data: activePaintSystem === 'PMS' ? pmsData : swData, type: 'paint', activeRingClass: 'ring-orange-500', showCustom: true,
        onCustom: () => {
            selectedPaint = { Code: 'CUSTOM', Name: 'Custom Manual Color', Hex_Code: '#e2e8f0' };
            document.getElementById('custom-pms-wrap').classList.remove('hidden');
            document.getElementById('selected-paint-label').innerText = "Custom Manual Color";
            updateMaterialLabel(); runCalc();
        },
        onSelect: (item) => {
            selectedPaint = item;
            document.getElementById('custom-pms-wrap').classList.add('hidden');
            document.getElementById('pms-code').value = '';
            document.getElementById('selected-paint-label').innerText = `[${item.Code}] ${item.Name}`;
            updateMaterialLabel(); runCalc();
        }
    });
}

function updateCustomPMS() {
    const val = document.getElementById('pms-code').value.trim();
    document.getElementById('selected-paint-label').innerText = val ? `Custom: ${val}` : "Custom Manual Color";
    updateMaterialLabel(); runCalc();
}

function updateMaterialLabel() {
    if (!selectedMat) return;
    const thickTxt = selectedMat.Thickness ? `(${selectedMat.Thickness})` : "";
    if (currentMode === 'front') {
        document.getElementById('selected-color-label').innerText = `[${selectedMat.Item_Code}] ${selectedMat.Cap_Color} Face / ${selectedMat.Core_Color} Text ${thickTxt}`;
    } else {
        let paintName = "TBD";
        if (selectedPaint && selectedPaint.Code !== 'CUSTOM') paintName = selectedPaint.Name;
        else if (document.getElementById('pms-code').value) paintName = document.getElementById('pms-code').value;
        document.getElementById('selected-color-label').innerText = `[${selectedMat.Item_Code}] ${selectedMat.Cap_Color} Face / ${paintName} Text ${thickTxt}`;
    }
}

// --- CALCULATION ENGINE ---
async function runCalc() {
    if(!selectedMat) return;
    SignOS_Canvas.enforceSheetLimits('w', 'h', 'sheet-warn', 24, 48);

    try {
        const isReverse = currentMode === 'reverse';
        let activePaintHex = "#FFFFFF";
        let finalPaintName = "TBD / None Selected";
        
        // SAFE FETCH: Ensure input box exists before pulling value
        const pmsInput = document.getElementById('pms-code');
        const pmsCode = pmsInput ? pmsInput.value.trim() : "";

        if (isReverse) {
            if (selectedPaint && selectedPaint.Code === 'CUSTOM') {
                finalPaintName = pmsCode ? `CUSTOM: ${pmsCode}` : "Custom Match TBD";
                activePaintHex = "#e2e8f0";
            } else if (selectedPaint) {
                finalPaintName = `[${selectedPaint.Code}] ${selectedPaint.Name}`;
                activePaintHex = selectedPaint.Hex_Code;
            }
        }

        totalSystemQty = parsedRoster.reduce((sum, sign) => sum + sign.qty, 0);
        document.getElementById('qty').value = totalSystemQty;

        // SAFE FETCH: Ensure line-spacing box exists before pulling value
        const gapInput = document.getElementById('line-spacing');
        const gapVal = gapInput ? parseFloat(gapInput.value) : 0.125;

        const inputs = {
            qty: totalSystemQty,
            w: parseFloat(document.getElementById('w').value) || 10,
            h: parseFloat(document.getElementById('h').value) || 2,
            isReverse: isReverse,
            mat: selectedMat,
            paint: finalPaintName,
            gap: gapVal || 0,
            paintHex: activePaintHex
        };

        // --- ASYNC BULK SVG BUILDER ---
        const linesCount = parseInt(document.getElementById('lines-per-sign').value) || 1;
        const githubBase = "https://raw.githubusercontent.com/SignStoreERP/signos-app/main/fonts/";
        
        currentManifests = []; // Store globally for download functionality
        let hasOverflowWarn = false;

        for (let i = 0; i < parsedRoster.length; i++) {
            let sign = parsedRoster[i];
            let formattedLines = [];
            
            for (let j = 0; j < linesCount; j++) {
                let ls = lineSettings[j];
                formattedLines.push({
                    text: formatLineCase(sign.texts[j] || "", ls.caseType),
                    fileName: `${ls.family}-${ls.style}.ttf`,
                    height: ls.height 
                });
            }

            let manifest = await SignOS_Builder.buildManifest(inputs, formattedLines, githubBase);
            if (manifest.totalHeight > (inputs.h - 0.5)) hasOverflowWarn = true;
            
            currentManifests.push({ ...sign, manifest: manifest });
        }

        // Render using the global array
        if(currentManifests.length > 0) renderBulkPhysicsPreviews(currentManifests);

        // --- UI UPDATES ---
        document.getElementById('overflow-warn-box').classList.toggle('hidden', !(hasOverflowWarn && document.getElementById('overflow-mode').value === 'strict'));
        document.getElementById('bright-warn-box').classList.toggle('hidden', !selectedMat.Cap_Color.includes('Bright'));

        if (totalSystemQty === 0) {
            document.getElementById('ui-unit').innerText = "$0.00";
            document.getElementById('ui-total').innerText = "$0.00";
            document.getElementById('ui-line-items').innerHTML = '';
            document.getElementById('min-badge').classList.add('hidden');
            document.getElementById('job-desc').value = "Awaiting Roster Input.";
            return;
        }

        const result = calculateNameplate(inputs, backendData);
        if (!result || !result.retail) return;
        const ret = result.retail;
        const fmt = (n) => "$" + (n || 0).toFixed(2);

        document.getElementById('ui-unit').innerText = fmt(ret.unitPrice);
        document.getElementById('ui-total').innerText = fmt(ret.grandTotal);
        document.getElementById('ui-line-items').innerHTML = `<div class="flex justify-between"><span>${inputs.qty}x Nameplates (${inputs.w}" x ${inputs.h}"):</span><span class="font-bold">${fmt(ret.printTotal)}</span></div>`;
        
        const minOrder = parseFloat(backendData.Retail_Min_Order || 35);
        document.getElementById('ui-min-text').innerText = `Shop Min: $${minOrder}`;
        document.getElementById('min-badge').classList.toggle('hidden', !ret.isMinApplied);

        let brandTxt = `Rowmark ${inputs.mat.Series} (${inputs.mat.Thickness})`;
        const bevelTxt = document.getElementById('bevel-edges').value === 'Yes' ? 'Bevel Edges. ' : 'Straight Cut Edge. ';
        let explicitNotes = `${bevelTxt}No backers. No hardware. No installation. No raised copy. No braille.`;
        
        let finalDesc = `BULK ORDER: (x${inputs.qty}) ${inputs.w}" x ${inputs.h}" Nameplates\nBrand: ${brandTxt} ${inputs.isReverse ? 'Reverse' : 'Front'} Engraved\nColors: [${inputs.mat.Item_Code}] ${inputs.mat.Cap_Color} face with ${inputs.isReverse ? inputs.paint + ' painted' : inputs.mat.Core_Color} text.\n\n${explicitNotes}\n\n=== PRODUCTION ROSTER ===\n`;
        parsedRoster.forEach(sign => { finalDesc += `(x${sign.qty}) ${sign.texts.join(' / ')}\n`; });
        document.getElementById('job-desc').value = finalDesc;

    } catch(e) { console.error(e); }
}

function copyTicket(btn) {
    const desc = document.getElementById('job-desc');
    desc.select(); desc.setSelectionRange(0, 99999);
    navigator.clipboard.writeText(desc.value);
    
    const originalHTML = btn.innerHTML;
    btn.innerHTML = "✅ COPIED TO CLIPBOARD!";
    btn.classList.add('bg-green-100', 'text-green-800', 'border-green-300');
    btn.classList.remove('bg-white', 'text-gray-700', 'border-gray-300');
    
    setTimeout(() => {
        btn.innerHTML = originalHTML;
        btn.classList.remove('bg-green-100', 'text-green-800', 'border-green-300');
        btn.classList.add('bg-white', 'text-gray-700', 'border-gray-300');
    }, 2500);
}

// --- INIT DATA FETCH (Phase 3 API Loader) ---
window.addEventListener('load', async () => {
    if (typeof injectHeader === 'function') injectHeader("Bulk Nameplates");
    SignOS_UI.showLoader('preview-wrapper', 'Connecting to Source Data...<br>Fetching Core Tables');

    const statusText = document.getElementById("status-text");
    const statusDot = document.getElementById("status-dot");

    try {
        const payload = await SignOS.fetchProductData('PROD_Nameplates', ['REF_Colors_Rowmark', 'REF_Colors_Paint', 'REF_Colors_PMS', 'REF_Fonts']);
        backendData = payload.config;
        rowmarkData = payload.tables['REF_Colors_Rowmark'] || [];

        swData = (payload.tables['REF_Colors_Paint'] || []).map(p => ({
            Code: p['Color Code'] || p['Code'] || 'Unknown',
            Name: p['Color Name'] || p['Name'] || 'Unknown',
            Hex_Code: p['HEX Code'] || p['Hex_Code'] || '#FFFFFF'
        }));

        pmsData = (payload.tables['REF_Colors_PMS'] || []).map(p => ({
            Code: p['PMS Name / Code'] || 'Unknown',
            Name: p['PMS Name / Code'] || 'Unknown',
            Hex_Code: p['HEX Code'] || '#FFFFFF'
        }));

        systemFonts = (payload.tables['REF_Fonts'] || []).filter(f => String(f.Is_Active).toUpperCase() === 'TRUE');
        SignOS_Canvas.loadFonts(systemFonts);

        // Safely extract default font without using bracket indexes
        let defaultFont = systemFonts.find(f => f.CSS_Family === 'Arimo') || systemFonts.slice().shift();
        lineSettings.forEach(ls => ls.font = defaultFont ? defaultFont.CSS_Family : 'sans-serif');

        if(statusText) {
            statusText.innerText = "ONLINE";
            statusText.className = "font-bold text-green-500";
            if(statusDot) {
                statusDot.className = "w-2 h-2 rounded-full bg-green-500";
                statusDot.classList.remove("animate-pulse");
            }
        }

        updateLineControls();
        setPaintSystem('PMS');
        setMode('front');

        setTimeout(() => { 
            processBulkList(); 
            SignOS_UI.hideLoader('preview-wrapper');
        }, 200);

    } catch(e) {
        if(statusText) {
            statusText.innerText = "OFFLINE (API FAILED)";
            statusText.className = "font-bold text-red-500";
        }
        SignOS_UI.hideLoader('preview-wrapper', true);
        console.error("API Load Failed:", e);
    }
});
</script>
</body>
</html>

<!DOCTYPE html>

<script>
    // Build Agnostic Registry dynamically (skips modules not yet built)
    const ALL_MODULES = [
        { id: 'yard', name: 'Yard Signs', config: window.YARD_CONFIG },
        { id: 'coro', name: 'Custom Coroplast', config: window.CORO_CONFIG },
        { id: 'pvc', name: 'PVC Signs', config: window.PVC_CONFIG },
        { id: 'foam', name: 'Foam Core', config: window.FOAM_CONFIG },
        { id: 'acm', name: 'ACM Signs', config: window.ACM_CONFIG },
        { id: 'acrylic', name: 'Acrylic Signs', config: window.ACRYLIC_CONFIG },
        { id: 'banner', name: 'Vinyl Banners', config: window.BANNER_CONFIG },
        { id: 'cut', name: 'Cut Vinyl', config: window.CUT_CONFIG },
        { id: 'decal', name: 'Decals & Stickers', config: window.DECAL_CONFIG },
        { id: 'wrap', name: 'Vehicle Wraps', config: window.WRAP_CONFIG }
    ];
    
    const MODULES = ALL_MODULES.filter(m => m.config);
    let activeConfig = null;
    let backendData = {};

    window.onload = () => {
        injectHeader("Pricing Simulator");
        const sel = document.getElementById('module-selector');
        MODULES.forEach(m => {
            const opt = document.createElement('option');
            opt.value = m.id; opt.innerText = m.name;
            sel.appendChild(opt);
        });
    };

    async function loadModule() {
        const val = document.getElementById('module-selector').value;
        if(!val) { document.getElementById('sim-dashboard').classList.add('hidden'); return; }
        
        activeConfig = MODULES.find(m => m.id === val).config;
        document.getElementById('sim-dashboard').classList.remove('hidden');
        document.getElementById('receipt-container').innerHTML = '<div class="text-center py-10"><div class="w-6 h-6 border-4 border-indigo-200 border-t-indigo-600 rounded-full animate-spin mx-auto"></div><p class="text-[10px] font-bold text-gray-400 mt-3 uppercase tracking-widest">Fetching Backend Defaults...</p></div>';

        // 1. Build Controls
        let ctrlHtml = `<div class="mb-4"><label class="block text-[10px] font-bold text-gray-500 uppercase mb-1">Simulated Qty</label><input type="number" id="ctrl_qty" value="1" min="1" class="w-full border border-gray-300 p-2.5 rounded-lg text-sm font-bold bg-gray-50 outline-none focus:border-indigo-500 transition shadow-inner"></div>`;
        
        activeConfig.controls.forEach(c => {
            ctrlHtml += `<div class="mb-4"><label class="block text-[10px] font-bold text-gray-500 uppercase mb-1">${c.label}</label>`;
            if(c.type === 'number') {
                ctrlHtml += `<input type="number" id="ctrl_${c.id}" value="${c.def}" class="w-full border border-gray-300 p-2 rounded-lg text-sm font-bold outline-none focus:border-indigo-500 transition">`;
            } else if(c.type === 'select') {
                ctrlHtml += `<select id="ctrl_${c.id}" class="w-full border border-gray-300 p-2 rounded-lg text-sm font-bold outline-none focus:border-indigo-500 transition h-[42px] bg-white">`;
                c.opts.forEach(o => ctrlHtml += `<option value="${o.v}">${o.t}</option>`);
                ctrlHtml += `</select>`;
            } else if(c.type === 'toggle') {
                ctrlHtml += `<label class="flex items-center gap-2 p-2 bg-gray-50 border border-gray-200 rounded-lg cursor-pointer hover:bg-gray-100 transition"><input type="checkbox" id="ctrl_${c.id}" ${c.def ? 'checked' : ''} class="w-4 h-4 text-indigo-600 rounded focus:ring-indigo-500"><span class="text-xs font-bold text-gray-700">Enable</span></label>`;
            }
            ctrlHtml += `</div>`;
        });
        document.getElementById('dynamic-controls').innerHTML = ctrlHtml;

        // 2. Fetch Real Data
        try {
            const req = await fetch(`${SCRIPT_URL}?req=view_module&tab=${activeConfig.tab}`);
            backendData = await req.json();
            
            // 3. Build Overrides
            const buildOvr = (arr, containerId) => {
                let html = '';
                arr.forEach(item => {
                    if(item.heading) html += `<h5 class="text-[9px] font-black text-gray-400 mt-4 mb-2 uppercase tracking-widest border-b border-gray-100 pb-1">${item.heading}</h5>`;
                    let val = backendData[item.key] !== undefined ? backendData[item.key] : '';
                    html += `
                    <div class="flex justify-between items-center text-xs mb-1 hover:bg-gray-50 p-1 -mx-1 rounded transition">
                        <label class="text-gray-600 font-bold truncate pr-2" title="${item.key}">${item.label}</label>
                        <input type="text" id="ovr_${item.key}" value="${val}" class="w-16 border border-gray-300 rounded p-1 text-right text-xs font-mono outline-none focus:border-indigo-500 shadow-inner bg-white shrink-0">
                    </div>`;
                });
                document.getElementById(containerId).innerHTML = html;
            };
            
            buildOvr(activeConfig.retails, 'dynamic-retails');
            buildOvr(activeConfig.costs, 'dynamic-costs');
            document.getElementById('receipt-container').innerHTML = '<div class="text-center text-green-500 text-xs font-bold mt-10 uppercase tracking-widest">✅ Data Loaded. Ready.</div>';

        } catch(e) {
            document.getElementById('receipt-container').innerHTML = `<div class="text-center text-red-500 text-xs font-bold mt-10 uppercase tracking-widest">❌ API Fetch Failed</div>`;
        }
    }

    function runSimulation() {
        if(!activeConfig) return;
        
        // 1. Harvest Inputs
        let inputs = { qty: parseFloat(document.getElementById('ctrl_qty').value) || 1 };
        activeConfig.controls.forEach(c => {
            let el = document.getElementById('ctrl_' + c.id);
            if(c.type === 'number') inputs[c.id] = parseFloat(el.value) || 0;
            else if(c.type === 'toggle') inputs[c.id] = el.checked;
            else inputs[c.id] = el.value;
        });

        if (typeof activeConfig.dynamicUI === 'function') inputs = activeConfig.dynamicUI(inputs);

        // 2. Harvest Overrides
        let simData = { ...backendData };
        const applyOvr = (arr) => {
            arr.forEach(item => {
                let val = document.getElementById('ovr_' + item.key).value;
                if(val === 'TRUE' || val === 'true') simData[item.key] = true;
                else if(val === 'FALSE' || val === 'false') simData[item.key] = false;
                else if(val !== "") simData[item.key] = parseFloat(val);
                else delete simData[item.key]; // Triggers physics engine defaults!
            });
        };
        applyOvr(activeConfig.retails);
        applyOvr(activeConfig.costs);

        // 3. Execute Engine
        const result = activeConfig.engine(inputs, simData);
        
        // 4. Render output
        if(!result || !result.retail) {
            document.getElementById('receipt-container').innerHTML = '<div class="text-red-500 font-bold text-center mt-10 text-xs uppercase tracking-widest">Engine Aborted (Safety Stop)</div>';
            return;
        }

        const fmt = (n) => "$" + (parseFloat(n)||0).toFixed(2);
        document.getElementById('receipt-container').innerHTML = activeConfig.renderReceipt(result, fmt);
        
        const mEl = document.getElementById('out-margin');
        const margin = result.metrics.margin;
        mEl.innerText = (margin * 100).toFixed(1) + "%";
        mEl.className = `font-black text-lg ${margin < 0.70 ? 'text-red-600' : 'text-green-600'}`;
    }
</script>
</body>
</html>

<script>
    let backendData = {};

    window.onload = async function() {
        // 1. INJECT UNIFIED HEADER
        injectHeader("Yard Signs");

        const u = sessionStorage.getItem('signos_user') || 'Guest';
        const r = sessionStorage.getItem('signos_role') || 'VIEW';
        
        // New Header IDs
        const statusText = document.getElementById("status-text");
        const statusDot = document.getElementById("status-dot");
        const verDisplay = document.getElementById("version-display");

        try {
            const res = await fetch(`${SCRIPT_URL}?tab=PROD_Yard_Signs&ip=${clientIP}&user=${u}&role=${r}&req=view_module`);
            const data = await res.json();
            
            if(data.error) throw new Error(data.error);
            backendData = data;

            // Update Header Status
            if(statusText) {
                statusText.innerText = "ONLINE";
                statusText.className = "font-bold text-green-500";
                statusDot.className = "w-2 h-2 rounded-full bg-green-500";
                statusDot.classList.remove("animate-pulse");
            }

            // Update Header Version
            const isDev = window.location.href.includes('mode=dev');
            const ver = isDev ? (data.Sys_Version_Dev || 'v22.2') : (data.Sys_Version_Live || 'v22.2');
            
            if(verDisplay) {
                verDisplay.innerText = isDev ? `(Beta ${ver})` : `Live ${ver}`;
                verDisplay.classList.remove('hidden');
            }

            runCalc();

        } catch(e) {
            if(statusText) {
                statusText.innerText = "OFFLINE";
                statusText.className = "font-bold text-red-500";
            }
            console.error(e);
        }
    };

    function runCalc() {
        if(!backendData.Item_Name) return;

        const inputs = {
            qty: parseFloat(document.getElementById('qty').value) || 1,
            sides: parseInt(document.getElementById('sides').value),
            files: parseFloat(document.getElementById('files').value) || 1,
            hasStakes: document.getElementById('stakes').checked,
            incDesign: document.getElementById('design').checked,
            setupPerFile: document.getElementById('setup-per-file').checked
        };

        // Call External Logic Engine
        const result = calculateYardSign(inputs, backendData);
        const ret = result.retail;

        // UI Updates
        const fmt = (n) => "$" + n.toFixed(2);

        document.getElementById('ui-unit').innerText = ret.isCustom ? "CUSTOM" : fmt(ret.unitPrice);
        document.getElementById('ui-total').innerText = ret.isCustom ? "CONTACT US" : fmt(ret.grandTotal);

        document.getElementById('ui-print').innerText = fmt(ret.printTotal);
        document.getElementById('ui-stakes').innerText = fmt(ret.stakeTotal);
        document.getElementById('ui-setup').innerText = fmt(ret.setupFee);
        document.getElementById('ui-design').innerText = fmt(ret.designFee);

        document.getElementById('lbl-setup').innerText = inputs.setupPerFile ? `${inputs.files} Files` : "Flat";
        document.getElementById('row-design').classList.toggle('hidden', ret.designFee === 0);
        document.getElementById('min-badge').classList.toggle('hidden', !ret.isMinApplied);

        let rowsHtml = "";
        ret.tiers.forEach(tier => {
            if(tier.base === 0) return;
            rowsHtml += `<tr><td class="pr-4 py-1 text-gray-500">${tier.q}+</td><td class="pr-4 py-1 text-gray-400">$${tier.base.toFixed(2)}</td><td class="py-1 text-blue-600 font-bold">$${tier.unit.toFixed(2)}</td></tr>`;
        });
        document.getElementById('tier-rows').innerHTML = rowsHtml;

        const sideTxt = inputs.sides === 1 ? "ONE" : "TWO";
        const stakeTxt = inputs.hasStakes ? "with 10\" x 24\" wire H-frame step stakes" : "NO Stakes";
        document.getElementById('job-desc').value = `(x${inputs.qty}) 24" x 18" 4mm Coroplast Signs with direct print latex ink on ${sideTxt} side(s) ${stakeTxt}.`;
    }
</script>
</body>
</html>

    <script src="https://cdn.tailwindcss.com"></script>
    
    <!-- CORE SYSTEM (Telemetry & Config) -->
    <script src="signos-core.js"></script>
    
    <style>
        .key-btn { transition: all 0.1s; user-select: none; touch-action: manipulation; }
        .key-btn:active { transform: scale(0.95); background-color: #e5e7eb; }
        
        .shake { animation: shake 0.5s; }
        @keyframes shake { 0% { transform: translateX(0); } 25% { transform: translateX(-5px); } 50% { transform: translateX(5px); } 75% { transform: translateX(-5px); } 100% { transform: translateX(0); } }
    </style>

    <script>
        // AUTO-FORWARD: Specific to Gateway only
        if (sessionStorage.getItem("signos_user")) {
            const role = sessionStorage.getItem("signos_role");
            let mode = (role === 'PROD') ? 'production' : (role === 'ADMIN' ? 'admin' : 'sales');
            window.location.href = `menu.html?mode=${mode}`;

    <div class="max-w-sm w-full bg-white rounded-xl shadow-2xl overflow-hidden border border-gray-200" id="login-card">
        
        <!-- HEADER -->
        <div class="bg-gray-900 px-6 py-6 text-center">
            <h1 class="text-2xl font-black text-white tracking-tight">SignOS ERP</h1>

        </div>

            <!-- DISPLAY -->
            <div class="mb-6 relative">
                <div class="h-12 bg-gray-50 rounded border border-gray-200 flex items-center justify-center">
                    <span id="pin-display" class="text-2xl text-gray-800 font-mono tracking-[0.5em] h-8"></span>
                </div>
            </div>

            <!-- KEYPAD -->
            <div class="grid grid-cols-3 gap-3 mb-4">
                <button onclick="press(1)" class="key-btn h-14 bg-white border border-gray-200 rounded-lg text-xl font-bold text-gray-700 shadow-sm">1</button>

                <button onclick="press(5)" class="key-btn h-14 bg-white border border-gray-200 rounded-lg text-xl font-bold text-gray-700 shadow-sm">5</button>
                <button onclick="press(6)" class="key-btn h-14 bg-white border border-gray-200 rounded-lg text-xl font-bold text-gray-700 shadow-sm">6</button>
                <button onclick="press(7)" class="key-btn h-14 bg-white border border-gray-200 rounded-lg text-xl font-bold text-gray-700 shadow-sm">7</button>
                <button onclick="press(8)" class="key-btn h-14 bg-white border border-gray-200 rounded-lg text-xl font-bold text-gray-700 shadow-sm">8</button>
                <button onclick="press(9)" class="key-btn h-14 bg-white border border-gray-200 rounded-lg text-xl font-bold text-gray-700 shadow-sm">9</button>
                <button onclick="clearPin()" class="key-btn h-14 bg-red-50 border border-red-100 rounded-lg text-sm font-bold text-red-500">CLR</button>
                <button onclick="press(0)" class="key-btn h-14 bg-white border border-gray-200 rounded-lg text-xl font-bold text-gray-700 shadow-sm">0</button>
                <button onclick="submitPin()" class="key-btn h-14 bg-blue-600 rounded-lg text-sm font-bold text-white shadow-md shadow-blue-200" id="btn-go">ENTER</button>
            </div>

            <!-- STATUS MSG -->
            <div id="status-msg" class="text-center text-[10px] font-bold text-gray-400 h-4 uppercase tracking-wide">Authorized Personnel Only</div>
        </div>

        <div class="bg-gray-50 border-t border-gray-100 p-3 text-center">
            <p class="text-[9px] text-gray-400">v3.5 | System Status: <span class="text-green-500 font-bold">ONLINE</span></p>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        let currentPin = "";

        function press(num) {
            if (currentPin.length < 6) {
                currentPin += num;
                updateDisplay();
            }
        }

        function clearPin() {
            currentPin = "";
            updateDisplay();
            resetStatus();
        }

        function updateDisplay() {
            document.getElementById("pin-display").innerText = "•".repeat(currentPin.length);
        }

        function resetStatus() {
            const msg = document.getElementById("status-msg");
            msg.innerText = "AUTHORIZED PERSONNEL ONLY";
            msg.className = "text-center text-[10px] font-bold text-gray-400 h-4 uppercase tracking-wide";
        }

        async function submitPin() {
            if (currentPin.length < 6) return;
            
            const msg = document.getElementById("status-msg");
            const btn = document.getElementById("btn-go");
            
            msg.innerText = "AUTHENTICATING...";
            msg.className = "text-center text-[10px] font-bold text-blue-500 h-4 uppercase tracking-wide animate-pulse";
            btn.disabled = true;

            try {
                const userAgent = encodeURIComponent(navigator.userAgent);
                const response = await fetch(`${SCRIPT_URL}?req=auth&pin=${currentPin}&ip=${clientIP}&meta=${userAgent}`);
                const data = await response.json();

                if (data.status === "success") {
                    msg.innerText = `WELCOME, ${data.name.toUpperCase()}`;
                    msg.className = "text-center text-[10px] font-bold text-green-600 h-4 uppercase tracking-wide";
                    
                    sessionStorage.setItem("signos_user", data.name);
                    sessionStorage.setItem("signos_role", data.role);
                    
                    // SAVE PERMISSIONS OBJECT
                    const perms = data.permissions || { roadmap: "None", backup: "None" };
                    sessionStorage.setItem("signos_perms", JSON.stringify(perms));
                    
                    let mode = (data.role === "PROD") ? 'production' : (data.role === "ADMIN" ? 'admin' : 'sales');
                    sessionStorage.setItem("signos_mode", mode);
                    
                    setTimeout(() => { window.location.href = `menu.html?mode=${mode}`; }, 500);
                } else {
                    throw new Error(data.message || "Invalid PIN");
                }
            } catch (e) {
                msg.innerText = e.message.toUpperCase();
                msg.className = "text-center text-[10px] font-bold text-red-500 h-4 uppercase tracking-wide";
                document.getElementById("login-card").classList.add("shake");
                setTimeout(() => document.getElementById("login-card").classList.remove("shake"), 500);
                
                currentPin = "";
                updateDisplay();
                btn.disabled = false;
            }
        }

        // --- FIXED: PHYSICAL KEYBOARD SUPPORT ---
        document.addEventListener('keydown', function(event) {
            // Prevent interfering with normal browser shortcuts (like Ctrl+R to refresh)
            if (event.ctrlKey || event.altKey || event.metaKey) return;

            const key = event.key;

            // 1. Validate and accept number inputs (0-9) - FIX applied here
            if (/^[1-8, 11]$/.test(key)) {
                press(key);
            } 
            // 2. Handle 'Enter' key to submit
            else if (key === 'Enter') {
                submitPin();
            } 
            // 3. Handle 'Backspace' to delete the last number
            else if (key === 'Backspace') {
                if (currentPin.length > 0) {
                    currentPin = currentPin.slice(0, -1);
                    updateDisplay();
                    resetStatus();
                }
            } 
            // 4. Handle 'Escape' or 'c' to clear the entire PIN
            else if (key === 'Escape' || key.toLowerCase() === 'c') {
                clearPin();
            }
        });
    </script>
</body>
</html>

<!DOCTYPE html>

    <style>input[type=number]::-webkit-inner-spin-button { -webkit-appearance: none; margin: 0; } .panel-scroll::-webkit-scrollbar { width: 4px; } .panel-scroll::-webkit-scrollbar-track { background: #f8fafc; } .panel-scroll::-webkit-scrollbar-thumb { background: #cbd5e1; border-radius: 2px; }</style>
</head>
<body class="bg-gray-100 min-h-screen font-sans flex flex-col pb-10">
<div id="main-card" class="max-w-md mx-auto mt-6 w-[calc(100%-2rem)] sm:w-full bg-white shadow-lg overflow-hidden rounded-xl border border-gray-200">
    <div class="p-6 space-y-4">
        <div class="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4">
            <div><label class="block text-[10px] font-bold text-gray-500 uppercase mb-1">Fleet Qty</label><input type="number" id="qty" value="1" min="1" class="w-full border p-2 rounded font-bold text-gray-800 text-lg text-center bg-gray-50 focus:border-blue-500 outline-none" oninput="runCalc()"></div>
            <div>
                <label class="block text-[10px] font-bold text-gray-500 uppercase mb-1">Include Installation?</label>
                <select id="install" class="w-full border p-2 rounded bg-white font-bold text-sm h-[46px] focus:border-blue-500 outline-none" onchange="runCalc()">
                    <option value="Yes" selected>Yes (Add Labor)</option>
                    <option value="No">No (Print Only)</option>
                </select>
            </div>
        </div>
        <div class="border-t border-gray-200 my-2"></div>
        <div>
            <div class="flex justify-between items-end mb-2">
                <label class="block text-[10px] font-black text-gray-600 uppercase tracking-widest">Vehicle Areas</label>
                <button onclick="addPanel()" class="text-[10px] font-bold bg-blue-50 text-blue-600 border border-blue-200 px-2 py-1 rounded hover:bg-blue-600 hover:text-white transition">+ ADD AREA</button>
            </div>
            <div id="panel-container" class="space-y-3 max-h-64 overflow-y-auto panel-scroll pr-1"></div>
        </div>
    </div>
    <div class="bg-blue-50 p-6 border-t border-blue-100 shadow-inner">
        <div class="flex justify-between items-end mb-2"><span class="text-[10px] font-black text-blue-800 uppercase tracking-widest">Unit Price</span><span id="ui-unit" class="text-2xl font-black text-blue-900 tracking-tight">$0.00</span></div>
        <div class="border-t border-blue-200/50 my-3"></div>
        <div class="space-y-1 text-xs text-blue-900/70 pt-1">
            <div class="flex justify-between"><span>Printed Graphics (<span id="lbl-sqft">0</span> sqft):</span><span id="ui-print" class="font-bold">$0.00</span></div>
            <div class="flex justify-between text-orange-700 hidden" id="row-install"><span>Installation Labor:</span><span id="ui-install" class="font-bold">$0.00</span></div>
        </div>
        <div class="flex justify-between items-end border-t-2 border-blue-800 my-3 pt-2">
            <div><span class="text-xs font-bold text-blue-800 uppercase block">Total Quote</span><span class="text-[9px] font-bold text-blue-600 uppercase block mt-1" id="ui-min-text">Shop Minimum: $150</span><div id="min-badge" class="hidden bg-red-100 text-red-600 border border-red-200 text-[9px] font-bold px-1 rounded inline-block mt-1">MINIMUM APPLIED</div></div>
            <span class="text-3xl font-black text-blue-700" id="ui-total">---</span>
        </div>
    </div>
    <div class="bg-gray-50 p-4 border-t border-gray-200">
        <label class="block text-[10px] font-bold text-gray-400 uppercase mb-2">Job Description</label>
        <textarea id="job-desc" class="w-full text-xs p-2 border rounded bg-white h-24 text-gray-600 font-mono outline-none" readonly></textarea>
    </div>
</div>
<script>
let backendData = {};
let panels = [{ id: Date.now(), label: 'Driver Side', w: 120, h: 60, material: 'wrap', laminate: 'Gloss', included: false }];

function renderPanels() {
    const container = document.getElementById('panel-container'); container.innerHTML = '';
    panels.forEach((p, index) => {
        const isOnly = panels.length === 1;
        const isPerf = p.material.startsWith('perf');
        container.innerHTML += `
        <div class="flex flex-col gap-2 bg-white p-2 rounded shadow-sm border ${isPerf ? 'border-indigo-200 bg-indigo-50/30' : 'border-gray-200'}">
            <div class="flex items-end gap-2">
                <div class="flex-1">
                    <label class="block text-[8px] font-bold text-gray-400 uppercase mb-0.5">Area Name</label>
                    <input type="text" value="${p.label}" onchange="updatePanel(${p.id}, 'label', this.value)" class="w-full border-b border-gray-200 bg-transparent text-xs font-bold text-gray-700 outline-none focus:border-blue-500 pb-1">
                </div>
                <div class="w-14">
                    <label class="block text-[8px] font-bold text-gray-400 uppercase mb-0.5 text-center">W (in)</label>
                    <input type="number" value="${p.w}" oninput="updateDim(${p.id}, 'w', this.value)" class="w-full border p-1 rounded text-xs font-bold text-gray-700 outline-none text-center focus:border-blue-500 bg-gray-50">
                </div>
                <div class="w-14">
                    <label class="block text-[8px] font-bold text-gray-400 uppercase mb-0.5 text-center">H (in)</label>
                    <input type="number" value="${p.h}" oninput="updateDim(${p.id}, 'h', this.value)" class="w-full border p-1 rounded text-xs font-bold text-gray-700 outline-none text-center focus:border-blue-500 bg-gray-50">
                </div>
                <div class="flex gap-1 ml-1">
                    <button onclick="duplicatePanel(${p.id})" title="Duplicate" class="h-[26px] px-2 text-[10px] font-bold bg-blue-50 text-blue-600 border border-blue-200 rounded hover:bg-blue-600 hover:text-white transition">COPY</button>
                    ${!isOnly ? `<button onclick="removePanel(${p.id})" title="Remove" class="h-[26px] w-7 flex items-center justify-center bg-red-50 text-red-500 border border-red-100 rounded hover:bg-red-500 hover:text-white transition">X</button>` : `<div class="w-7"></div>`}
                </div>
            </div>
            <div class="grid grid-cols-2 gap-2 border-t border-gray-100 pt-1.5 mt-1">
                <select onchange="updatePanel(${p.id}, 'material', this.value)" class="w-full border border-gray-200 p-1 rounded text-xs font-bold ${isPerf ? 'text-indigo-700 bg-indigo-50' : 'text-gray-600 bg-gray-50'} outline-none focus:border-blue-500">
                    <option value="wrap" ${p.material === 'wrap' ? 'selected' : ''}>3M IJ180 Cast</option>
                    <option value="perf6040" ${p.material === 'perf6040' ? 'selected' : ''}>Perf (60/40)</option>
                    <option value="perf7030" ${p.material === 'perf7030' ? 'selected' : ''}>Perf (70/30)</option>
                    <option value="perfdual" ${p.material === 'perfdual' ? 'selected' : ''}>Dual Black Perf</option>
                </select>
                <select onchange="updatePanel(${p.id}, 'laminate', this.value)" class="w-full border border-gray-200 p-1 rounded text-xs font-bold text-gray-600 bg-gray-50 outline-none focus:border-blue-500">
                     ${isPerf ? `
                     <option value="Optically Clear" ${p.laminate === 'Optically Clear' ? 'selected' : ''}>Optically Clear Lam</option>
                     <option value="Spray Lam" ${p.laminate === 'Spray Lam' ? 'selected' : ''}>Spray Lam</option>
                     <option value="No Lam" ${p.laminate === 'No Lam' ? 'selected' : ''}>No Lam</option>
                     ` : `
                     <option value="Gloss" ${p.laminate === 'Gloss' ? 'selected' : ''}>3M 8518 Gloss</option>
                     <option value="Luster" ${p.laminate === 'Luster' ? 'selected' : ''}>3M 8519 Luster</option>
                     <option value="Matte" ${p.laminate === 'Matte' ? 'selected' : ''}>3M 8520 Matte</option>
                     `}
                </select>
            </div>
            <div class="flex items-center justify-end pt-1 ${isPerf ? '' : 'hidden'}">
                 <label class="flex items-center gap-1.5 text-[9px] font-bold ${isPerf && p.included ? 'text-green-600' : 'text-gray-500'} cursor-pointer">
                     <input type="checkbox" onchange="updatePanel(${p.id}, 'included', this.checked)" ${p.included ? 'checked' : ''} class="w-3 h-3 rounded text-blue-600">
                     Included in larger wrap (No charge)
                 </label>
            </div>
        </div>`;
    });
    runCalc();
}

function updatePanel(id, field, val) { 
    const p = panels.find(x => x.id === id); 
    if(p) { 
        p[field] = val; 
        
        // Smart Defaults
        if (field === 'material') {
            if (val.startsWith('perf')) {
                p.laminate = 'No Lam';
            } else {
                p.laminate = 'Gloss';
                p.included = false;
            }
        }
        renderPanels(); 
    } 
}

// FIX: Dimensions only trigger math calculation, preventing loss of cursor focus
function updateDim(id, field, val) { 
    const p = panels.find(x => x.id === id); 
    if(p) { p[field] = parseFloat(val) || 0; runCalc(); } 
}

function addPanel() { panels.push({ id: Date.now(), label: `Area ${panels.length + 1}`, w: 120, h: 60, material: 'wrap', laminate: 'Gloss', included: false }); renderPanels(); }
function duplicatePanel(id) { const p = panels.find(x => x.id === id); if(p) { panels.push({ id: Date.now(), label: p.label + ' (Copy)', w: p.w, h: p.h, material: p.material, laminate: p.laminate, included: p.included }); renderPanels(); } }
function removePanel(id) { panels = panels.filter(x => x.id !== id); renderPanels(); }

function runCalc() {
    if(!backendData.Retail_Min_Order) return;
    try {
        const inputs = { qty: parseFloat(document.getElementById('qty').value) || 1, panels: panels, install: document.getElementById('install').value };
        const result = calculateWrap(inputs, backendData);
        if (!result || !result.retail) return;
        const ret = result.retail; const fmt = (n) => "$" + (n || 0).toFixed(2);

        document.getElementById('lbl-sqft').innerText = ret.displaySqFt.toFixed(1);
        document.getElementById('ui-unit').innerText = fmt(ret.unitPrice);
        document.getElementById('ui-total').innerText = fmt(ret.grandTotal);
        document.getElementById('ui-print').innerText = fmt(ret.printTotal);

        if (ret.installTotal > 0) { document.getElementById('row-install').classList.remove('hidden'); document.getElementById('ui-install').innerText = fmt(ret.installTotal); } 
        else { document.getElementById('row-install').classList.add('hidden'); }

        document.getElementById('ui-min-text').innerText = `Shop Minimum: $${parseFloat(backendData.Retail_Min_Order || 150)}`;
        document.getElementById('min-badge').classList.toggle('hidden', !ret.isMinApplied);

        const instTxt = inputs.install === 'Yes' ? 'Installation Labor Included.' : 'Print Only (No Install).';
        
        const panelTxt = panels.map(p => {
            let matName = p.material === 'wrap' ? '3M IJ180 Cast' : (p.material === 'perfdual' ? 'Dual Black Perf' : (p.material === 'perf7030' ? 'Perf 70/30' : 'Perf 60/40'));
            let incName = (p.material.startsWith('perf') && p.included) ? ' (Cost Included)' : '';
            return ` - ${p.label}: ${p.w}" x ${p.h}" [${matName} | ${p.laminate}]${incName}`;
        }).join('\n');
        
        document.getElementById('job-desc').value = `(x${inputs.qty}) Vehicle Graphics Package.\nAreas:\n${panelTxt}\n\n${instTxt}`;
    } catch(e) { console.error(e); }
}
window.addEventListener('load', async () => {
    if (typeof injectHeader === 'function') injectHeader("Vehicle Wraps");
    renderPanels(); 
    const statusText = document.getElementById("status-text");
    const statusDot = document.getElementById("status-dot");
    try {
        const req = await fetch(`${SCRIPT_URL}?req=view_module&tab=PROD_Vinyl_Wraps`);
        backendData = await req.json();
        
        if(statusText) {
            statusText.innerText = "ONLINE";
            statusText.className = "font-bold text-green-500";
            if(statusDot) {
                statusDot.className = "w-2 h-2 rounded-full bg-green-500";
                statusDot.classList.remove("animate-pulse");
            }
        }
        runCalc(); 
    } catch(e) { console.error(e); }
});
</script>
</body>
</html>

<body class="bg-gray-100 min-h-screen font-sans flex flex-col">

                    <p class="text-slate-600 text-sm leading-relaxed">Review the calculated total. This is your market-competitive price. Note that quantity discounts apply automatically as you increase volume.</p>

                    <p class="text-slate-600 text-sm leading-relaxed">Click 'Copy Description' to grab the technical specs. Paste this directly into QuickBooks or Freshdesk to maintain data integrity for the production team.</p>
                </div>
            </div>
        `
    };

    const openArticle = (id) => {
        document.getElementById('article-content').innerHTML = ARTICLES[id] || 'Content not found.';
        const overlay = document.getElementById('article-overlay');
        overlay.classList.add('active');
        overlay.scrollTop = 0; // Ensure article starts at the top
        document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
    };

    const closeArticle = () => {
        document.getElementById('article-overlay').classList.remove('active');
        document.body.style.overflow = 'auto';
    };

    const closeArticleOnClickAway = (event) => {
        if (event.target.id === 'article-overlay') {
            closeArticle();
        }
    };

    // --- AUTH & INITIALIZATION ---
    window.onload = function() {
        const u = sessionStorage.getItem('signos_user') || 'GUEST';
        const r = sessionStorage.getItem('signos_role') || 'SALES';
        
        document.getElementById('auth-user').innerText = u;
        document.getElementById('auth-role').innerText = r;

        if (window.location.href.includes('signos-app')) {
            const badge = document.getElementById('env-badge');
            badge.innerText = "DEV MODE";
            badge.className = "px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded text-[8px] font-black bg-orange-500 text-white uppercase tracking-tighter";
        }
    };
</script>

// 1. SAFETY VALVE
function val(obj, key) {
    if (!obj) return "";
    return obj[key] || obj[key.toUpperCase()] || obj[key.toLowerCase()] || "";
}

// 2. STYLE MAP
const ICON_STYLES = {
    blue: "bg-blue-50 text-blue-600",
    green: "bg-green-50 text-green-600",
    purple: "bg-purple-50 text-purple-600",
    red: "bg-red-50 text-red-600",
    orange: "bg-orange-50 text-orange-600",
    slate: "bg-slate-50 text-slate-600",
    teal: "bg-teal-50 text-teal-600",
    indigo: "bg-indigo-50 text-indigo-600",
    pink: "bg-pink-50 text-pink-600",
    yellow: "bg-yellow-50 text-yellow-600",
    gray: "bg-gray-100 text-gray-600"
};

// 3. RENDER LOGIC 
function renderMenu(data, role) {
    const container = document.getElementById('menu-container');
    container.innerHTML = "";

    // Get Categories
    const cats = [...new Set(data.map(i => val(i, 'Category')))].filter(c => c);

    // Define Custom Sort Order
    const sortOrder = ["Rigid Signs", "Roll Media", "Services", "System"];
    
    cats.sort((a, b) => {
        const idxA = sortOrder.indexOf(a);
        const idxB = sortOrder.indexOf(b);
        if (idxA === -1 && idxB === -1) return a.localeCompare(b);
        if (idxA === -1) return 1;
        if (idxB === -1) return -1;
        return idxA - idxB;
    });

    cats.forEach(cat => {
        const section = document.createElement('div');
        section.innerHTML = `<h2 class="text-[10px] font-black text-gray-400 uppercase tracking-widest mb-3 ml-1">${cat}</h2>`;
        
        const grid = document.createElement('div');
        grid.className = "grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-3";

        data.filter(i => val(i, 'Category') === cat).forEach(mod => {
            
            // --- NEW: TWIN-ENGINE PERMISSION CHECK ---
            const checkTrue = (v) => v === true || String(v).toUpperCase() === "TRUE";
            
            let isAllowed = false;
            if (role === 'SUPER') {
                isAllowed = true;
            } else if (role === 'ADMIN') {
                isAllowed = IS_DEV_ENV ? checkTrue(val(mod, 'Dev_ADMIN')) : checkTrue(val(mod, 'Live_ADMIN'));
            } else if (role === 'SALES') {
                isAllowed = IS_DEV_ENV ? checkTrue(val(mod, 'Dev_SALES')) : checkTrue(val(mod, 'Live_SALES'));
            } else if (role === 'PROD') {
                isAllowed = IS_DEV_ENV ? checkTrue(val(mod, 'Dev_PROD')) : checkTrue(val(mod, 'Live_PROD'));
            }

            if (!isAllowed && role !== 'SUPER') return;

            // Version Logic
            const liveVer = val(mod, 'Live_Ver');
            const devVer = val(mod, 'Dev_Ver');

            let verText = "";
            let verClass = "";

            if (IS_DEV_ENV) {
                if (!devVer || devVer === '') return;
                verText = `DEV ${devVer}`;
                verClass = "bg-orange-100 text-orange-800 border-orange-200";
            } else {
                if (!liveVer || liveVer === '') return;
                verText = `v${liveVer.replace('v','')}`; // Shorten for mobile
                verClass = "bg-green-100 text-green-800 border-green-200";
            }

            // Render Item
            const displayName = val(mod, 'Display_Name');
            const fileLink = val(mod, 'File_Link');
            const iconColor = val(mod, 'Icon');
            const iconPath = val(mod, 'Icon_Path');
            
            let targetMode = (role === 'PROD') ? 'production' : (role === 'ADMIN' || role === 'SUPER' ? 'dev' : 'sales');

            const link = document.createElement('a');
            link.href = `${fileLink}?mode=${targetMode}`;
            
            link.className = "relative bg-white p-4 rounded-xl shadow-sm border border-gray-200 active:scale-98 active:bg-gray-50 transition-all duration-100 flex items-center justify-between group";

            const colorClass = ICON_STYLES[(iconColor || 'blue').toLowerCase()] || ICON_STYLES['blue'];
            const draftBadge = (!isAllowed && role === 'SUPER') 
                ? `<div class="absolute -top-2 -right-2 text-[8px] font-bold bg-purple-600 text-white px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full shadow-sm z-10">HIDDEN</div>` 
                : '';

            const iconHtml = iconPath 
                ? `<svg class="w-6 h-6" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="${iconPath}"></path></svg>` 
                : `<span class="text-xl font-bold">●</span>`;

            link.innerHTML = `
                ${draftBadge}
                <div class="flex items-center gap-4 w-full">
                    <div class="w-12 h-12 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center shrink-0 ${colorClass} shadow-inner">
                        ${iconHtml}
                    </div>
                    <div class="flex-1 min-w-0"> 
                        <h3 class="font-bold text-gray-800 text-sm truncate">${displayName}</h3>
                        <div class="flex items-center gap-2 mt-1">
                            <span class="text-[9px] font-mono px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded font-bold ${verClass}">${verText}</span>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="text-gray-300">
                        <svg class="w-5 h-5" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2" d="M9 5l7 7-7 7"></path></svg>
                    </div>
                </div>
            `;
            grid.appendChild(link);
        });

        if (grid.children.length > 0) {
            section.appendChild(grid);
            container.appendChild(section);
        }
    });
}

// 4. MAIN INIT
window.onload = async function() {
    const user = sessionStorage.getItem('signos_user');
    const role = sessionStorage.getItem('signos_role');
    
    if (!user) {
        window.location.href = 'index.html';
        return;
    }

    document.getElementById('auth-user').innerText = user;
    document.getElementById('auth-role').innerText = role;

    // Environment Badge Logic
    const envEl = document.getElementById('env-badge');
    if (IS_DEV_ENV) {
        envEl.innerHTML = `<span class="text-orange-600 font-bold">⚠️ DEV MODE</span> <span class="text-gray-300 mx-1">|</span> <span class="text-gray-400">${clientIP}</span>`;
    } else {
        envEl.innerHTML = `<span class="text-green-600 font-bold">● LIVE</span> <span class="text-gray-300 mx-1">|</span> <span class="text-gray-400">${clientIP}</span>`;
    }

    // IP Address Fix
    const ipWatcher = setInterval(() => {
        if (clientIP !== 'Unknown') {
            if (IS_DEV_ENV) {
                envEl.innerHTML = `<span class="text-orange-600 font-bold">⚠️ DEV MODE</span> <span class="text-gray-300 mx-1">|</span> <span class="text-gray-400">${clientIP}</span>`;
            } else {
                envEl.innerHTML = `<span class="text-green-600 font-bold">● LIVE</span> <span class="text-gray-300 mx-1">|</span> <span class="text-gray-400">${clientIP}</span>`;
            }
            clearInterval(ipWatcher);
        }
    }, 100);
    setTimeout(() => clearInterval(ipWatcher), 5000);

    // Admin Visibility
    if (role === 'ADMIN' || role === 'SUPER') {
        document.getElementById('admin-workflow').classList.remove('hidden');
        if (role === 'SUPER') document.getElementById('super-badge').classList.remove('hidden');
        
        // Backup Permission Check
        const perms = JSON.parse(sessionStorage.getItem('signos_perms') || '{}');
        const btnBackup = document.getElementById('btn-backup');
        if (role !== 'SUPER' && perms.backup !== 'Run' && perms.backup !== 'Full') {
            if(btnBackup) btnBackup.classList.add('hidden');
        }
    }

    // --- FETCH MENU DATA ---
    try {
        const response = await fetch(`${SCRIPT_URL}?tab=SYS_Modules&ip=${clientIP}&user=${user}&role=${role}&req=table`);
        const data = await response.json();

        // Safety Check
        if (data.error) throw new Error(data.error);
        if (!Array.isArray(data)) throw new Error("Invalid Data Format");

        // Hide Loader & Render
        document.getElementById('loader').classList.add('hidden');
        document.getElementById('menu-container').classList.remove('hidden');
        
        renderMenu(data, role);

    } catch (e) {
        document.getElementById('loader').innerText = "CONNECTION FAILED: " + e.message;
        document.getElementById('loader').classList.add('text-red-500', 'font-bold');
        console.error("Menu Load Error:", e);
    }
};
</script>
</body>
</html>

<script>
    // 1. On Load: Check Permissions
    window.onload = function() {
        const u = sessionStorage.getItem('signos_user');
        const r = sessionStorage.getItem('signos_role');
        const permsRaw = sessionStorage.getItem('signos_perms');
        const perms = permsRaw ? JSON.parse(permsRaw) : { backup: "None" };

        // STRICT SECURITY GATE
        if (perms.backup !== 'Run' && perms.backup !== 'Full') {
            alert("ACCESS DENIED: You do not have Backup permissions.");
            window.location.href = 'menu.html';
            return;
        }

        document.getElementById('auth-user').innerText = u || 'GUEST';
        document.getElementById('auth-role').innerText = r || 'VIEW';
    };

    // 2. The Missing Function
    async function runExport() {
        const pin = document.getElementById('admin-pin').value;
        const btn = document.getElementById('btn-run');
        const loader = document.getElementById('loading');
        const icon = document.getElementById('icon-run');
        const btnText = document.getElementById('btn-text');

        // Reset UI
        document.getElementById('result-area').classList.add('hidden');
        document.getElementById('error-area').classList.add('hidden');

        if(!pin) { alert("Please enter your PIN."); return; }

        // Lock UI
        btn.disabled = true;
        loader.classList.remove('hidden');
        icon.classList.add('hidden');
        btnText.innerText = "PROCESSING...";

        try {
            // Call API
            // ADDED BACKTICKS (` `) around the string
const url = `${SCRIPT_URL}?req=manual_archive&pin=${pin}&ip=${clientIP}`;
            const response = await fetch(url);
            const data = await response.json();

            if (data.status === "success") {
                // Success UI
                document.getElementById('result-area').classList.remove('hidden');
                document.getElementById('row-count').innerText = data.rows_archived || 0;
                document.getElementById('file-link').href = data.url;
            } else {
                throw new Error(data.message || "API Error");
            }
        } catch (e) {
            // Error UI
            document.getElementById('error-area').classList.remove('hidden');
            document.getElementById('error-text').innerText = e.message;
        } finally {
            // Unlock UI
            btn.disabled = false;
            loader.classList.add('hidden');
            icon.classList.remove('hidden');
            btnText.innerText = "GENERATE BACKUP";
        }
    }
</script>


</body>
</html>

<style type="text/tailwindcss">

            </button>
        </div>
    </div>
